\chapter{4.2}
\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g}{}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g}\index{4.2@{4.2}}

\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md791}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{C}{C}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md791}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added physics support
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_physics_constraint_timeline}{sp\+Physics\+Constraint\+Timeline}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_physics_constraint_reset_timeline}{sp\+Physics\+Constraint\+Reset\+Timeline}}
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_physics_8h_ace8c5a0af9ceb543621f31fc6107e6a9}{sp\+Physics}} to be passed to {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_skeleton_8h_aad82746c478357901e74515b407a0415}{sp\+Skeleton\+\_\+update\+World\+Transform()}}
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_skeleton_data_8h_a3f8bda7277d329f2d9920180a5a05757}{sp\+Skeleton\+Data\+\_\+find\+Physics\+Constraint()}} to query a physics constraint by name
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_skeleton_8h_afa5ee8ca851caa8a191930fa97b9ae28}{sp\+Skeleton\+\_\+find\+Physics\+Constraint()}} to query a physics constraint by name
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_skeleton_8h_a96f300ac718b445f3e268c4bff7c0c3a}{sp\+Skeleton\+\_\+physics\+Translate()}} to translate all physics constraints by some distances in the skeleton coordinate system
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_skeleton_8h_a3d46c50a2aa001b8b3b4dc19f8c7ed16}{sp\+Skeleton\+\_\+physics\+Rotate()}} to rotate all physics constraints by some distances in the skeleton coordinate system
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_skeleton_aa71ba1e49feeaf1e258e37c58f4e17de}{sp\+Skeleton\+::time}} to keep track of time for physics simulations
\item See also breaking changes for {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_skeleton_8h_aad82746c478357901e74515b407a0415}{sp\+Skeleton\+\_\+update\+World\+Transform()}} and the requirement to call {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_skeleton_8h_ab2bf19cc92d104c0e5403eb4fc4c733c}{sp\+Skeleton\+\_\+update()}} to advance pyhsics each frame.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_inherit_timeline}{sp\+Inherit\+Timeline}}
\item Added \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-api-reference\#TrackEntry-alphaAttachmentThreshold}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily sp\+Track\+Entry\+::alpha\+Attachment\+Threshold}}}
\item Removed {\ttfamily const} qualifiers where appropriate
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_animation_state_8h_a1417d50db79b970eb46d14aad34768a4}{sp\+Track\+Entry\+\_\+set\+Mix\+Duration()}} to set the mix duration in conjunction with a delay
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_animation_state_8h_ad9289e9400b210a50b7db2e67f393383}{sp\+Track\+Entry\+\_\+was\+Applied()}} to check if the entry has been applied
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_bone_8h_a33507ba6729eebf23cb835b048c5b478}{sp\+Bone\+\_\+world\+To\+Parent()}} to transform coordinates from world space to the parent space of a bone
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_bone_8h_a461a6907ad9c35a1c75bc88e19a40151}{sp\+Bone\+\_\+local\+To\+Parent()}} to transform coordinates from a bone\textquotesingle{}s local space to its parent space
\item Added non essential fields {\ttfamily icon} and {\ttfamily visible} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_bone_data}{sp\+Bone\+Data}}
\item Added non essential fields {\ttfamily path} and {\ttfamily visible} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_slot_data}{sp\+Slot\+Data}}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily sp\+Track\+Entry\+::attachment\+Threshold} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_track_entry_a706e22c5d5fadd481a0f438b700b4d83}{sp\+Track\+Entry\+::mix\+Attachment\+Threshold}}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily sp\+Track\+Entry\+::draw\+Order\+Threshold} to {\ttfamily sp\+Track\+Entry\+::mix\+Draw\+Ordert\+Threshold}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily sp\+Transform\+Mode} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_bone_data_8h_a3f29b53874aa6588441ce4ec740050e7}{sp\+Inherit}} and all {\ttfamily SP\+\_\+\+TRANSFORMMODE\+\_\+\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} enums to {\ttfamily SP\+\_\+\+INHERIT\+\_\+\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}
\item Changed {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_mesh_attachment_a73e85e96b32ca8302c836cc703865ed4}{sp\+Mesh\+Attachment\+::edges}} from {\ttfamily int \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} to {\ttfamily unsigned short \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}
\item You must call {\ttfamily sp\+Skeleton\+\_\+update(delta)} before calling {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_skeleton_8h_aad82746c478357901e74515b407a0415}{sp\+Skeleton\+\_\+update\+World\+Transform()}} if the frame time has advanced. This is needed to update physics accordingly
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_skeleton_8h_aad82746c478357901e74515b407a0415}{sp\+Skeleton\+\_\+update\+World\+Transform()}} takes an additional {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_physics_8h_ace8c5a0af9ceb543621f31fc6107e6a9}{sp\+Physics}} parameter. See the {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_physics_8h_ace8c5a0af9ceb543621f31fc6107e6a9}{sp\+Physics}} documentation for information on what the different enum values do
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md792}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{SFML}{SFML}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md792}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added physics examples

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md793}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{SDL}{SDL}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md793}

\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-sdl-c_8c_a2f02ef7b6004547b87d9d350472949d9}{sp\+Skeleton\+Drawable\+\_\+update()}} now takes an additional {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_physics_8h_ace8c5a0af9ceb543621f31fc6107e6a9}{sp\+Physics} physics} parameter that specifies how physics should be updated
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md794}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{C++}{C++}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md794}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added physics support
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Physics\+Constraint\+XXXTimeline} and {\ttfamily Physics\+Constraint\+Reset\+Timeline}
\item Added {\ttfamily Physics} to be passed to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::update\+World\+Transform()}
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\+::find\+Physics\+Constraint()} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\+::get\+Physics\+Constraints()} to query physics constraints
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::find\+Physics\+Constraint()} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::get\+Physics\+Constraints()} to query physics constraints
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::physics\+Translate()} to translate all physics constraints by some distances in the skeleton coordinate system
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::physics\+Rotate()} to rotate all physics constraints by some distances in the skeleton coordinate system
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::time} to keep track of time for physics simulations
\item See also breaking changes for {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::update\+World\+Transform()} and the requirement to call {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::update()} to advance pyhsics each frame.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Inherit\+Timeline}
\item Added \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-api-reference\#TrackEntry-alphaAttachmentThreshold}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\+::\+\_\+alpha\+Attachment\+Threshold}}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\+::set\+Mix\+Duration()} to set the mix duration in conjunction with a delay
\item Added {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\+::was\+Applied()} to check if the entry has been applied
\item Added {\ttfamily Bone\+::world\+To\+Parent()} to transform coordinates from world space to the parent space of a bone
\item Added {\ttfamily Bone\+::local\+To\+Parent()} to transform coordinates from a bone\textquotesingle{}s local space to its parent space
\item Added non essential fields {\ttfamily icon} and {\ttfamily visible} to {\ttfamily Bone\+Data}
\item Added non essential fields {\ttfamily path} and {\ttfamily visible} to {\ttfamily Slot\+Data}
\item Added {\ttfamily set\+To\+Setup\+Pose()} to all contraint classes
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\+::attachment\+Threshold} to {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\+::mix\+Attachment\+Threshold}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\+::draw\+Order\+Threshold} to {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\+::mix\+Draw\+Ordert\+Threshold}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Transform\+Mode} to {\ttfamily Inherit} and all {\ttfamily Transform\+Mode\+\_\+\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} enums to {\ttfamily Inherit\+\_\+\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}
\item You must call {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::update(delta)} before calling {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::update\+World\+Transform()} if the frame time has advanced. This is needed to update physics accordingly
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::update\+World\+Transform()} takes an additional {\ttfamily Physics} parameter. See the {\ttfamily Physics} documentation for information on what the different enum values do
\item All {\ttfamily Updatable} sub-\/classes like {\ttfamily Bone} and constraints now take an additional {\ttfamily Physics} parameter for their {\ttfamily update()} methods
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md795}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cocos2d-\/x}{Cocos2d-\/x}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md795}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md798}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{UE4}{UE4}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md798}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking}}\+: Renamed runtime folder from {\ttfamily spine-\/ue4} to {\ttfamily spine-\/ue}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking}}\+: Renamed plugin {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_spine_plugin}{Spine\+Plugin}}. You must update your project\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Build.\+cs} file accordingly
\item {\bfseries{Breaking}}\+: Starting with Unreal Engine 5.\+3 imported {\ttfamily .skel}/{\ttfamily .json} and {\ttfamily .atlas} files in the same folder must NOT have a common prefix. E.\+g. {\ttfamily skeleton.\+json} and {\ttfamily skeleton.\+atlas} will not work. Make sure to rename at least one of the two files so there is no prefix collision, e.\+g. {\ttfamily skeleton-\/data.\+json} and {\ttfamily skeleton.\+atlas}.
\item Added compatibility with UE 5.\+3
\item Added more example maps
\item Added blueprint-\/callable methods {\ttfamily Physics\+Translate()}, {\ttfamily Physics\+Rotate()} and {\ttfamily Reset\+Physics\+Constraints()} (which will reset all physics constraints in the skeleton) to {\ttfamily Spine\+Skeleton\+Component} and {\ttfamily Spine\+Widget}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md799}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Godot}{Godot}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md799}

\item {\bfseries{Breaking}}\+: Renamed {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+set\+\_\+draw\+\_\+order\+\_\+threshold} and {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+get\+\_\+draw\+\_\+order\+\_\+threshold} to {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+set\+\_\+mix\+\_\+draw\+\_\+order\+\_\+threshold} and {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+get\+\_\+mix\+\_\+draw\+\_\+order\+\_\+threshold}
\item {\bfseries{BReaking}}\+: {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_spine_skeleton_ab4745bff432fddd6c68bf363cf98c3fb}{Spine\+Skeleton.\+update\+\_\+world\+\_\+transform}} takes an additional {\ttfamily physics} parameter that specifies how physics should be updated

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-api-reference\#TrackEntry-alphaAttachmentThreshold}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+Alpha\+Attachment\+Threshold}}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Track\+Entry} {\ttfamily Attachment\+Threshold} to {\ttfamily Mix\+Attachment\+Threshold}, renamed {\ttfamily Draw\+Order\+Threshold} to {\ttfamily Mix\+Draw\+Order\+Threshold}.
\item Changed signature of {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+Update\+World\+Transform()} to {\ttfamily Update\+World\+Transform(Skeleton.\+Physics physics)}. The default replacement for {\ttfamily skeleton.\+Update\+World\+Transform()} calls is {\ttfamily skeleton.\+Update\+World\+Transform(Skeleton.\+Physics.\+Update)}. If you are certain that a subsequent call to {\ttfamily skeleton.\+Update\+World\+Transform(Skeleton.\+Physics.\+Update)} follows in the same frame, you can pass {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+Physics.\+Pose} as argument instead of {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+Physics.\+Update}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md801}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Unity}{Unity}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md801}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Officially supported Unity versions are 2017.\+1-\/6000.\+0}}.
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily On\+Post\+Process\+Vertices} callback parameter {\ttfamily Mesh\+Generator\+Buffers} now provides access to {\ttfamily uv2\+Buffer} and {\ttfamily uv3\+Buffer} properties of {\ttfamily Mesh\+Generator}, automatically allocating buffers upon access if {\ttfamily tint\+Black} is disabled. This allows for passing own vertex data to a shader on second and third uv channels.
\item Added {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic Grayscale} shader to provide a basic grayscale shader for Skeleton\+Graphic as well. Skeleton\+Graphic Material {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic\+Default\+Grayscale} uses this shader and can be assigned at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} components as usual.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} now supports automatic scaling based on its {\ttfamily Rect\+Transform} bounds. Automatic scaling can be enabled by setting the added {\ttfamily Layout Scale \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode}} Inspector property to either {\ttfamily Width Controls Height}, {\ttfamily Height Controls Width}, {\ttfamily Fit\+In\+Parent} or {\ttfamily Envelope\+Parent}. It is set to {\ttfamily None} by default to keep previous behaviour and avoid breaking existing projects. To modify the reference layout bounds, hit the additional {\ttfamily Edit Layout Bounds} toggle button to switch into edit mode, adjust the bounds or hit {\ttfamily Match Rect\+Transform with Mesh}, and hit the button again when done adjusting. The skeleton will now be scaled accordingly to fit the reference layout bounds to the object\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Rect\+Transform}.
\item Added previously missing unlit URP 2D shader variant, available under {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/2\+D/\+Spine/\+Skeleton}.
\item Added support for light cookies at {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Sprite} shader.
\item Timeline extension package\+: An additional \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} preferences parameter {\ttfamily Timeline} -\/ {\ttfamily Default Mix Duration} has been added, setting newly added {\ttfamily Spine\+Animation\+State\+Clip} clips accordingly, defaults to false. This \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} preferences parameter can be enabled to default to the previous behaviour before this update.
\item Tint Black\+: Added support for \href{http://en.esotericsoftware.com/spine-slots\#Tint-black}{\texttt{ Tint Black}} functionality at all \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} URP shaders (2D and 3D shaders) and at all standard pipeline {\ttfamily Spine/\+Sprite} shaders. This feature can be enabled via the {\ttfamily Tint Black} material parameter in the Inspector. Note\+: The URP Sprite shaders provided in the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} URP Shaders extension UPM package require the latest version of the spine-\/unity runtime (package version 4.\+1.\+12, 2023-\/05-\/31 or newer) to display the added material parameters in the Inspector GUI.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic.\+Mesh\+Scale} property to allow access to calculated mesh scale. {\ttfamily Mesh\+Scale} is based on (1) Canvas pixels per unit, and (2) {\ttfamily Rect\+Transform} bounds when using {\ttfamily Layout Scale \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode}} other than {\ttfamily None} at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} which scales the skeleton mesh to fit the parent {\ttfamily Rect\+Transform} bounds accordingly.
\item Added {\ttfamily update\+Separator\+Part\+Scale} property to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} to let render separator parts follow the scale (lossy scale) of the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} Game\+Object. Defaults to {\ttfamily false} to maintain existing behaviour.
\item Added experimental {\ttfamily Editor\+Skeleton\+Player} component to allow Editor playback of the initial animation set at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} or {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} components. Add this component to your skeleton Game\+Object to enable the in-\/editor animation preview. Allows configurations for continuous playback when selected, deselected, and alternative single-\/frame preview by setting {\ttfamily Fixed Track Time} to any value other than 0. Limitations\+: At skeletons with variable material count the Inspector preview may be too unresponsive. It is then recommended to disable the {\ttfamily Editor\+Skeleton\+Player} component (at the top of the Inspector) to make it responsive again, then you can disable {\ttfamily Play When Selected} and re-\/enable the component to preview playback only when deselected.
\item Added example component {\ttfamily Render\+Combined\+Mesh} to render a combined mesh of multiple meshes or submeshes. This is required by {\ttfamily Outline\+Only} shaders to render a combined outline when using {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Separator} or multiple atlas pages which would normally lead to outlines around individual parts. To add a combined outline to your Skeleten\+Renderer\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Add a child Game\+Object and move it a bit back (e.\+g. position Z = 0.\+01).
\item Add a {\ttfamily Render\+Combined\+Mesh} component, provided in the {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Scripts/\+Sample Components} directory.
\item Copy the original material, add \+\_\+\+\_\+\+Outline\+\_\+ to its name and set the shader to your outline-\/only shader like {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Outline/\+Skeleton-\/\+Outline\+Only} or {\ttfamily Spine/\+Outline/\+Outline\+Only-\/\+ZWrite}.
\item Assign this \+\_\+\+\_\+\+Outline\+\_\+ material at the new child Game\+Object\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Mesh\+Renderer} component. If you are using {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Separator} and need to enable and disable the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Separator} component at runtime, you can increase the {\ttfamily Render\+Combined\+Mesh} {\ttfamily Reference Renderers} array by one and assign the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} itself at the last entry after the parts renderers. Disabled {\ttfamily Mesh\+Renderer} components will be skipped when combining the final mesh, so the combined mesh is automatically filled from the desired active renderers.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Timeline extension package\+: Added static {\ttfamily Editor\+Event} callback to allow editor scripts to react to animation events outside of play-\/mode. Register to the events via {\ttfamily Spine.\+Unity.\+Playables.\+Spine\+Animation\+State\+Mixer\+Behaviour.\+Editor\+Event += Your\+Callback;}.
\item URP Shaders\+: Added {\ttfamily Depth Write} property to shaders {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton} and {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton Lit}. Defaults to false to maintain existing behaviour.
\item Added {\ttfamily Animation Update} mode (called {\ttfamily Update\+Timing} in code) {\ttfamily In Late Update} for {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic}. This allows you to update the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} skeleton in the same frame that the Mecanim Animator updated its state, which happens between {\ttfamily Update} and {\ttfamily Late\+Update}.
\item URP Shaders\+: Added URP "{}\+Blend Mode"{} shader variants for both URP 3D and URP 2D renderers. They are listed under shader name "{}\+Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Blend Modes/"{} and "{}\+Universal Render Pipeline/2\+D/\+Spine/\+Blend Modes/"{} respectively.
\item URP Shaders\+: Added support for \href{http://en.esotericsoftware.com/spine-slots\#Tint-black}{\texttt{ Tint Black}} functionality at "{}\+Blend Modes"{} \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} URP shaders (2D and 3D shaders).
\item Physics\+Constraints\+: Skeleton Game\+Objects now automatically apply Transform translation and rotation to the skeleton\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Physics\+Constraints}. You can disable applying translation or rotation at the Skeleton component Inspector under {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ Physics Inheritance} by setting {\ttfamily Position} to (0,0)and {\ttfamily Rotation} to 0, or by setting the properties {\ttfamily physics\+Position\+Inheritance\+Factor} to {\ttfamily Vector2.\+zero} and {\ttfamily physics\+Rotation\+Inheritance\+Factor} to {\ttfamily 0} at the skeleton component via code.
\item Added {\ttfamily Physics Constraints} example scene (located in {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Other Examples}) together with {\ttfamily celestial-\/circus} example skeleton assets. This scene demonstrates Transform movement automatically affecting physics constraints of a skeleton.
\item Physics\+Constraints\+: Skeleton components now allow you to use relative instead of world-\/space Transform movement by assigning a Transform (typically the parent) to the new {\ttfamily Movement relative to} property. Leave this property at {\ttfamily null} (the default) to use world-\/space Transform movement for physics.
\item Physics\+Constraints\+: Added \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Preferences settings {\ttfamily Editor Instantiation} -\/ {\ttfamily Physics Inheritance} -\/ {\ttfamily Default Position} and {\ttfamily Default Rotation} to initialize skeletons physics settings with the desired Transform position and rotation inheritance factors when added to a scene via drag-\/and-\/drop.
\item Skeleton\+Graphic\+: Added Tint Black blend mode shaders {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic Tint Black Additive}, {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic Tint Black Multiply} and {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic Tint Black Screen}.
\item Skeleton\+Graphic\+: Added pre-\/defined Skeleton\+Graphic material sets for main workflow parameters in folders {\ttfamily spine-\/unity/\+Materials} instead of requiring manual copies\+: {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic-\/\+PMATexture} containing materials for premultiplied-\/alpha texture workflow ({\ttfamily Straight Alpha Texture} disabled) and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic-\/\+Staight\+Alpha\+Texture} containing materials for straight alpha texture workflow ({\ttfamily Straight Alpha Texture} enabled). These directories contain a set of materials with {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group Compatible} disabled for usage with {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ PMA \doxylink{struct_vertex}{Vertex} \doxylink{external_2magic__enum_2example_2example_8cpp_a692f5062ca261bdb3a62a63faddfd27f}{Color}} enabled at the component. Each directory also provides a subdirectory {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group\+Compatible} with materials with {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group Compatible} enabled for usage with {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group} alpha (requiring {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ PMA \doxylink{struct_vertex}{Vertex} \doxylink{external_2magic__enum_2example_2example_8cpp_a692f5062ca261bdb3a62a63faddfd27f}{Color}} disabled at the component).
\item Skeleton\+Graphic\+: Added auto-\/detect functionality for parameters {\ttfamily Advanced} -\/ {\ttfamily Tint Black}, {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group Compatible} and {\ttfamily PMA \doxylink{struct_vertex}{Vertex} \doxylink{external_2magic__enum_2example_2example_8cpp_a692f5062ca261bdb3a62a63faddfd27f}{Color}}. If unsure which settings are correct, hit the {\ttfamily Detect} button next to each parameter, in top to bottom order, or the {\ttfamily Detect Settings} to detect all three. Also added automatic material assignment via a {\ttfamily Detect Material} button in the {\ttfamily Advanced} section and a {\ttfamily Detect} button next to the {\ttfamily Material} property at the top of the component Inspector, as well as next to the {\ttfamily Blend \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode} Materials} section when using multiple canvas renderers with blend modes. The suitable material is selected based on these three settings, combined with texture settings (PMA or straight alpha texture settings). If you receive incorrect results, likely your texture settings are incorrectly setup for your PMA or Straight alpha texture export settings.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Texture} example components now provide a {\ttfamily shader\+Passes} parameter to customize which passes are rendered to the {\ttfamily Render\+Texture}. It defaults to {\ttfamily -\/1} for all passes to keep the existing behaviour. You might want to set it to {\ttfamily 0} to only render the first pass e.\+g. to avoid issues when using a URP shader at the original skeleton.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic\+Render\+Texture} example component now also received a {\ttfamily quad\+Material} property, defaulting to the newly added Material asset {\ttfamily Render\+Quad\+Graphic\+Material} which applies proper premultiplied-\/alpha blending of the render texture. The {\ttfamily quad\+Material} member variable was moved from {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Texture} to the common base class {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Texture\+Base}.
\item All \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Outline shaders, including the URP outline shader, now provide an additional parameter {\ttfamily Width in Screen Space}. Enable it to keep the outline width constant in screen space instead of texture space. Requires more expensive computations, so enable only where necessary. Defaults to {\ttfamily disabled} to maintain existing behaviour.
\item Added support for Blend\+Mode\+Materials at runtime instantiation from files via an additional method {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\+Asset.\+Setup\+Runtime\+Blend\+Mode\+Materials}. See example scene {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Other Examples/\+Instantiate from Script} for a usage example.
\item Skeleton\+Graphic\+: You can now offset the skeleton mesh relative to the pivot via a newly added green circle handle. This allows you to e.\+g. frame only the face of a skeleton inside a masked frame. Previously offsetting the pivot downwards fails when {\ttfamily Layout Scale \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode}} scales the mesh smaller and towards the pivot (e.\+g. the feet) and thus out of the frame. Now you can keep the pivot in the center of the {\ttfamily Rect\+Transform} while offsetting only the mesh downwards, keeping the desired skeleton area (e.\+g. the face) centered while resizing. Moving the new larger green circle handle moves the mesh offset, while moving the blue pivot circle handle moves the pivot as usual.
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton} shader now performs proper alpha-\/testing when {\ttfamily Depth Write} is enabled, using the existing {\ttfamily Shadow alpha cutoff} parameter.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Root\+Motion} components now provide a public {\ttfamily \doxylink{test__rml__tbb_8cpp_a98b1050f09da390896f964fb7a892391}{Initialize()}} method which is automatically called when calling {\ttfamily skeleton\+Animation.\+Initialize(true)} to update the necessary skeleton references. If a different root bone shall be used, be sure to set {\ttfamily skeleton\+Root\+Motion.\+root\+Motion\+Bone\+Name} before calling {\ttfamily skeleton\+Animation.\+Initialize(true)}.
\item Skeleton Mecanim\+: Added new {\ttfamily Mix \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode}} {\ttfamily Match}. When selected, \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} animation weights are calculated to best match the provided Mecanim clip weights. This mix mode is recommended on any layer using blend tree nodes.
\item URP Shaders\+: Added {\ttfamily ZWrite} variant of outline shader {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Outline/\+Skeleton-\/\+Outline\+Only ZWrite}. Suitable for e.\+g. depth of field (DoF) effect where writing to the depth buffer is required. Note that for DoF effect, {\ttfamily Render Queue} needs to be set to {\ttfamily Alpha \doxylink{class_test}{Test}}.
\item Skeleton\+Graphic\+: Exposed {\ttfamily Set\+Scaled\+Pivot\+Offset} as public method outside of the editor to support programatically moving mesh offsets at runtime based on mesh bounds.
\item Skeleton\+Mecanim\+: Added {\ttfamily Scene Preview} option to preview an Animation Clip for e.\+g. easier event placement. When enabled, the Animation Clip selected in the Animation window is previewed in the Scene and Game views. Lock the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} Inspector window, open the Animation window and select the Animation Clip. Then in the Animation window scrub through the timeline to see the current animation frame previewed.
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton Lit} shader now supports \href{https://docs.unity3d.com/6000.0/Documentation/Manual/urp/probevolumes-concept.html}{\texttt{ Adaptive Probe Volumes (APV)}} introduced in Unity 6. The shader also provides a new material property {\ttfamily APV per Pixel} to either calculate APV lighting contribution per pixel (the default) or per vertex.
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Sprite} shader now also supports \href{https://docs.unity3d.com/6000.0/Documentation/Manual/urp/probevolumes-concept.html}{\texttt{ Adaptive Probe Volumes (APV)}} introduced in Unity 6. APV lighting contribution is automatically calculated per pixel.
\item All \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Outline shaders, including the URP outline shaders, now provide an additional parameter {\ttfamily Fill}. Enable it to also fill the opaque area inside the outline with the outline color. Prevents a semi-\/transparent gap between outline and skeleton. Defaults to {\ttfamily disabled} to maintain existing behaviour.
\item Added example component {\ttfamily Render\+Existing\+Mesh\+Graphic} (similar to {\ttfamily Render\+Existing\+Mesh}) to render a {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} mesh again with different materials. This might be required by e.\+g. URP and Skeleton\+Graphic outline shaders skipping additional render passes. To add a second outline variant of your Skeleton\+Graphic\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Add a Game\+Object at the same hierarchy level as the reference Skeleton\+Graphic and move it before the reference Skeleton\+Graphic to render behind.
\item Add a {\ttfamily Render\+Existing\+Mesh\+Graphic} component.
\item In the {\ttfamily Render\+Existing\+Mesh\+Graphic} component Inspector at {\ttfamily Reference Skeleton Graphic} assign the original {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} object.
\item At {\ttfamily Replacement Material} assign e.\+g. the included {\itshape Skeleton\+Graphic\+Default\+Outline} material to replace all materials with this material. Alternatively, if {\ttfamily Multiple Canvas\+Renderers} is enabled at the reference Skeleton\+Graphic, you can add entries to the {\ttfamily Replacement Materials} list and at each entry assign the original Skeleton\+Graphic material (e.\+g. {\itshape Skeleton\+Graphic\+Default}) to be replaced and the respective {\ttfamily Replacement Material} (e.\+g. {\itshape Skeleton\+Graphic\+Default\+Outline}).
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Changed {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_spine_shader_with_outline_g_u_i}{Spine\+Shader\+With\+Outline\+GUI}} outline related methods from {\ttfamily private} to {\ttfamily protected virtual} to allow for custom shader GUI subclasses to switch to different outline shaders.
\item Changed {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower} and {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower\+Graphic} methods {\ttfamily Late\+Update} and {\ttfamily Initialize} to {\ttfamily virtual} to allow easier overriding for e.\+g. positional offset in custom subclasses.
\item {\ttfamily Mesh\+Generator} received a new optimization option to avoid rendering fully transparent attachments at slot alpha 0 by default. Comment out {\ttfamily \#define SLOT\+\_\+\+ALPHA\+\_\+\+DISABLES\+\_\+\+ATTACHMENT} in {\ttfamily \doxylink{_mesh_generator_8cs}{Mesh\+Generator.\+cs}} to revert to previous behaviour. You may only need this option disabled when utilizing a custom shader which uses vertex color alpha for purposes other than transparency.
\item Physics\+Constraints\+: bool properties {\ttfamily Apply\+Translation\+To\+Physics} and {\ttfamily Apply\+Rotation\+To\+Physics} were changed to {\ttfamily Vector2 Physics\+Position\+Inheritance\+Factor} and {\ttfamily float Physics\+Rotation\+Inheritance\+Factor} to allow the Transform movement the be scaled by a factor before being applied to the skeleton. You can set the properties to {\ttfamily Vector2.\+zero} and {\ttfamily 0} respectively to disable applying any Transform movement at all. The {\ttfamily Advanced} Inspector section {\ttfamily Physics Constraints} was renamed to {\ttfamily Physics Inheritance}, the properties in the section are now called {\ttfamily Position} and {\ttfamily Rotation}.
\item Skeleton\+Graphic Materials\+: Since the addition of new material sets for the {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group\+Compatible} parameters, the default Skeleton\+Graphic materials all have {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group Compatible} disabled. Please assign the respective material from the {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group\+Compatible} material subdirectory if you want {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group Compatible} enabled at your Skeleton\+Graphic.
\item Skeleton\+Graphic\+: The parameter {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic.\+Mesh\+Generator.\+settings.\+canvas\+Group\+Tint\+Black} was changed to {\ttfamily canvas\+Group\+Compatible} to help with auto-\/detecting correct \doxylink{struct_vertex}{Vertex} \doxylink{class_data}{Data} and Material settings. Set the parameter to true if the Skeleton\+Graphic component is located below a {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group} component. The parameter value is automatically migrated from {\ttfamily canvas\+Group\+Tint\+Black}.
\item Inspector\+: String attribute {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_spine_skin}{Spine\+Skin()}} now allows to include {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}None\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} in the list of parameters. Previously the {\ttfamily include\+None=true} parameter of the {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_spine_skin}{Spine\+Skin()}} attribute defaulted to {\ttfamily true} but was ignored. Now it defaults to {\ttfamily false} and has an effect on the list. Only the Inspector GUI is affected by this behaviour change.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic\+Render\+Texture} example component\+: {\ttfamily protected Raw\+Image quad\+Raw\+Image} was changed to {\ttfamily protected Skeleton\+Submesh\+Graphic quad\+Maskable\+Graphic} for a bugfix. This is only relevant for subclasses of {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic\+Render\+Texture} or when querying the {\ttfamily Raw\+Image} component via e.\+g. {\ttfamily skeleton\+Graphic\+Render\+Texture.\+quad.\+Get\+Component\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Raw\+Image\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}()}.
\item Fixed a bug where when Linear color space is used and {\ttfamily PMA vertex colors} enabled, additive slots add a too dark (too transparent) color value. If you want the old incorrect behaviour (darker additive slots) or are not using Linear but Gamma color space, you can comment-\/out the define {\ttfamily LINEAR\+\_\+\+COLOR\+\_\+\+SPACE\+\_\+\+FIX\+\_\+\+ADDITIVE\+\_\+\+ALPHA} in {\ttfamily \doxylink{_mesh_generator_8cs}{Mesh\+Generator.\+cs}} to deactivate the fix or just to skip unnecessary instructions.
\item Fixed Skeleton\+Root\+Motion components ignoring parent bone scale when set by transform constraints. Using applied scale of parent bone now. If you need the old behaviour, comment out the line {\ttfamily \#define USE\+\_\+\+APPLIED\+\_\+\+PARENT\+\_\+\+SCALE} in \doxylink{_skeleton_root_motion_base_8cs}{Skeleton\+Root\+Motion\+Base.\+cs}.
\item Fixed Skeleton\+Utility callback update order when used with Skeleton\+Root\+Motion components so that the position when following a bone is updated after Skeleton\+Root\+Motion clears root-\/bone position. The order of Skeleton\+Utility\+Bone callbacks is changed to be later to achieve this. This is a breaking change in the unlikely case that you are using Skeleton\+Root\+Motion together with Skeleton\+Utility and subscribed to {\ttfamily Update\+Local}, {\ttfamily Update\+World} or {\ttfamily Update\+Complete} yourself and relied on a certain callback order. One solution is to then resubscribe your own callback events accordingly by calling {\ttfamily .Update\+Local -\/= Callback; .Update\+Local += Callback;}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Changes of default values}}
\item {\bfseries{Deprecated}}
\item {\bfseries{Restructuring (Non-\/\+Breaking)}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md802}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{XNA/\+Mono\+Game}{XNA/\+Mono\+Game}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md802}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Apply external movement to physics\+: If you are not directly modifying {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+X} or {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+Y}, you can apply external game object movement to skeleton physics as follows\+: Add a {\ttfamily Vector2 last\+Position;} member variable to your class interacting with the skeleton. Then call e.\+g. the following code each frame\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{Vector2\ currentPosition\ =\ <current\ world\ position>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{Vector2\ externalPositionDelta\ =\ currentPosition\ -\/\ lastPosition;}
\DoxyCodeLine{skeleton.PhysicsTranslate(externalPositionDelta.x,\ externalPositionDelta.y);}
\DoxyCodeLine{lastPosition\ =\ currentPosition;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md803}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{Java}{Java}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md803}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added physics support
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Physics\+Constraint\+XXXTimeline} and {\ttfamily Physics\+Constraint\+Reset\+Timeline}
\item Added {\ttfamily Physics} to be passed to {\ttfamily Skeleton\#update\+World\+Transform()}
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\#find\+Physics\+Constraint()} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\#get\+Physics\+Constraints()} to query physics constraints
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\#find\+Physics\+Constraint()} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\#get\+Physics\+Constraints()} to query physics constraints
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\#physics\+Translate()} to translate all physics constraints by some distances in the skeleton coordinate system
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\#physics\+Rotate()} to rotate all physics constraints by some distances in the skeleton coordinate system
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\#time} and respective setters/getters to keep track of time for physics simulations
\item See also breaking changes for {\ttfamily Skeleton\#update\+World\+Transform()} and the requirement to call {\ttfamily Skeleton\#update()} to advance pyhsics each frame.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Inherit\+Timeline}
\item Added \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-api-reference\#TrackEntry-alphaAttachmentThreshold}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#alpha\+Attachment\+Threshold}}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#set\+Mix\+Duration()} to set the mix duration in conjunction with a delay
\item Added {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#was\+Applied()} to check if the entry has been applied
\item Added {\ttfamily Bone\#world\+To\+Parent()} to transform coordinates from world space to the parent space of a bone
\item Added {\ttfamily Bone\#local\+To\+Parent()} to transform coordinates from a bone\textquotesingle{}s local space to its parent space
\item Added non essential fields {\ttfamily icon} and {\ttfamily visible} to {\ttfamily Bone\+Data}
\item Added non essential fields {\ttfamily path} and {\ttfamily visible} to {\ttfamily Slot\+Data}
\item Added {\ttfamily set\+To\+Setup\+Pose()} to all contraint classes
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#attachment\+Threshold} to {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#mix\+Attachment\+Threshold} along with respective getters/settesr
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\+::draw\+Order\+Threshold} to {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#mix\+Draw\+Ordert\+Threshold} along with respective getters/settesr
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Transform\+Mode} to {\ttfamily Inherit} and all {\ttfamily Transform\+Mode\+\_\+\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} enums to {\ttfamily Inherit\+\_\+\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}
\item You must call {\ttfamily Skeleton\#update(delta)} before calling {\ttfamily Skeleton\#update\+World\+Transform()} if the frame time has advanced. This is needed to update physics accordingly
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\#update\+World\+Transform()} takes an additional {\ttfamily Physics} parameter. See the {\ttfamily Physics} documentation for information on what the different enum values do
\item All {\ttfamily Updatable} sub-\/classes like {\ttfamily Bone} and constraints now take an additional {\ttfamily Physics} parameter for their {\ttfamily update()} methods
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md804}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{lib\+GDX}{lib\+GDX}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md804}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md809}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Three.\+js backend}{Three.\+js backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md809}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added physics support
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md810}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Player}{Player}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md810}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added physics support
\item Added {\ttfamily scale} field to configuration which defines the scale to load the skeleton at
\item Added {\ttfamily update\+World\+Transform} field to configuration which expects a function that updates the skeleton. Defaults to player.\+skeleton.\+update\+World\+Transform(spine.\+Physics.\+update)
\item Added {\ttfamily skeleton} to {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\+Config} to specify the URL of the skeleton .json or .skel file. Deprecated {\ttfamily json\+URL} and {\ttfamily binary\+URL}. The old fields can still be used, but will be removed in \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 4.\+3
\item Added {\ttfamily atlas} to {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\+Config} to specify the URL of the .atlas file. Deprecated {\ttfamily atlas\+URL}. The old field can still be used, but will be removed in \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 4.\+3.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md811}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Pixi}{Pixi}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md811}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added spine-\/pixi runtime, also backported to \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 4.\+1. See \href{https://esotericsoftware.com/spine-pixi}{\texttt{ https\+://esotericsoftware.\+com/spine-\/pixi}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md812}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Phaser}{Phaser}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md812}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added spine-\/phaser runtime, also backported to \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 4.\+1. See \href{https://esotericsoftware.com/spine-phaser}{\texttt{ https\+://esotericsoftware.\+com/spine-\/phaser}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md813}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{Haxe}{Haxe}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md813}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md814}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{Flutter}{Flutter}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md814}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md815}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{4.\+1}{4.\+1}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md815}
\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md816}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{C}{C}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md816}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Support for sequences.
\item Support for {\ttfamily shortest\+Rotation} in animation state. See \href{https://github.com/esotericsoftware/spine-runtimes/issues/2027}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/esotericsoftware/spine-\/runtimes/issues/2027}}.
\item Added CMake parameter {\ttfamily SPINE\+\_\+\+SANITIZE} which will enable sanitizers on mac\+OS and Linux.
\item Added {\ttfamily SPINE\+\_\+\+MAJOR\+\_\+\+VERSION}, {\ttfamily SPINE\+\_\+\+MINOR\+\_\+\+VERSION}, and {\ttfamily SPINE\+\_\+\+VERSION\+\_\+\+STRING}. Parsing skeleton .JSON and .skel files will report an error if the skeleton version does not match the runtime version.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_region_attachment}{sp\+Region\+Attachment}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_mesh_attachment}{sp\+Mesh\+Attachment}} now contain a {\ttfamily sp\+Texture\+Region\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} instead of encoding region fields directly.
\item {\ttfamily sp\+\_\+\+Attachment\+Loader\+\_\+new\+Region\+Attachment()} and {\ttfamily sp\+Attachment\+Loader\+\_\+new\+Mesh\+Attachment()} now take an additional {\ttfamily Sequence\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} parameter.
\item {\ttfamily sp\+Mesh\+Attachment\+\_\+update\+UVs()} was renamed to {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_mesh_attachment_8h_a530c4562a02bf798e997d0e70f6bef54}{sp\+Mesh\+Attachment\+\_\+update\+Region()}}.
\item {\ttfamily sp\+Region\+Attachment\+\_\+update\+Offset()} was renamed to {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_region_attachment_8h_a296541039313c8c1ae8d67a198f1c4fb}{sp\+Region\+Attachment\+\_\+update\+Region()}}, {\ttfamily sp\+Region\+Attachment\+\_\+set\+UVs()} was merged into {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_region_attachment_8h_a296541039313c8c1ae8d67a198f1c4fb}{sp\+Region\+Attachment\+\_\+update\+Region()}}.
\item {\ttfamily sp\+Slot\+\_\+get\+Attachment\+Time()} and {\ttfamily sp\+Slot\+\_\+set\+Attachment\+Time()} have been removed.
\item {\ttfamily sp\+Vertex\+Attachment-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}deform\+Attachment} was renamed to {\ttfamily sp\+Vertex\+Attachment-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}timeline\+Attachment}.
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_skeleton_8h_ab2bf19cc92d104c0e5403eb4fc4c733c}{sp\+Skeleton\+\_\+update()}} has been removed.
\item {\ttfamily sp\+Skeleton-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}time} has been removed.
\item {\ttfamily sp\+Vertex\+Effect} has been removed.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md817}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SFML}{SFML}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md817}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Updated example to use SFML 2.\+5.\+1.
\item Added dragon example.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md818}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{C++}{C++}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md818}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Support for sequences.
\item Support for {\ttfamily shortest\+Rotation} in animation state. See \href{https://github.com/esotericsoftware/spine-runtimes/issues/2027}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/esotericsoftware/spine-\/runtimes/issues/2027}}.
\item Added CMake parameter {\ttfamily SPINE\+\_\+\+SANITIZE} which will enable sanitizers on mac\+OS and Linux.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily SPINE\+\_\+\+MAJOR\+\_\+\+VERSION}, {\ttfamily SPINE\+\_\+\+MINOR\+\_\+\+VERSION}, and {\ttfamily SPINE\+\_\+\+VERSION\+\_\+\+STRING}. Parsing skeleton .JSON and .skel files will report an error if the skeleton version does not match the runtime version.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Bounds\+::get\+Bounding\+Box()}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Bounds\+::get\+Polygons()}, and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Bounds\+::get\+Bounding\+Boxes()}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment} and {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment} no longer implement {\ttfamily Has\+Renderer\+Object}.
\item {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment} and {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment} now contain a {\ttfamily Texture\+Region\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} instead of encoding region fields directly.
\item {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader\+::new\+Region\+Attachment()} and {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader\+::new\+Mesh\+Attachment()} now take an additional {\ttfamily Sequence\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} parameter.
\item {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment\+::update\+UVs()} was renamed to {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment\+::update\+Region()}.
\item {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment\+::update\+Offset()} was renamed to {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment\+::update\+Region()}, {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment\+::set\+UVs()} was merged into {\ttfamily update\+Region()}.
\item {\ttfamily Slot\+::get\+Attachment\+Time()} and {\ttfamily Slot\+::set\+Attachment\+Time()} have been removed.
\item {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\+::get\+Deform\+Attachment()} was renamed to {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\+::get\+Timeline\+Attachment()}.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::update()} has been removed.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+::get\+Time()} has been removed.
\item {\ttfamily Vertex\+Effect} has been removed.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md819}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cocos2d-\/x}{Cocos2d-\/x}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md819}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+Cocos2dX} to avoid name clash with spine-\/cpp class.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md820}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SFML}{SFML}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md820}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Updated example to use SFML 2.\+5.\+1.
\item Added dragon example.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md821}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UE4}{UE4}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md821}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Updated example project to UE 4.\+27
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md822}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{C}{C}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md822}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Full support for sequences.
\item Support for {\ttfamily shortest\+Rotation} in animation state. See \href{https://github.com/esotericsoftware/spine-runtimes/issues/2027}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/esotericsoftware/spine-\/runtimes/issues/2027}}.
\item {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment} and {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment} now provide a {\ttfamily Region} property. Use this property instead of the removed {\ttfamily Renderer\+Object} property (see section {\itshape Breaking Changes} below).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Removed {\ttfamily Renderer\+Object} property from {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment} and {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment}. Use {\ttfamily attachment.\+Region} property instead. Removed removed {\ttfamily IHas\+Renderer\+Object} interface. Use {\ttfamily IHas\+Texture\+Region} instead.
\item Replaced {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+Update\+Offset} and {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment.\+Update\+UVs} with {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Update\+Region}. The caller must ensure that the attachment\textquotesingle{}s region is not {\ttfamily null}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Attachment\+Region\+Extensions} methods {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Set\+Region}, {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment.\+Set\+Region} and {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+Set\+Region(region, update)}. Use {\ttfamily attachment.\+Region = region; if (update) attachment.\+Update\+Region()} instead.
\item {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader.\+New\+Region\+Attachment()} and {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader.\+New\+Mesh\+Attachment()} take an additional {\ttfamily Sequence} parameter.
\item {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+Deform\+Attachment} property has been replaced with {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+Timeline\+Attachment}.
\item {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+Compute\+World\+Vertices()} takes a {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}} instead of a {\ttfamily Bone} as the first argument.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+Update(float delta\+Time)} method.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Slot.\+Attachment\+Time} property.
\item Removed extension method {\ttfamily Atlas\+Region.\+Get\+Spine\+Atlas\+Rect()} parameter {\ttfamily include\+Rotate} (with default value {\ttfamily true}). Most likely this method was never used with {\ttfamily include\+Rotate=false} in user code so no changes are required.
\item {\ttfamily Atlas\+Region.\+Packed\+Width} and {\ttfamily Atlas\+Region.\+Packed\+Height} are swapped compared to 4.\+0 when packing rotation is equal to 90 degrees. Most likely this property was never accessed in user code so no changes are required.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md823}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Unity}{Unity}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md823}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Officially supported Unity versions are 2017.\+1-\/2023.\+1}}.
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Spine\+Atlas\+Asset.\+Create\+Runtime\+Instance} methods now provide an optional {\ttfamily new\+Custom\+Texture\+Loader} parameter (defaults to {\ttfamily null}) which can be set to e.\+g. {\ttfamily (a) =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} new Your\+Custom\+Texture\+Loader(a)} to use your own {\ttfamily Texture\+Loader} subclass instead of {\ttfamily Materials\+Texture\+Loader}.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} now provide an Inspector parameter {\ttfamily Advanced} -\/ {\ttfamily Animation Update} with modes {\ttfamily In Update} {\bfseries{(previous behaviour, the default)}}, {\ttfamily In Fixed\+Update} and {\ttfamily Manual Update}. This allows to update animation in {\ttfamily Fixed\+Update} when using the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Root\+Motion} component (which is the recommended combination now, issuing a warning otherwise). The reason is that when root motion leads to a collision with a physics collider, it can introduce jittery excess movement when updating animation in {\ttfamily Update} due to more {\ttfamily Update} calls following a single {\ttfamily Fixed\+Update} call.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Root\+Motion} properties {\ttfamily Previous\+Rigidbody\+Root\+Motion} and {\ttfamily Additional\+Rigidbody2\+DMovement}. Setting or querying these movement vectors can be necessary when multiple scripts call {\ttfamily Rigidbody2\+D.\+Move\+Position} on the same object where the last call overwrites the effect of preceding ones.
\item {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower} and {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower\+Graphic} now provide an additional {\ttfamily Follow Parent World Scale} parameter to allow following simple scale of parent bones (rotated/skewed scale can\textquotesingle{}t be supported).
\item Improved {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ Fix Prefab Override Mesh\+Filter} property for {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} (and subclasses{\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim}), now providing an additional option to use a global value which can be set in {\ttfamily Edit -\/ Preferences -\/ \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine}}.
\item Timeline naming improvements\+: {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Animation\+State Clip} Inspector parameter {\ttfamily Custom Duration} changed and inverted to {\ttfamily Default Mix Duration} for more clarity. Shortened all Timeline add track menu entries from\+: {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_playables}{Spine.\+Unity.\+Playables} -\/ \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}track type\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} -\/ \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}track type\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Animation \doxylink{struct_state}{State} Track} to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation Track}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Animation\+State Graphic Track} to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic Track}, and {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Skeleton Flip Track} to {\ttfamily Skeleton Flip Track}.
\item Timeline track appearance and Inspector\+: Tracks now show icons and track colors to make them easier to distinguish. When a Track is selected, the Inspector now shows an editable track name which was previously only editable at the Timeline asset.
\item Added example component {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Texture} to render a {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} to a {\ttfamily Render\+Texture}, mainly for proper transparency. Added an example scene named {\ttfamily Render\+Texture Fade\+Out Transparency} that demonstrates usage for a fadeout transparency effect.
\item Added another fadeout example component named {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Texture\+Fadeout} which takes over transparency fadeout when enabled. You can use this component as-\/is, attach it in disabled state and enable it to start a fadeout effect.
\item Timeline clips now offer an additional {\ttfamily Alpha} parameter for setting a custom constant mix alpha value other than 1.\+0, just as {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+Alpha}. Defaults to 1.\+0.
\item {\ttfamily Get\+Remapped\+Clone} copying from {\ttfamily Sprite} now provides additional {\ttfamily pma\+Clone\+Texture\+Format} and {\ttfamily pma\+Clone\+Mipmaps} parameters to explicitly specify the texture format of a newly created PMA texture.
\item \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} property Inspector fields ({\ttfamily Animation Name}, {\ttfamily Bone Name}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}} and similar) now display the name in red when the respective animation/bone/etc no longer exists at the skeleton data. This may be helpful when such items have been renamed or deleted.
\item Added {\ttfamily Unscaled\+Time} property at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} as well, behaving like {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic.\+Unscaled\+Time}. If enabled, Animation\+State uses unscaled game time ({\ttfamily Time.\+unscaled\+Delta\+Time}), running animations independent of e.\+g. game pause ({\ttfamily Time.\+time\+Scale}).
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} now provide an additional {\ttfamily On\+Animation\+Rebuild} callback delegate which is issued after both the skeleton and the animation state have been initialized.
\item Timeline {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation Track} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic Track} now provide an {\ttfamily Unscaled Time} property. Whenever starting a new animation clip of this track, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation.\+Unscaled\+Time} or {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic.\+Unscaled\+Time} will be set to this value. This allows you to play back Timeline clips either in normal game time or unscaled game time. Note that {\ttfamily Playable\+Director.\+Update\+Method} is ignored and replaced by this property, which allows more fine-\/granular control per Timeline track.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Root\+Motion} callback delegates {\ttfamily Process\+Root\+Motion\+Override} and {\ttfamily Physics\+Update\+Root\+Motion\+Override} to customize how root motion is applied. The new property {\ttfamily disable\+On\+Override} determines whether the callback will be issued in addition or instead of normally applying root motion. Added property {\ttfamily root\+Motion\+Scale\+Rotation} to allow scaling rotational root-\/motion to match e.\+g. a 90 degree rotation to a custom target angle.
\item Added outline shader parameter {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ Opaque Alpha} which can be used to exclude problematic semi-\/transparent areas, which may receive an undesired large outline color overlay otherwise.
\item Added \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Preferences setting {\ttfamily Prefabs} -\/ {\ttfamily Optimize Preview Meshes}. When enabled, \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} prefab preview meshes will be removed in a pre-\/build step to reduce build size. This increases build time as all prefabs in the project will be processed. Defaults to false to not slow down builds substantially every time.
\item Added \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Preferences setting {\ttfamily Reload Skeleton\+Data after Play}. When enabled, the shared {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data} of all skeletons in the active scene is reloaded (from the {\ttfamily .json} or {\ttfamily .skel.\+bytes} file) after exiting play-\/mode. You can disable this setting to avoid the reloading delay if you can ensure that there are no (accidental) modifications to the shared {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data} during play-\/mode (otherwise it would carry over its effect into subsequent plays). Defaults to {\ttfamily true} (the safe setting), which maintains existing behaviour.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation\+Multi} sample component methods {\ttfamily Set\+Active\+Skeleton(int index)} and getter property {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animations} to more easily apply changes at all Skeleton\+Animation instances instead of only the active one.
\item PMA textures now have {\ttfamily s\+RGB (\doxylink{external_2magic__enum_2example_2example_8cpp_a692f5062ca261bdb3a62a63faddfd27f}{Color} Texture)} disabled by default, the preset template {\ttfamily PMATexture\+Preset.\+preset} has been adjusted accordingly. As PMA textures are only allowed with Gamma color space, {\ttfamily s\+RGB (\doxylink{external_2magic__enum_2example_2example_8cpp_a692f5062ca261bdb3a62a63faddfd27f}{Color} Texture)} shall be disabled to prevent border artifacts when mipmaps are enabled. In Gamma color space having this setting disabled has no drawbacks, only benefits.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Texture} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic\+Render\+Texture} components now support automatic down-\/scaling when required size on screen exceeds {\ttfamily Max Render Texture Size}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic Fill} shader to provide functionality of {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Fill} shader for {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic}.
\item Lit \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} URP shaders ({\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Sprite} and {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton Lit}) now support {\ttfamily Forward+} rendering path as introduced by Unity 2022.\+2 and URP version 14.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} now supports automatic scaling based on its {\ttfamily Rect\+Transform} bounds. Automatic scaling can be enabled by setting the added {\ttfamily Layout Scale \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode}} Inspector property to either {\ttfamily Width Controls Height}, {\ttfamily Height Controls Width}, {\ttfamily Fit\+In\+Parent} or {\ttfamily Envelope\+Parent}. It is set to {\ttfamily None} by default to keep previous behaviour and avoid breaking existing projects. To modify the reference layout bounds, hit the additional {\ttfamily Edit Layout Bounds} toggle button to switch into edit mode, adjust the bounds or hit {\ttfamily Match Rect\+Transform with Mesh}, and hit the button again when done adjusting. The skeleton will now be scaled accordingly to fit the reference layout bounds to the object\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Rect\+Transform}.
\item Added previously missing unlit URP 2D shader variant, available under {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/2\+D/\+Spine/\+Skeleton}.
\item Added support for light cookies at {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Sprite} shader.
\item Timeline extension package\+: An additional \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} preferences parameter {\ttfamily Timeline} -\/ {\ttfamily Default Mix Duration} has been added, setting newly added {\ttfamily Spine\+Animation\+State\+Clip} clips accordingly, defaults to false. This \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} preferences parameter can be enabled to default to the previous behaviour before this update.
\item Tint Black\+: Added support for \href{http://en.esotericsoftware.com/spine-slots\#Tint-black}{\texttt{ Tint Black}} functionality at all \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} URP shaders (2D and 3D shaders) and at all standard pipeline {\ttfamily Spine/\+Sprite} shaders. This feature can be enabled via the {\ttfamily Tint Black} material parameter in the Inspector. Note\+: The URP Sprite shaders provided in the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} URP Shaders extension UPM package require the latest version of the spine-\/unity runtime (package version 4.\+1.\+12, 2023-\/05-\/31 or newer) to display the added material parameters in the Inspector GUI.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic.\+Mesh\+Scale} property to allow access to calculated mesh scale. {\ttfamily Mesh\+Scale} is based on (1) Canvas pixels per unit, and (2) {\ttfamily Rect\+Transform} bounds when using {\ttfamily Layout Scale \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode}} other than {\ttfamily None} at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} which scales the skeleton mesh to fit the parent {\ttfamily Rect\+Transform} bounds accordingly.
\item Added {\ttfamily update\+Separator\+Part\+Scale} property to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} to let render separator parts follow the scale (lossy scale) of the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} Game\+Object. Defaults to {\ttfamily false} to maintain existing behaviour.
\item Added experimental {\ttfamily Editor\+Skeleton\+Player} component to allow Editor playback of the initial animation set at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} or {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} components. Add this component to your skeleton Game\+Object to enable the in-\/editor animation preview. Allows configurations for continuous playback when selected, deselected, and alternative single-\/frame preview by setting {\ttfamily Fixed Track Time} to any value other than 0. Limitations\+: At skeletons with variable material count the Inspector preview may be too unresponsive. It is then recommended to disable the {\ttfamily Editor\+Skeleton\+Player} component (at the top of the Inspector) to make it responsive again, then you can disable {\ttfamily Play When Selected} and re-\/enable the component to preview playback only when deselected.
\item Added example component {\ttfamily Render\+Combined\+Mesh} to render a combined mesh of multiple meshes or submeshes. This is required by {\ttfamily Outline\+Only} shaders to render a combined outline when using {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Separator} or multiple atlas pages which would normally lead to outlines around individual parts. To add a combined outline to your Skeleten\+Renderer\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Add a child Game\+Object and move it a bit back (e.\+g. position Z = 0.\+01).
\item Add a {\ttfamily Render\+Combined\+Mesh} component, provided in the {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Scripts/\+Sample Components} directory.
\item Copy the original material, add \+\_\+\+\_\+\+Outline\+\_\+ to its name and set the shader to your outline-\/only shader like {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Outline/\+Skeleton-\/\+Outline\+Only} or {\ttfamily Spine/\+Outline/\+Outline\+Only-\/\+ZWrite}.
\item Assign this \+\_\+\+\_\+\+Outline\+\_\+ material at the new child Game\+Object\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Mesh\+Renderer} component. If you are using {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Separator} and need to enable and disable the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Separator} component at runtime, you can increase the {\ttfamily Render\+Combined\+Mesh} {\ttfamily Reference Renderers} array by one and assign the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} itself at the last entry after the parts renderers. Disabled {\ttfamily Mesh\+Renderer} components will be skipped when combining the final mesh, so the combined mesh is automatically filled from the desired active renderers.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Timeline extension package\+: Added static {\ttfamily Editor\+Event} callback to allow editor scripts to react to animation events outside of play-\/mode. Register to the events via {\ttfamily Spine.\+Unity.\+Playables.\+Spine\+Animation\+State\+Mixer\+Behaviour.\+Editor\+Event += Your\+Callback;}.
\item URP Shaders\+: Added {\ttfamily Depth Write} property to shaders {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton} and {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton Lit}. Defaults to false to maintain existing behaviour.
\item Added {\ttfamily Animation Update} mode (called {\ttfamily Update\+Timing} in code) {\ttfamily In Late Update} for {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic}. This allows you to update the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} skeleton in the same frame that the Mecanim Animator updated its state, which happens between {\ttfamily Update} and {\ttfamily Late\+Update}.
\item URP Shaders\+: Added URP "{}\+Blend Mode"{} shader variants for both URP 3D and URP 2D renderers. They are listed under shader name "{}\+Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Blend Modes/"{} and "{}\+Universal Render Pipeline/2\+D/\+Spine/\+Blend Modes/"{} respectively.
\item URP Shaders\+: Added support for \href{http://en.esotericsoftware.com/spine-slots\#Tint-black}{\texttt{ Tint Black}} functionality at "{}\+Blend Modes"{} \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} URP shaders (2D and 3D shaders).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Made {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic.\+unscaled\+Time} parameter protected, use the new property {\ttfamily Unscaled\+Time} instead.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} {\ttfamily On\+Rebuild} callback delegate is now issued after the skeleton has been initialized, before the {\ttfamily Animation\+State} component is initialized. This makes behaviour consistent with {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} component behaviour. Use the new callback {\ttfamily On\+Animation\+Rebuild} if you want to receive a callback after the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} {\ttfamily Animation\+State} has been initialized.
\item Changed name of prefab skeleton meshes stored at prefabs from {\ttfamily Skeleton Prefab Mesh "{}name"{}} to {\ttfamily Skeleton Prefab Mesh \mbox{[}name\mbox{]}} to avoid issues with quotes in mesh asset names (see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/issues/2572}{\texttt{ this issue}}). Likely this change poses no problems at all, however if you are parsing the prefab\textquotesingle{}s mesh name for whatever reason, be sure to adjust the pattern accordingly.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Changes of default values}}
\item {\bfseries{Deprecated}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Shader macro {\ttfamily RETURN\+\_\+\+UNLIT\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+ADDITIVE\+\_\+\+SLOT} in {\ttfamily spine-\/unity/\+Shaders/\+Sprite/\+CGIncludes/\+Shader\+Shared.\+cginc} has been deprecated and will be removed in spine-\/unity 4.\+2. Use RETURN\+\_\+\+UNLIT\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+ADDITIVE\+\_\+\+SLOT\+\_\+\+TINT instead.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Restructuring (Non-\/\+Breaking)}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Moved \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} URP Shaders Examples directory from the main package directory to Samples which can be installed via the Unity Package Manager. To import, select the {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Universal RP Shaders} package in the Package Manager window, expand {\ttfamily Samples} at the bottom and hit {\ttfamily Import} next to {\ttfamily Examples}. This follows the standard \href{https://docs.unity3d.com/Manual/cus-samples.html}{\texttt{ samples guideline}} and prevents warning messages about unexpectedly altered immutable assets.
\end{DoxyItemize}

This allows users to modify bone transforms and other skeleton properties before and after the world transforms of all bones are calculated. \begin{DoxyItemize}
