\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md841}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UE4}{UE4}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md841}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Spine\+Widget} now supports the full widget transform, including rendering scale/shear.
\item Materials on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+Component} are now blueprint read and writeable. This allows setting dynamic material instances at runtime.
\item Added {\ttfamily Initial\+Skin} property to {\ttfamily USpine\+Widget}. This allows previewing different skins in the UMG Designer. Initial skins can still be overridden via blueprint events such as {\ttfamily On Initialized}.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} {\ttfamily Spine\+Widget} no longer has the {\ttfamily Scale} property. Instead the size x/y properties can be used.
\item Added {\ttfamily Set\+Slot\+Color} on {\ttfamily USpine\+Skeleton\+Component} to easily set the color of a slot via blueprints.
\item Changed mixes set on an {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\+Asset} will now be applied to instances of {\ttfamily USpine\+Skeleton\+Component}.
\item Generated normals are now correctly flipped for back faces.
\item Modifying parent materials updates material instances accordingly.
\item Only {\ttfamily .json} files that are actually encoding \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} skeletons will be loaded. Other {\ttfamily .json} files will be left to other importers.
\item Updated example project to UE 4.\+27.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md842}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{C}{C}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md842}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Timeline API has been extended to support component-\/wise timelines exported by \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 4.\+0.
\item Added {\ttfamily Animation\+State.\+clear\+Next()} which removes the given {\ttfamily Track\+Entry} and all entries after it.
\item Added support for texture atlas key value pairs, see {\ttfamily Atlas\+Region.\+names} and {\ttfamily Atlas\+Region.\+values}.
\item Added support for reverse animation playback via {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+Reverse}.
\item Added proportional spacing mode support for path constraints.
\item Added support for uniform scaling for two bone IK.
\item Fixed applying a constraint reverting changes from other constraints.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} Removed {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data} and {\ttfamily Skeleton} methods\+: {\ttfamily Find\+Bone\+Index}, {\ttfamily Find\+Slot\+Index}. Bones and slots have an {\ttfamily Index} field that should be used instead. Be sure to check for e.\+g. {\ttfamily bone == null} accordingly before accessing {\ttfamily bone.\+Index}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md843}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Unity}{Unity}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md843}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Officially supported Unity versions are 2017.\+1-\/2022.\+1}}.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Removed all {\ttfamily Spine.\+Unity.\+Attachment\+Tools.\+Skin\+Utilities} Skin extension methods. These have become obsoleted and error-\/prone since the introduction of the new Skin API in 3.\+8. To fix any compile errors, replace any usage of {\ttfamily Skin} extension methods with their counterparts, e.\+g. replace occurrances of {\ttfamily skin.\+Add\+Attachments()} with {\ttfamily skin.\+Add\+Skin()}. Please see the example scene {\ttfamily Mix and Match Skins} on how to use the new Skin API to combine skins, or the updated old example scenes {\ttfamily Mix and Match} and {\ttfamily Mix and Match Equip} on how you can update an existing project using the old workflow. If you are using {\ttfamily skeleton\+Animation.\+Skeleton.\+Unshare\+Skin()} in your code, you can replace it with {\ttfamily Skin custom\+Skin = new Skin("{}custom skin"{}); custom\+Skin.\+Add\+Skin(skeleton\+Animation.\+Skeleton.\+Skin);}.
\item {\ttfamily Skin.\+Get\+Attachments()} has been replaced by {\ttfamily Skin.\+Attachments}, returning an {\ttfamily ICollection\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Skin\+Entry\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}. This makes access more consistent and intuitive. To fix any compile errors, replace any occurrances of {\ttfamily Skin.\+Get\+Attachments()} by {\ttfamily Skin.\+Attachments}.
\item Removed redundant {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_attachment_tools_1_1_attachment_clone_extensions}{Spine.\+Unity.\+Attachment\+Tools.\+Attachment\+Clone\+Extensions}} extension methods {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Get\+Copy()} and {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Get\+Linked\+Mesh()}. To fix any compile errors, replace any occurrances with {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Copy()} and {\ttfamily Attachment.\+New\+Linked\+Mesh()}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_attachment_tools_1_1_attachment_region_extensions}{Spine.\+Unity.\+Attachment\+Tools.\+Attachment\+Region\+Extensions}} extension methods {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Get\+Region()}. Use {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Renderer\+Object as Atlas\+Region} instead.
\item Removed redundant {\ttfamily Spine.\+Skeleton\+Extensions} extension methods\+: Replace\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+Set\+Property\+To\+Setup\+Pose()}
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+Set\+Draw\+Order\+To\+Setup\+Pose()}
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+Set\+Slot\+Attachments\+To\+Setup\+Pose()}
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+Set\+Slot\+Attachment\+To\+Setup\+Pose()}
\end{DoxyItemize}

with {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+Set\+Slots\+To\+Setup\+Pose()}. Replace\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Slot.\+Set\+Color\+To\+Setup\+Pose()}
\item {\ttfamily Slot.\+Set\+Attachment\+To\+Setup\+Pose()}
\end{DoxyItemize}

with {\ttfamily Slot.\+Set\+To\+Setup\+Pose()}.

Also removed less commonly used extension methods\+: {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+Allow\+Immediate\+Queue()}, {\ttfamily Animation.\+Set\+Keyed\+Items\+To\+Setup\+Pose()} and {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Is\+Renderable()}.
\item {\bfseries{{\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} now no longer uses a {\ttfamily Raw\+Image} component at each submesh renderer}} Game\+Object when {\ttfamily allow\+Multiple\+Canvas\+Renderers} is true. Instead, a new custom component {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Submesh\+Graphic} is used which is more resource friendly. Replacement of these components will be performed automatically through editor scripting, saving scenes or prefabs will persist the upgrade.
\item {\bfseries{Linear color space\+:}} Previously \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot} colors were not displayed the same in Unity as in the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Editor. This is now fixed at all shaders, including URP and LWRP shaders. See section {\itshape Additions} below for more details. If you have tweaked \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot} colors to look correct in {\ttfamily Linear} color space in Unity but incorrect in \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine}, you might want to adjust the tweaked colors. \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot} colors displayed in Unity should now match colors displayed in the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Editor when configured to display as {\ttfamily Linear} color space in the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Editor Settings.
\item {\bfseries{Additive Slots have always been lit}} before they were written to the target buffer. Now all lit shaders provide an additional parameter {\ttfamily Light Affects Additive} which defaults to {\ttfamily false}, as it is the more intuitive default value. You can enable the old behaviour by setting this parameter to {\ttfamily true}.
\item {\bfseries{Corrected blending behaviour of all {\ttfamily Sprite} shaders}} in {\ttfamily Premultiply Alpha} blend mode (including URP and LWRP packages). Previously vertex color alpha was premultiplied again, even though {\ttfamily Premultiply Alpha} blend mode assumes PMA texture and PMA vertex color input. Slot-\/alpha blending will thus be correctly lighter after upgrading to 4.\+0. If you have compensated this problem by disabling {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ PMA \doxylink{struct_vertex}{Vertex} Colors} you can now re-\/enable this parameter, also allowing for rendering Additive slots in a single pass.
\item {\bfseries{Corrected all {\ttfamily Outline} shaders outline thickness}} when {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ Sample 8 Neighbourhood} is disabled (thus using {\ttfamily 4 Neighbourhood}). Previously weighting was incorrectly thick (4x as thick) compared to 8 neighbourhood, now it is more consistent. This might require adjustment of all your outline materials where {\ttfamily Sample 8 Neighbourhood} is disabled to restore the previous outline thickness, by adjusting the {\ttfamily Outline Threshold} parameter through adding a {\ttfamily /4} to make the threshold 4 times smaller.
\item Reverted changes\+: {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower} property {\ttfamily follow\+Local\+Scale} has intermediately been renamed to {\ttfamily follow\+Scale} but was renamed back to {\ttfamily follow\+Local\+Scale}. Serialized values (scenes and prefabs) will automatically be upgraded, only code accessing {\ttfamily follow\+Scale} needs to be adapted.
\item Fixed Timeline not pausing (and resuming) clip playback on Director pause, this is now the default behaviour. If you require the old behaviour (e.\+g. to continue playing an idle animation during Director pause), there is now an additional parameter {\ttfamily Don\textquotesingle{}t Pause with Director} provided that can be enabled for each Timeline clip.
\item Fixed Timeline {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Animation\+State Clips} ignoring empty space on the Timeline after a clip\textquotesingle{}s end. Timeline clips now also offer {\ttfamily Don\textquotesingle{}t End with Clip} and {\ttfamily Clip End Mix Out Duration} parameters if you prefer the old behaviour of previous versions. By default when empty space follows the clip on the timeline, the empty animation is set on the track with a Mix\+Duration of {\ttfamily Clip End Mix Out Duration}. Set {\ttfamily Don\textquotesingle{}t End with Clip} to {\ttfamily true} to continue playing the clip\textquotesingle{}s animation instead and mimic the old 3.\+8 behaviour. If you prefer pausing the animation instead of mixing out to the empty animation, set {\ttfamily Clip End Mix Out Duration} to a value less than 0, then the animation is paused instead.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions and Improvements}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Additional {\bfseries{Fix Draw Order}} parameter at Skeleton\+Renderer, defaults to {\ttfamily disabled} (previous behaviour). Applies only when 3+ submeshes are used (2+ materials with alternating order, e.\+g. "{}\+A B A"{}). If {\ttfamily true}, Material\+Property\+Blocks are assigned at each material to prevent aggressive batching of submeshes by e.\+g. the LWRP renderer, leading to incorrect draw order (e.\+g. "{}\+A1 B A2"{} changed to "{}\+A1\+A2 B"{}). You can leave this parameter disabled when everything is drawn correctly to save the additional performance cost.
\item {\bfseries{Additional Timeline features.}} Spine\+Animation\+State\+Clip now provides a {\ttfamily Speed Multiplier}, a start time offset parameter {\ttfamily Clip In}, support for blending successive animations by overlapping tracks. An additional {\ttfamily Use Blend Duration} parameter {\itshape (defaults to true)} allows for automatic synchronisation of Mix\+Duration with the current overlap blend duration. An additional \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} preferences parameter {\ttfamily Use Blend Duration} has been added which can be disabled to default to the previous behaviour before this update.
\item Additional {\ttfamily Sprite\+Mask and Rect\+Mask2D} example scene added for demonstration of mask setup and interaction.
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{boostmultiprec_8cpp_ad5abe8020ead32dcab5e3c15d6d7c30e}{Real} physics hinge chains} for both 2D and 3D physics. The \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#SkeletonUtilityBone}{\texttt{ Skeleton\+Utility\+Bone}} Inspector provides an interface to create 2D and 3D hinge chains. Previously created chains have only been respecting gravity, but not momentum of the skeleton or parent bones. The new physics rig created when pressing {\ttfamily Create 3D Hinge Chain} and {\ttfamily Create 2D Hinge Chain} creates a more complex setup that also works when flipping the skeleton. Note that the chain root node is no longer parented to bones of the skeleton. This is a requirement in Unity to have momentum applied properly -\/ do not reparent the chain root to bones of your skeleton, or you will loose any momentum applied by the skeleton\textquotesingle{}s movement.
\item {\ttfamily Outline rendering functionality for all shaders.} Every shader now provides an additional set of {\ttfamily Outline} parameters to enable custom outline rendering. When outline rendering is enabled via the {\ttfamily Material} inspector, it automatically switches the shader to the respective {\ttfamily Spine/\+Outline} shader variant. Outlines are generated by sampling neighbour pixels, so be sure to add enough transparent padding when exporting your atlas textures to fit the desired outline width. In order to enable outline rendering at a skeleton, it is recommended to first prepare an additional outline material copy and then switch the material of the target skeleton to this material. This prevents unnecessary additional runtime material copies and drawcalls. Material switching can be prepared via a \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#SkeletonRendererCustomMaterials}{\texttt{ Skeleton\+Renderer\+Custom\+Materials}} component and then enabled or disabled at runtime. Alternatively, you can also directly modify the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer.\+Custom\+Material\+Override} property. Outline rendering is fully supported on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} shaders as well.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer.\+Editor\+Skip\+Skin\+Sync} scripting API property to be able to set custom skins in editor scripts. Enable this property when overwriting the Skeleton\textquotesingle{}s skin from an editor script. Without setting this parameter, changes will be overwritten by the next inspector update. Only affects Inspector synchronisation of skin with {\ttfamily initial\+Skin\+Name}, not startup initialization.
\item {\ttfamily Atlas\+Utilities.\+Get\+Repacked\+Attachments()} and {\ttfamily Atlas\+Utilities.\+Get\+Repacked\+Skin()} provide support for additional texture channels such as normal maps via the optional parameter {\ttfamily additional\+Texture\+Property\+IDs\+To\+Copy}. See the spine-\/unity runtime documentation, section \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#Combining-Skins}{\texttt{ Combining Skins -\/ Advanced -\/ Runtime Repacking with Normalmaps}} for further info and example usage code.
\item {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower} can now optionally follow (uniform) world scale of the reference bone. There is now a {\ttfamily \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode}} dropdown selector in the Inspector which can be set to either {\ttfamily Local} or {\ttfamily World Uniform}.
\item All {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic} shaders now provide a parameter {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group Compatible} which can be enabled to support {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group} alpha blending. For correct results, you should then disable {\ttfamily Pma \doxylink{struct_vertex}{Vertex} Colors} in the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} Inspector, in section {\ttfamily Advanced} (otherwise \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot} alpha will be applied twice).
\item {\bfseries{Now supporting Universal Render Pipeline (URP), including the 2D Renderer pipeline, through an additional UPM package.}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Installation\+:}} You can download the Unity Package Manager (UPM) package via the \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity-download}{\texttt{ download page}} or find it in the \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/tree/3.8-beta/spine-unity/Modules}{\texttt{ spine-\/runtimes/spine-\/unity/\+Modules}} subdirectory on the git repository. You can then either unzip (copy if using git) the package to
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item a) the {\ttfamily Packages} directory in your project where it will automatically be loaded, or
\item b) to an arbitrary directory outside the Assets directory and then open Package Manager in Unity, select the {\ttfamily +} icon, choose {\ttfamily Add package from disk..} and point it to the package.\+json file.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The Project panel should now show an entry {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Universal RP Shaders} under {\ttfamily Packages}. If the directory is not yet listed, you will need to close and re-\/open Unity to have it display the directory and its contents.
\item {\bfseries{Usage\+:}} The package provides two shaders specifically built for the universal render pipeline\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton}, as a universal variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton} shader,
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton Lit}, as a universal variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Lit} shader,
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Sprite}, as a universal variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Sprite/\+Vertex Lit} and {\ttfamily Pixel Lit} shaders, which were not functioning in the universal render pipeline,
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/2\+D/\+Spine/\+Skeleton Lit}, as a universal 2D Renderer variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Lit} shader, and
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/2\+D/\+Spine/\+Sprite}, as a universal 2D Renderer variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Sprite/\+Vertex Lit} and {\ttfamily Pixel Lit} shaders. The shaders can be assigned to materials as usual and will respect your settings of the assigned {\ttfamily Universal\+Render\+Pipeline\+Asset} under {\ttfamily Project Settings -\/ Graphics}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Restrictions}} As all \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} shaders, the URP shaders {\bfseries{do not support {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha} (PMA) atlas textures in Linear color space}}. Please export your atlas textures as {\ttfamily straight alpha} textures with disabled {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha} setting when using Linear color space. You can check the current color space via {\ttfamily Project Settings -\/ Player -\/ Other Settings -\/ \doxylink{external_2magic__enum_2example_2example_8cpp_a692f5062ca261bdb3a62a63faddfd27f}{Color} Space.}.
\item {\bfseries{Example\+:}} You can find an example scene in the package under {\ttfamily com.\+esotericsoftware.\+spine.\+urp-\/shaders-\/3.\+8/\+Examples/\+URP Shaders.\+unity} that demonstrates usage of the URP shaders.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Preferences now provide an {\bfseries{{\ttfamily Atlas Texture Settings}}} parameter for applying customizable texture import settings at all newly imported \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} atlas textures. When exporting atlas textures from \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} with {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha} enabled (the default), you can leave it at {\ttfamily PMATexture\+Preset}. If you have disabled {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha}, set it to the included {\ttfamily Straight\+Alpha\+Texture\+Preset} asset. You can also create your own {\ttfamily Texture\+Importer} {\ttfamily Preset} asset and assign it here (include {\ttfamily PMA} or {\ttfamily Straight} in the name). In Unity versions before 2018.\+3 you can use {\ttfamily Texture2D} template assets instead of the newer {\ttfamily Preset} assets. Materials created for imported textures will also have the {\ttfamily Straight Alpha Texture} parameter configured accordingly.
\item All {\ttfamily Sprite} shaders (including URP and LWRP extension packages) now provide an additional {\ttfamily Fixed Normal Space} option {\ttfamily World-\/\+Space}. PReviously options were limited to {\ttfamily View-\/\+Space} and {\ttfamily Model-\/\+Space}.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} now fully supports \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#SkeletonUtility}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility}}} for generating a hierarchy of \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#SkeletonUtilityBone}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Bones}}} in both modes {\ttfamily Follow} and {\ttfamily Override}. This also enables creating hinge chain physics rigs and using {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Constraints} such as {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Ground\+Constraint} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Eye\+Constraint} on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic}.
\item Added {\bfseries{native support for slot blend modes}} {\ttfamily Additive}, {\ttfamily Multiply} and {\ttfamily Screen} with automatic assignment at newly imported skeleton assets. {\ttfamily Blend\+Mode\+Material\+Assets} are now obsolete and replaced by the native properties at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\+Asset}. The {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\+Asset} Inspector provides a new {\ttfamily Blend Modes -\/ Upgrade} button to upgrade an obsolete {\ttfamily Blend\+Mode\+Material\+Asset} to the native blend modes properties. This upgrade will be performed automatically on imported and re-\/imported assets.
\item {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower} and {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower\+Graphic} components now provide better support for following bones when the skeleton\textquotesingle{}s Transform is not the parent of the follower\textquotesingle{}s Transform. Previously e.\+g. rotating a common parent Transform did not lead to the desired result, as well as negatively scaling a skeleton\textquotesingle{}s Transform when it is not a parent of the follower\textquotesingle{}s Transform.
\item {\bfseries{Linear color space\+:}} Previously \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot} colors were not displayed the same in Unity as in the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Editor (when configured to display as {\ttfamily Linear} color space in \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Editor Settings). This is now fixed at all shaders, including URP and LWRP shaders.
\item All \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} shaders (also including URP and LWRP shaders) now support {\ttfamily PMA \doxylink{struct_vertex}{Vertex} Colors} in combination with {\ttfamily Linear} color space. Thus when using \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} shaders, you should always enable {\ttfamily PMA \doxylink{struct_vertex}{Vertex} Colors} at the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} component. This allows using single pass {\ttfamily Additive} Slots rendering. Note that textures shall still be exported as {\ttfamily Straight alpha} when using {\ttfamily Linear} color space, so combine {\ttfamily PMA \doxylink{struct_vertex}{Vertex} Colors} with {\ttfamily Straight Texture}. All {\ttfamily Sprite} shaders now provide an additional blend mode for this, named {\ttfamily PMA \doxylink{struct_vertex}{Vertex}, Straight Texture} which shall be the preferred Sprite shader blend mode in {\ttfamily Linear} color space.
\item Additive Slots have always been lit before they were written to the target buffer. Now all lit shaders provide an additional parameter {\ttfamily Light Affects Additive} which defaults to {\ttfamily false}, as it is the more intuitive default value. You can enable the old behaviour by setting this parameter to {\ttfamily true}.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Root\+Motion} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim\+Root\+Motion} components now support arbitrary bones in the hierarchy as {\ttfamily Root Motion Bone}. Previously there were problems when selecting a non-\/root bone as {\ttfamily Root Motion Bone}. {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+ScaleX} and {\ttfamily .ScaleY} and parent bone scale is now respected as well.
\item URP and LWRP {\ttfamily Sprite} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Lit} shaders no longer require {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ Add Normals} enabled to properly cast and receive shadows. It is recommended to disable {\ttfamily Add Normals} if normals are otherwise not needed.
\item Added an example component {\ttfamily Root\+Motion\+Delta\+Compensation} located in {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Scripts/\+Sample Components} which can be used for applying simple delta compensation. You can enable and disable the component to toggle delta compensation of the currently playing animation on and off.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Ragdoll} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Ragdoll2D} now support bone scale at any bone in the skeleton hierarchy. This includes negative scale and root bone scale.
\item {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Get\+Remapped\+Clone(\+Sprite)} method now provides an additional optional parameter {\ttfamily use\+Original\+Region\+Scale}. When set to {\ttfamily true}, the replaced attachment\textquotesingle{}s scale is used instead of the Sprite\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Pixel per Unity} setting, allowing for more consistent scaling. {\itshape Note\+:} When remapping Sprites, be sure to set the Sprite\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Mesh \doxylink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{Type}} to {\ttfamily Full Rect} and not {\ttfamily Tight}, otherwise the scale will be wrong.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} now {\bfseries{supports all \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot} blend modes}} when {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ Multiple Canvas Renderers} is enabled in the Inspector. The {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} Inspector now provides a {\ttfamily Blend \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode} Materials} section where you can assign {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} materials for each blend mode, or use the new default materials. New {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} shaders and materials have been added for each blend mode. The {\ttfamily Blend\+Modes.\+unity} example scene has been extended to demonstrate this new feature. For detailed information see the \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#Parameters}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic documentation page}}}.
\item Timeline clips now also offer {\ttfamily Don\textquotesingle{}t End with Clip} and {\ttfamily Clip End Mix Out Duration} parameters. By default when empty space follows the clip on the timeline, the empty animation is set on the track with a Mix\+Duration of {\ttfamily Clip End Mix Out Duration}. Set {\ttfamily Don\textquotesingle{}t End with Clip} to {\ttfamily true} to continue playing the clip\textquotesingle{}s animation instead and mimic the old 3.\+8 behaviour. If you prefer pausing the animation instead of mixing out to the empty animation, set {\ttfamily Clip End Mix Out Duration} to a value less than 0, then the animation is paused instead.
\item Prefabs containing {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} now provide a proper Editor preview, including the preview thumbnail.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} (and subclasses{\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim}) now provide a property {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ Fix Prefab Override Mesh\+Filter}, which when enabled fixes the prefab always being marked as changed. It sets the Mesh\+Filter\textquotesingle{}s hide flags to {\ttfamily Dont\+Save\+In\+Editor}. Unfortunately this comes at the cost of references to the {\ttfamily Mesh\+Filter} by other components being lost, therefore this parameter defaults to {\ttfamily false} to keep the safe existing behaviour.
\item {\ttfamily Bounding\+Box\+Follower} and {\ttfamily Bounding\+Box\+Follower\+Graphic} now provide previously missing {\ttfamily used\+By\+Effector} and {\ttfamily used\+By\+Composite} parameters to be set at all generated colliders.
\item {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower} and {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower\+Graphic} now provide an additional {\ttfamily Follow Parent World Scale} parameter to allow following simple scale of parent bones (rotated/skewed scale can\textquotesingle{}t be supported).
\item Improved {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ Fix Prefab Override Mesh\+Filter} property for {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} (and subclasses{\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim}), now providing an additional option to use a global value which can be set in {\ttfamily Edit -\/ Preferences -\/ \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine}}.
\item Timeline naming improvements\+: {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Animation\+State Clip} Inspector parameter {\ttfamily Custom Duration} changed and inverted to {\ttfamily Default Mix Duration} for more clarity. Shortened all Timeline add track menu entries from\+: {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_playables}{Spine.\+Unity.\+Playables} -\/ \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}track type\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} -\/ \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}track type\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Animation \doxylink{struct_state}{State} Track} to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation Track}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Animation\+State Graphic Track} to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic Track}, and {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Skeleton Flip Track} to {\ttfamily Skeleton Flip Track}.
\item Timeline track appearance and Inspector\+: Tracks now show icons and track colors to make them easier to distinguish. When a Track is selected, the Inspector now shows an editable track name which was previously only editable at the Timeline asset.
\item Added example component {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Texture} to render a {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} to a {\ttfamily Render\+Texture}, mainly for proper transparency. Added an example scene named {\ttfamily Render\+Texture Fade\+Out Transparency} that demonstrates usage for a fadeout transparency effect.
\item Added another fadeout example component named {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Texture\+Fadeout} which takes over transparency fadeout when enabled. You can use this component as-\/is, attach it in disabled state and enable it to start a fadeout effect.
\item Timeline clips now offer an additional {\ttfamily Alpha} parameter for setting a custom constant mix alpha value other than 1.\+0, just as {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+Alpha}. Defaults to 1.\+0.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} now provides additional render callback delegates {\ttfamily On\+Instructions\+Prepared}, {\ttfamily Assign\+Mesh\+Override\+Single\+Renderer} and {\ttfamily Assign\+Mesh\+Override\+Multiple\+Renderers}. {\ttfamily On\+Instructions\+Prepared} is raised at the end of Late\+Update after render instructions are done, target renderers are prepared, and the mesh is ready to be generated. The two {\ttfamily Assign\+Mesh\+Override} delegates allow separate code to take over mesh and material assignment of a {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} component.
\item Added example component {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic\+Render\+Texture} to render a {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} to a {\ttfamily Render\+Texture} (similar as {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Texture}), mainly for proper transparency. Extended example scene {\ttfamily Render\+Texture Fade\+Out Transparency} accordingly.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Changes of default values}}
\item {\bfseries{Deprecated}}
\item {\bfseries{Restructuring (Non-\/\+Breaking)}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md844}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XNA/\+Mono\+Game}{XNA/\+Mono\+Game}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md844}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added normalmap support via {\ttfamily Spine\+Effect\+Normalmap} and support for loading multiple texture layers following a suffix-\/pattern. Please see the example code on how to use them.
\item Added {\ttfamily Z} property to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} to provide a constant Z offset that\textquotesingle{}s added to all vertices.
\item Added {\ttfamily ZSpacing} property to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} to allow specifying the distance on the z-\/axis between attachments.
\item Skeleton\+Debug\+Renderer bone color attributes are now public and modifiable by user.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md845}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Java}{Java}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md845}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Timeline API has been extended to support component-\/wise timelines exported by \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 4.\+0.
\item Added {\ttfamily Animation\+State.\+clear\+Next()} which removes the given {\ttfamily Track\+Entry} and all entries after it.
\item Added support for texture atlas key value pairs, see {\ttfamily Region.\+names} and {\ttfamily Region.\+values}.
\item Added support for reverse animation playback via {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+get\+Reverse()} and {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+set\+Reverse()}.
\item Added proportional spacing mode support for path constraints.
\item Added support for uniform scaling for two bone IK.
\item Fixed applying a constraint reverting changes from other constraints.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} Removed {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data} and {\ttfamily Skeleton} methods\+: {\ttfamily find\+Bone\+Index}, {\ttfamily find\+Slot\+Index}. Bones and slots have an {\ttfamily index} field that should be used instead.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md846}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lib\+GDX}{lib\+GDX}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md846}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Exposed colors in {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+Debug}.
\item Updated to lib\+GDX 1.\+10.\+0.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md847}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Lua}{Lua}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md847}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Expose non-\/essential colors on bones, bounding box, clipping, and path attachments.
\item Timeline API has been extended to support component-\/wise timelines exported by \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 4.\+0.
\item Added {\ttfamily Animation\+State.\+clear\+Next()} which removes the given {\ttfamily Track\+Entry} and all entries after it.
\item Added support for texture atlas key value pairs, see {\ttfamily Atlas\+Region.\+names} and {\ttfamily Atlas\+Region.\+values}.
\item Added support for reverse animation playback via {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+reverse}.
\item Added proportional spacing mode support for path constraints.
\item Added support for uniform scaling for two bone IK.
\item Fixed applying a constraint reverting changes from other constraints.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md848}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Love2D}{Love2D}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md848}
\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md849}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Corona}{Corona}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md849}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} spine-\/corona has been renamed to spine-\/solar2d. Change your {\ttfamily require "{}spine-\/corona.\+spine"{}} statements to {\ttfamily require "{}spine-\/solar2d.\+spine"{}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md850}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Typescript/\+Javascript}{Typescript/\+Javascript}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md850}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} refactored to ECMAScript modules. See this \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/blog/spine-goes-npm}{\texttt{ blog post}} as well as the updated \doxylink{external_2spine-runtimes_2spine-ts_2_r_e_a_d_m_e_8md}{README.md}.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} the {\ttfamily build/} folder and compiled artifacts are no longer part of the repository. Instead, {\ttfamily npm run build} in {\ttfamily spine-\/ts/} to generate ECMAScript modules and IIFE modules in {\ttfamily spine-\/\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}module-\/name\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}/dist}.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} the {\ttfamily .npmignore} and {\ttfamily package.\+json} files in the root directory have been deleted. Use the corresponding files in {\ttfamily spine-\/ts/} instead, or better, depend on the packages from the NPM registry.
\item Updated runtime to be compatible with Type\+Script 3.\+6.\+3.
\item Added {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager\#set\+Raw\+Data\+URI(path, data)}. Allows to set raw data URIs for a specific path, which in turn enables embedding assets into Java\+Script/\+HTML.
\item Expose non-\/essential colors on bones, bounding box, clipping, and path attachments.
\item Timeline API has been extended to support component-\/wise timelines exported by \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 4.\+0.
\item Added {\ttfamily Animation\+State.\+clear\+Next()} which removes the given {\ttfamily Track\+Entry} and all entries after it.
\item Added support for texture atlas key value pairs, see {\ttfamily Atlas\+Region.\+names} and {\ttfamily Atlas\+Region.\+values}.
\item Added support for reverse animation playback via {\ttfamily Track\+Entry.\+reverse}.
\item Added proportional spacing mode support for path constraints.
\item Added support for uniform scaling for two bone IK.
\item Fixed applying a constraint reverting changes from other constraints.
\item {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager} constructor now takes an option {\ttfamily Downloader} instance. Used to download assets only once and share them between {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager} instances.
\item Added web worker support to {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager}.
\item Added various default parameters to {\ttfamily Animation\+State} methods for ease of use.
\item Added {\ttfamily Spine\+Canvas}, a simpler way to render a scene via spine-\/webgl. See {\ttfamily spine-\/ts/spine-\/webgl/examples/barebones.\+html} and {\ttfamily spine-\/ts/spine-\/webgl/examples/mix-\/and-\/match.\+html}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md851}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Web\+GL backend}{Web\+GL backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md851}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} removed {\ttfamily Shared\+Asset\+Manager}. Use {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager} with a shared {\ttfamily Downloader} instance instead.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} the global object {\ttfamily spine.\+webgl} no longer exists. All classes and functions are now exposed on the global {\ttfamily spine} object directly. Simply replace any reference to {\ttfamily spine.\+webgl.} in your source code with {\ttfamily spine.}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md852}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Canvas backend}{Canvas backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md852}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Renderer now accounts for whitespace stripping.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} the global object {\ttfamily spine.\+canvas} no longer exists. All classes and functions are now exposed on the global {\ttfamily spine} object directly. Simply replace any reference to {\ttfamily spine.\+canvas.} in your source code with {\ttfamily spine.}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md853}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Three.\+js backend}{Three.\+js backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md853}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mesh} now takes an optional {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mesh\+Material\+Parameters\+Customizer} function that allows you to modify the {\ttfamily Shader\+Material\+Parameters} before the material is finalized. Use it to modify things like THREEJS\textquotesingle{} {\ttfamily Material.\+depth\+Test} etc. See \#1590.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} the global object {\ttfamily spine.\+canvas} no longer exists. All classes and functions are now exposed on the global {\ttfamily spine} object directly. Simply replace any reference to {\ttfamily spine.\+threejs.} in your source code with {\ttfamily spine.}.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} the default fragment shader of {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mesh\+Material} now explicitely discards fragments with alpha \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0.\+5. See \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/issues/1985}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/issues/1985}}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} reversal of the previous breaking change\+: the default fragment shader of {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mesh\+Material} does no longer discard fragments with alpha \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0.\+5. Pass a {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mesh\+Material\+Parameters\+Customizer} to the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mesh} constructor, and modify {\ttfamily parameters.\+alpha\+Test} to be \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md854}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Player}{Player}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md854}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\+Config.\+raw\+Data\+URIs}. Allows to embed data URIs for skeletons, atlases and atlas page images directly in the HTML/\+JS without needing to load it from a separate file. See the example for a demonstration.
\item Added {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\+Config.\+frame}. If set, the callback is called each frame, before the skeleton is posed or drawn.
\item Added {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\+Config.\+update}. If set, the callback is called each frame, just after the skeleton is posed.
\item Added {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\+Config.\+draw}. If set, the callback is called each frame, just after the skeleton is drawn.
\item Added {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\+Config.\+downloader}. The {\ttfamily spine.\+Downloader} instance can be shared between players so assets are only downloaded once.
\item If {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\+Config.\+json\+URL} ends with an anchor, the anchor text is used to find the skeleton in the specified JSON file.
\item Added {\ttfamily Spine\+Player.\+dispose()}, disposes all CPU and GPU side resources, removes all listeners, and removes the player DOM from the parent.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md855}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{3.\+8}{3.\+8}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md855}
\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md856}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{AS3}{AS3}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md856}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}\#get\+Attachment\+Vertices()} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}\#get\+Deform()}.
\item Changed the {\ttfamily .json} curve format and added more assumptions for omitted values, reducing the average size of JSON exports.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Skin\#add\+Attachment()} to {\ttfamily Skin\#set\+Attachment()}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\#apply\+Deform()} and replaced it with {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\#deform\+Attachment}. The attachment set on this field is used to decide if a {\ttfamily Deform\+Timeline} should be applied to the attachment active on the slot to which the timeline is applied.
\item Removed {\ttfamily inherit\+Deform} field, getter, and setter from {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment}.
\item Changed {\ttfamily .skel} binary format, added a string table. References to strings in the data resolve to this string table, reducing storage size of binary files considerably.
\item Changed the {\ttfamily .json} and {\ttfamily .skel} file formats to accomodate the new feature and file size optimiations. Old projects must be exported with \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 3.\+8.\+20+ to be compatible with the 3.\+8 \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} runtimes.
\item Switched projects from FDT to Visual Studio Code. See updated {\ttfamily README.\+md} files for instructions.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Binary} to load binary {\ttfamily .skel} files. See {\ttfamily Mix\+And\+Match\+Example.\+as} in {\ttfamily spine-\/startling-\/example}.
\item Added {\ttfamily x} and {\ttfamily y} coordinates for setup pose AABB in {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data}.
\item Added support for rotated mesh region UVs.
\item Added skin-\/specific bones and constraints which are only updated if the skeleton\textquotesingle{}s current skin contains them.
\item Improved Skin API to make it easier to handle mix-\/and-\/match use cases.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#get\+Attachments()}. Returns all attachments in the skin.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#get\+Attachments(int slot\+Index)}. Returns all attachements in the skin for the given slot index.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#add\+Skin(\+Skin skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#copy\+Skin(\+Skin skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin. {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment} are shallowly copied and will retain any parent mesh relationship. All other attachment types are deep copied.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Attachment\#\doxylink{level1__impl_8h_a7ffc26122ca6f9bec01f9bc5e64f3006}{copy()}} to all attachment type implementations. This lets you deep copy an attachment to modify it independently from the original, i.\+e. when programmatically changing texture coordinates or mesh vertices.
\item Added {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment\#new\+Linked\+Mesh()}, creates a linked mesh linkted to either the original mesh, or the parent of the original mesh.
\item Added IK softness.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md857}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Starling}{Starling}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md857}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Mix\+And\+Match\+Example.\+as} to demonstrate the new Skin API additions and how to load binary {\ttfamily .skel} files.
\item Switched projects from FDT to Visual Studio Code. See updated {\ttfamily README.\+md} files for instructions.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md858}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{C}{C}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md858}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}

\item Changed the {\ttfamily .json} curve format and added more assumptions for omitted values, reducing the average size of JSON exports.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily sp\+Skin\+\_\+add\+Attachment()} to {\ttfamily Skin\#sp\+Skin\+\_\+add\+Attachment()}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily sp\+Vertex\+Attachment\+\_\+apply\+Deform()} and replaced it with {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\#deform\+Attachment}. The attachment set on this field is used to decide if a {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_deform_timeline}{sp\+Deform\+Timeline}} should be applied to the attachment active on the slot to which the timeline is applied.
\item Removed {\ttfamily inherit\+Deform} field, getter, and setter from {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_mesh_attachment}{sp\+Mesh\+Attachment}}.
\item Changed {\ttfamily .skel} binary format, added a string table. References to strings in the data resolve to this string table, reducing storage size of binary files considerably.

\item Added support for rotated mesh region UVs.
\item Added skin-\/specific bones and constraints which are only updated if the skeleton\textquotesingle{}s current skin contains them.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_skin_8h_a82d24c4f7bd2fd4618ad1157daca7bfc}{sp\+Skin\+\_\+get\+Attachments()}}. Returns all attachments in the skin.

\item Added {\ttfamily sp\+Skin\+\_\+add\+Skin(sp\+Skin\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin.
\item Added {\ttfamily sp\+Skin\+\_\+copy\+Skin(sp\+Skin\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin. {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_vertex_attachment}{sp\+Vertex\+Attachment}} are shallowly copied and will retain any parent mesh relationship. All other attachment types are deep copied.
\item All attachments inserted into skins are reference counted. When the last skin referencing an attachment is disposed, the attachment will also be disposed.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_attachment_8h_a2add982a3f7f8133e4d4d028fe1a5e5b}{sp\+Attachment\+\_\+copy()}} to all attachment type implementations. This lets you deep copy an attachment to modify it independently from the original, i.\+e. when programmatically changing texture coordinates or mesh vertices.
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{spine-c_2include_2spine_2_mesh_attachment_8h_a22fa8d109b80c9ba18159f4d95c9ee2f}{sp\+Mesh\+Attachment\+\_\+new\+Linked\+Mesh()}}, creates a linked mesh linkted to either the original mesh, or the parent of the original mesh.
\item Added IK softness.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking Changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Slot\+::get\+Attachment\+Vertices()} to {\ttfamily Slot\+::get\+Deform()}.
\item Changed the {\ttfamily .json} curve format and added more assumptions for omitted values, reducing the average size of JSON exports.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Skin\+::add\+Attachment()} to {\ttfamily Skin\+::set\+Attachment()}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\+::apply\+Deform()} and replaced it with {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\+::get\+Deform\+Attachment()}. The attachment set on this field is used to decide if a {\ttfamily Deform\+Timeline} should be applied to the attachment active on the slot to which the timeline is applied.
\item Removed {\ttfamily \+\_\+inherit\+Deform} field, getter, and setter from {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment}.
\item Changed {\ttfamily .skel} binary format, added a string table. References to strings in the data resolve to this string table, reducing storage size of binary files considerably.
\item Changed the {\ttfamily .json} and {\ttfamily .skel} file formats to accomodate the new feature and file size optimiations. Old projects must be exported with \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 3.\+8.\+20+ to be compatible with the 3.\+8 \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} runtimes.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Animation\+State} and {\ttfamily Track\+Entry} now also accept a subclass of {\ttfamily Animation\+State\+Listener\+Object} as a listener for animation events in the overloaded {\ttfamily set\+Listener()} method.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Binary} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Json} now parse and set all non-\/essential data like audio path.
\item Added {\ttfamily x} and {\ttfamily y} coordinates for setup pose AABB in {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data}.
\item Added support for rotated mesh region UVs.
\item Added skin-\/specific bones and constraints which are only updated if the skeleton\textquotesingle{}s current skin contains them.
\item Improved Skin API to make it easier to handle mix-\/and-\/match use cases.
\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#get\+Attachments(int slot\+Index)}. Returns all attachements in the skin for the given slot index.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#add\+Skin(Skin \&skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#copy\+Skin(Skin \&skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin. {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment} are shallowly copied and will retain any parent mesh relationship. All other attachment types are deep copied.
\item All attachments inserted into skins are reference counted. When the last skin referencing an attachment is disposed, the attachment will also be disposed.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Attachment\#\doxylink{level1__impl_8h_a7ffc26122ca6f9bec01f9bc5e64f3006}{copy()}} to all attachment type implementations. \item Added {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment\#new\+Linked\+Mesh()}, creates a linked mesh linkted to either the original mesh, or the parent of the original mesh.
\item Added IK softness.
\item Exposed {\ttfamily x} and {\ttfamily y} on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data} through getters and setters.
\end{DoxyItemize}
