\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md864}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UE4}{UE4}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md864}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily b\+Auto\+Playing} flag to {\ttfamily USpine\+Skeleton\+Animation\+Component}. When {\ttfamily false}, the component will not update the internal animation state and skeleton.
\item Updated example project to UE 4.\+22.
\item (Re-\/)Importing \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} assets will perform a version compatibility check and alert users about mismatches in editor mode.
\item {\ttfamily USpine\+Skeleton\+Renderer\+Component} allows passing a {\ttfamily USpine\+Skeleton\+Component} to update it. This way, the renderer component can be used without a skeleton component on the same actor.
\item Added blueprint-\/callable methods to {\ttfamily Spine\+Skeleton\+Component} and {\ttfamily Spine\+Skeleton\+Animation\+Component} to query and set skins, and enumerate bones, slots, and animations.
\item Extended skeleton data editor preview. The preview now shows bones, slots, animations, and skins found in the skeleton data. See this \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/blog/Unreal-Engine-4-quality-of-life-improvements}{\texttt{ blog post}}.
\item Added preview animation and skin fields, allowing you to preview animations and skins right in the editor. See this \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/blog/Unreal-Engine-4-quality-of-life-improvements}{\texttt{ blog post}}.
\item Removed dependency on {\ttfamily RHI}, {\ttfamily Render\+Core}, and {\ttfamily Shader\+Core}.
\item Re-\/importing atlases and their textures now works consistently in all situations.
\item Added mix-\/and-\/match example to demonstrate the new Skin API.
\item Materials on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+Component} are now blueprint read and writeable. This allows setting dynamic material instances at runtime.
\item Added {\ttfamily Initial\+Skin} property to {\ttfamily USpine\+Widget}. This allows previewing different skins in the UMG Designer. Initial skins can still be overridden via blueprint events such as {\ttfamily On Initialized}.
\item {\ttfamily USpine\+Widget} will now report its own desired size based on the setup pose dimensions of the skeleton. This is used when selecting {\ttfamily Size to content} on a {\ttfamily USpine\+Widget} in the designer.
\item Updated example project to UE 5.\+2.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md865}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{C}{C}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md865}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Changed {\ttfamily Ik\+Constraint\+Data.\+Bones} type from {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_list}{List}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Bone\+Data\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} to {\ttfamily Exposed\+List\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Bone\+Data\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}}} for unification reasons. {\itshape Note\+: this modification will most likely not affect user code.}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Slot.\+Attachment\+Vertices} to {\ttfamily Slot.\+Deform}.
\item Changed the {\ttfamily .json} curve format and added more assumptions for omitted values, reducing the average size of JSON exports.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Skin.\+Add\+Attachment()} to {\ttfamily Skin.\+Set\+Attachment()}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Find\+Attachments\+For\+Slot(int slot\+Index, \doxylink{class_list}{List}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Attachment\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} attachments)} and {\ttfamily Find\+Names\+For\+Slot (int slot\+Index, \doxylink{class_list}{List}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}string\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} names)} and replaced it with {\ttfamily Skin.\+Get\+Attachments(int slot\+Index, \doxylink{class_list}{List}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Skin\+Entry\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} attachments)} which returns the combined {\ttfamily Skin\+Entry} object holding both name and attachment.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+Apply\+Deform()} and replaced it with {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+Deform\+Attachment}. The attachment set on this field is used to decide if a {\ttfamily Deform\+Timeline} should be applied to the attachment active on the slot to which the timeline is applied.
\item Removed {\ttfamily inherit\+Deform} field, getter, and setter from {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment}.
\item Changed {\ttfamily .skel} binary format, added a string table. References to strings in the data resolve to this string table, reducing storage size of binary files considerably.
\item Changed the {\ttfamily .json} and {\ttfamily .skel} file formats to accomodate the new feature and file size optimiations. Old projects must be exported with \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 3.\+8.\+20+ to be compatible with the 3.\+8 \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} runtimes.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily x} and {\ttfamily y} coordinates for setup pose AABB in {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data}.
\item Added support for rotated mesh region UVs.
\item Added skin-\/specific bones and constraints which are only updated if the skeleton\textquotesingle{}s current skin contains them.
\item Improved Skin API to make it easier to handle mix-\/and-\/match use cases.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin.\+Get\+Attachments()}. Returns all attachments in the skin.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin.\+Get\+Attachments(int slot\+Index, \doxylink{class_list}{List}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Skin\+Entry\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} attachments)}. Returns all attachements in the skin for the given slot index. This method replaces {\ttfamily Find\+Attachments\+For\+Slot} and {\ttfamily Find\+Names\+For\+Slot}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin.\+Add\+Skin(\+Skin skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin.\+Copy\+Skin(\+Skin skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin. {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment} are shallowly copied and will retain any parent mesh relationship. All other attachment types are deep copied.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Copy()} to all attachment type implementations. This lets you deep copy an attachment to modify it independently from the original, i.\+e. when programmatically changing texture coordinates or mesh vertices.
\item Added {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment.\+New\+Linked\+Mesh()}, creates a linked mesh linkted to either the original mesh, or the parent of the original mesh.
\item Added IK softness.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md866}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Unity}{Unity}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md866}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Officially supported Unity versions are 2017.\+1-\/2020.\+2}}.
\item {\bfseries{\doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} {\ttfamily .asmdef} files are again active by default}}. They have previously been deactivated to {\ttfamily .txt} extension which is now no longer necessary.
\item {\bfseries{Removed Pose\+Skeleton() and Pose\+With\+Animation()}} extension methods to prevent issues where animations are not mixed out. Problem was that these methods did not set Animation\+State, leaving incorrect state at e.\+g. attachments enabled at slots when starting subsequent animations. As a replacement you can use {\ttfamily Animation\+State.\+Clear\+Track(0);} followed by {\ttfamily var entry = Animation\+State.\+Set\+Animation(0, animation, loop); entry.\+Track\+Time = time} to achieve similar behaviour.
\item {\bfseries{The {\ttfamily Shadow alpha cutoff} shader parameter is now respecting slot-\/color alpha}} values at all \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} shaders. \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} fragment\textquotesingle{}s texture color alpha is multiplied with slot-\/color alpha before the result is tested against the {\ttfamily Shadow alpha cutoff} threshold.
\item {\bfseries{Removed redundant {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Get\+Clone()} and {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment.\+Get\+Linked\+Clone()} extension methods}}. Use methods {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Copy} and {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment.\+New\+Linked\+Mesh()} instead.
\item {\bfseries{Renamed extension method {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Get\+Clone(bool clone\+Meshes\+As\+Linked)} to {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Get\+Copy(bool clone\+Meshes\+As\+Linked)}}} to follow the naming scheme of the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} API.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\+Asset.\+atlas\+Assets} is now an array of the base class {\ttfamily Atlas\+Asset\+Base} instead of {\ttfamily Spine\+Atlas\+Asset}, which provides {\ttfamily IEnumerable\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} Materials} instead of {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_list}{List}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} materials}. Replace any access via {\ttfamily atlas\+Asset.\+materials\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}} with {\ttfamily atlas\+Asset.\+Materials.\+First()} and add a {\ttfamily using System.\+Linq;} statement.
\item {\bfseries{Changed {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment.\+Get\+Linked\+Mesh()} method signatures\+:}} removed optional parameters {\ttfamily bool inherit\+Deform = true, bool copy\+Original\+Properties = false}.
\item Changed namespace {\ttfamily Spine.\+Unity.\+Modules} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine_1_1_unity}{Spine.\+Unity}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_examples}{Spine.\+Unity.\+Examples}} after restructuring (see section below) in respective classes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item When receiving namespace related errors, replace using statements of {\ttfamily using Spine.\+Unity.\+Modules.\+Attachment\+Tools;} with {\ttfamily using \doxylink{namespace_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_attachment_tools}{Spine.\+Unity.\+Attachment\+Tools};}. You can remove {\ttfamily using Spine.\+Unity.\+Modules;} statements when a {\ttfamily using \doxylink{namespace_spine_1_1_unity}{Spine.\+Unity}} statement is already present in the file.
\item {\ttfamily Attachment\+Tools}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Parts\+Renderer}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Separator}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+Custom\+Materials} changed to namespace {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine_1_1_unity}{Spine.\+Unity}}.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Ghost}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Ghost\+Renderer}, {\ttfamily Atlas\+Region\+Attacher}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic\+Mirror}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Ragdoll}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Ragdoll2D}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Eye\+Constraint}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Ground\+Constraint}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Kinematic\+Shadow} changed to namespace {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_examples}{Spine.\+Unity.\+Examples}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Split {\ttfamily Editor/\+Utility/\+Spine\+Editor\+Utilities} class into multiple files with partial class qualifier.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Nested classes {\ttfamily Spine\+Editor\+Utilities.\+Asset\+Utility} and {\ttfamily Spine\+Editor\+Utilities.\+Editor\+Instantiation} are now no longer nested. If you receive namespace related errors, replace any occurrance of
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Spine\+Editor\+Utilities.\+Asset\+Utility} with {\ttfamily Asset\+Utility} and
\item {\ttfamily Spine\+Editor\+Utilities.\+Editor\+Instantiation} with {\ttfamily Editor\+Instantiation}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Timeline Support has been moved to a separate UPM Package}} Previously the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Timeline integration was located in the {\ttfamily Modules/\+Timeline} directory and was deactivated by default, making it necessary to activate it via the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Preferences. Now the Timeline integration has been moved to an additional UPM package which can be found under {\ttfamily Modules/com.\+esotericsoftware.\+spine.\+timeline}.
\item {\bfseries{Installation\+:}} You can download the Unity Package Manager (UPM) package via the \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity-download}{\texttt{ download page}} or find it in the \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/tree/3.8-beta/spine-unity/Modules}{\texttt{ spine-\/runtimes/spine-\/unity/\+Modules}} subdirectory on the git repository. You can then either unzip (copy if using git) the package to a) the {\ttfamily Packages} directory in your project where it will automatically be loaded, or b) to an arbitrary directory outside the Assets directory and then open Package Manager in Unity, select the {\ttfamily +} icon, choose {\ttfamily Add package from disk..} and point it to the package.\+json file. The Project panel should now show an entry {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Timeline Extensions} under {\ttfamily Packages}. If the directory is not yet listed, you will need to close and re-\/open Unity to have it display the directory and its contents.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim}\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Layer Mix \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode}} enum name {\ttfamily Mix\+Mode.\+Spine\+Style} has been renamed to {\ttfamily Mix\+Mode.\+Hard}. This is most likely not set via code and thus unlikely to be a problem. Serialized scenes and prefabs are unaffected.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Root\+Motion} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim\+Root\+Motion} components now support arbitrary bones in the hierarchy as {\ttfamily Root Motion Bone}. Previously there were problems when selecting a non-\/root bone as {\ttfamily Root Motion Bone}. {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+ScaleX} and {\ttfamily .ScaleY} and parent bone scale is now respected as well.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{\doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Preferences stored in Assets/\+Editor/\+Spine\+Settings.\+asset}} Now \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} uses the new {\ttfamily Settings\+Provider} API, storing settings in a Spine\+Settings.\+asset file which can be shared with team members. Your old preferences are automatically migrated to the new system.
\item Added support for Unity\textquotesingle{}s Sprite\+Mask to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim}. All mask interaction modes are supported. See this \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/blog/Unity-SpriteMask-and-RectMask2D-support}{\texttt{ blog post}}.
\item Added support for Unity\textquotesingle{}s Rect\+Mask2D to Skeleton\+Graphics. See this \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/blog/Unity-SpriteMask-and-RectMask2D-support}{\texttt{ blog post}}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Create 2D Hinge Chain} button at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Bone} inspector, previously only {\ttfamily Create 3D Hinge Chain} was available.
\item {\bfseries{Now supporting Lightweight Render Pipeline (LWRP) through an additional UPM package.}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Installation\+:}} You can download the Unity Package Manager (UPM) package via the \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity-download}{\texttt{ download page}} or find it in the \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/tree/3.8-beta/spine-unity/Modules}{\texttt{ spine-\/runtimes/spine-\/unity/\+Modules}} subdirectory on the git repository. You can then either unzip (copy if using git) the package to
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item a) the {\ttfamily Packages} directory in your project where it will automatically be loaded, or
\item b) to an arbitrary directory outside the Assets directory and then open Package Manager in Unity, select the {\ttfamily +} icon, choose {\ttfamily Add package from disk..} and point it to the package.\+json file.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} If you are using git and Unity 2019.\+2 or newer versions and receive an error that dependencies could not be resolved by the package manager (only higher versions of Unity\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Lightweight RP} package are available, e.\+g. {\ttfamily 6.\+9.\+0} and up), please copy the prepared package-\/\+UNITYVERSION.\+json file for your Unity version (e.\+g. {\ttfamily package-\/2019.\+2.\+json}) over the existing package.\+json file to change the dependency accordingly. Unfortunately Unity\textquotesingle{}s Package Manager does not provide a way to specify a version range for a dependency like "{}5.\+7.\+2 -\/ 6.\+9.\+0"{} yet, so this manual step is necessary for git users.

The Project panel should now show an entry {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Lightweight RP Shaders} under {\ttfamily Packages}. If the directory is not yet listed, you will need to close and re-\/open Unity to have it display the directory and its contents.
\item {\bfseries{Usage\+:}} The package provides two shaders specifically built for the lightweight render pipeline\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Lightweight Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton}, as a lightweight variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton} shader,
\item {\ttfamily Lightweight Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton Lit}, as a lightweight variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Lit} shader and
\item {\ttfamily Lightweight Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Sprite}, as a lightweight variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Sprite/\+Vertex Lit} and {\ttfamily Pixel Lit} shaders, which were not functioning in the lightweight render pipeline. The shaders can be assigned to materials as usual and will respect your settings of the assigned {\ttfamily Lightweight\+Render\+Pipeline\+Asset} under {\ttfamily Project Settings -\/ Graphics}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Restrictions}} As all \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} shaders, the LWRP shaders {\bfseries{do not support {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha} (PMA) atlas textures in Linear color space}}. Please export your atlas textures as {\ttfamily straight alpha} textures with disabled {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha} setting when using Linear color space. You can check the current color space via {\ttfamily Project Settings -\/ Player -\/ Other Settings -\/ \doxylink{external_2magic__enum_2example_2example_8cpp_a692f5062ca261bdb3a62a63faddfd27f}{Color} Space.}.
\item {\bfseries{Example\+:}} You can find an example scene in the package under {\ttfamily com.\+esotericsoftware.\+spine.\+lwrp-\/shaders-\/3.\+8/\+Examples/\+LWRP Shaders.\+unity} that demonstrates usage of the LWRP shaders.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Lit ZWrite} shader. This variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Lit} shader writes to the depth buffer with configurable depth alpha threshold. Apart from that it is identical to {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Lit}.
\item Additional yield instructions to wait for animation track events {\ttfamily End}, {\ttfamily Complete} and {\ttfamily Interrupt}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Wait\+For\+Spine\+Animation\+Complete} now proves an additional {\ttfamily bool include\+End\+Event} parameter, defaults to {\ttfamily false} (previous behaviour).
\item Added a new {\ttfamily Wait\+For\+Spine\+Animation\+End} yield instruction.
\item Added a new generic {\ttfamily Wait\+For\+Spine\+Animation} yield instruction which can be configured to wait for any combination of animation track events. It is now used as base class for {\ttfamily Wait\+For\+Spine\+Animation\+Complete} and {\ttfamily Wait\+For\+Spine\+Animation\+End}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Additional {\bfseries{Fix Draw Order}} parameter at Skeleton\+Renderer, defaults to {\ttfamily disabled} (previous behaviour). Applies only when 3+ submeshes are used (2+ materials with alternating order, e.\+g. "{}\+A B A"{}). If true, Material\+Property\+Blocks are assigned at each material to prevent aggressive batching of submeshes by e.\+g. the LWRP renderer, leading to incorrect draw order (e.\+g. "{}\+A1 B A2"{} changed to "{}\+A1\+A2 B"{}). You can leave this parameter disabled when everything is drawn correctly to save the additional performance cost.
\item {\bfseries{Additional Timeline features.}} Spine\+Animation\+State\+Clip now provides a {\ttfamily Speed Multiplier}, a start time offset parameter {\ttfamily Clip In}, support for blending successive animations by overlapping tracks. An additional {\ttfamily Use Blend Duration} parameter {\itshape (defaults to true)} allows for automatic synchronisation of Mix\+Duration with the current overlap blend duration. An additional \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} preferences parameter {\ttfamily Use Blend Duration} has been added which can be disabled to default to the previous behaviour before this update.
\item Additional {\ttfamily Sprite\+Mask and Rect\+Mask2D} example scene added for demonstration of mask setup and interaction.
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{boostmultiprec_8cpp_ad5abe8020ead32dcab5e3c15d6d7c30e}{Real} physics hinge chains} for both 2D and 3D physics. The \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#SkeletonUtilityBone}{\texttt{ Skeleton\+Utility\+Bone}} Inspector provides an interface to create 2D and 3D hinge chains. Previously created chains have only been respecting gravity, but not momentum of the skeleton or parent bones. The new physics rig created when pressing {\ttfamily Create 3D Hinge Chain} and {\ttfamily Create 2D Hinge Chain} creates a more complex setup that also works when flipping the skeleton. Note that the chain root node is no longer parented to bones of the skeleton. This is a requirement in Unity to have momentum applied properly -\/ do not reparent the chain root to bones of your skeleton, or you will loose any momentum applied by the skeleton\textquotesingle{}s movement.
\item {\ttfamily Outline rendering functionality for all shaders.} Every shader now provides an additional set of {\ttfamily Outline} parameters to enable custom outline rendering. When outline rendering is enabled via the {\ttfamily Material} inspector, it automatically switches the shader to the respective {\ttfamily Spine/\+Outline} shader variant. Outlines are generated by sampling neighbour pixels, so be sure to add enough transparent padding when exporting your atlas textures to fit the desired outline width. In order to enable outline rendering at a skeleton, it is recommended to first prepare an additional outline material copy and then switch the material of the target skeleton to this material. This prevents unnecessary additional runtime material copies and drawcalls. Material switching can be prepared via a \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#SkeletonRendererCustomMaterials}{\texttt{ Skeleton\+Renderer\+Custom\+Materials}} component and then enabled or disabled at runtime. Alternatively, you can also directly modify the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer.\+Custom\+Material\+Override} property. Outline rendering is fully supported on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} shaders as well.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer.\+Editor\+Skip\+Skin\+Sync} scripting API property to be able to set custom skins in editor scripts. Enable this property when overwriting the Skeleton\textquotesingle{}s skin from an editor script. Without setting this parameter, changes will be overwritten by the next inspector update. Only affects Inspector synchronisation of skin with {\ttfamily initial\+Skin\+Name}, not startup initialization.
\item All {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic} shaders now provide a parameter {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group Compatible} which can be enabled to support {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group} alpha blending. For correct results, you should then disable {\ttfamily Pma \doxylink{struct_vertex}{Vertex} Colors} in the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} Inspector, in section {\ttfamily Advanced} (otherwise \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot} alpha will be applied twice).
\item {\bfseries{Now supporting Universal Render Pipeline (URP), including the 2D Renderer pipeline, through an additional UPM package.}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Installation\+:}} You can download the Unity Package Manager (UPM) package via the \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity-download}{\texttt{ download page}} or find it in the \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/tree/3.8-beta/spine-unity/Modules}{\texttt{ spine-\/runtimes/spine-\/unity/\+Modules}} subdirectory on the git repository. You can then either unzip (copy if using git) the package to
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item a) the {\ttfamily Packages} directory in your project where it will automatically be loaded, or
\item b) to an arbitrary directory outside the Assets directory and then open Package Manager in Unity, select the {\ttfamily +} icon, choose {\ttfamily Add package from disk..} and point it to the package.\+json file.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The Project panel should now show an entry {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Universal RP Shaders} under {\ttfamily Packages}. If the directory is not yet listed, you will need to close and re-\/open Unity to have it display the directory and its contents.
\item {\bfseries{Usage\+:}} The package provides two shaders specifically built for the universal render pipeline\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton}, as a universal variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton} shader,
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Skeleton Lit}, as a universal variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Lit} shader,
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Sprite}, as a universal variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Sprite/\+Vertex Lit} and {\ttfamily Pixel Lit} shaders, which were not functioning in the universal render pipeline,
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/2\+D/\+Spine/\+Skeleton Lit}, as a universal 2D Renderer variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Lit} shader, and
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/2\+D/\+Spine/\+Sprite}, as a universal 2D Renderer variant of the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Sprite/\+Vertex Lit} and {\ttfamily Pixel Lit} shaders. The shaders can be assigned to materials as usual and will respect your settings of the assigned {\ttfamily Universal\+Render\+Pipeline\+Asset} under {\ttfamily Project Settings -\/ Graphics}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Restrictions}} As all \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} shaders, the URP shaders {\bfseries{do not support {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha} (PMA) atlas textures in Linear color space}}. Please export your atlas textures as {\ttfamily straight alpha} textures with disabled {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha} setting when using Linear color space. You can check the current color space via {\ttfamily Project Settings -\/ Player -\/ Other Settings -\/ \doxylink{external_2magic__enum_2example_2example_8cpp_a692f5062ca261bdb3a62a63faddfd27f}{Color} Space.}.
\item {\bfseries{Example\+:}} You can find an example scene in the package under {\ttfamily com.\+esotericsoftware.\+spine.\+urp-\/shaders-\/3.\+8/\+Examples/\+URP Shaders.\+unity} that demonstrates usage of the URP shaders.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Preferences now provide an {\bfseries{{\ttfamily Atlas Texture Settings}}} parameter for applying customizable texture import settings at all newly imported \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} atlas textures. When exporting atlas textures from \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} with {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha} enabled (the default), you can leave it at {\ttfamily PMATexture\+Preset}. If you have disabled {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha}, set it to the included {\ttfamily Straight\+Alpha\+Texture\+Preset} asset. You can also create your own {\ttfamily Texture\+Importer} {\ttfamily Preset} asset and assign it here (include {\ttfamily PMA} or {\ttfamily Straight} in the name). In Unity versions before 2018.\+3 you can use {\ttfamily Texture2D} template assets instead of the newer {\ttfamily Preset} assets. Materials created for imported textures will also have the {\ttfamily Straight Alpha Texture} parameter configured accordingly.
\item All {\ttfamily Sprite} shaders (including URP and LWRP extension packages) now provide an additional {\ttfamily Fixed Normal Space} option {\ttfamily World-\/\+Space}. PReviously options were limited to {\ttfamily View-\/\+Space} and {\ttfamily Model-\/\+Space}.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} now fully supports \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#SkeletonUtility}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility}}} for generating a hierarchy of \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#SkeletonUtilityBone}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Bones}}} in both modes {\ttfamily Follow} and {\ttfamily Override}. This also enables creating hinge chain physics rigs and using {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Constraints} such as {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Ground\+Constraint} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Eye\+Constraint} on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic}.
\item Added {\ttfamily On\+Mesh\+And\+Materials\+Updated} callback event to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic}. It is issued at the end of {\ttfamily Late\+Update}, before rendering.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton-\/\+Outline\+Only} single pass shader to LWRP and URP extension modules. It can be assigned to materials as {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Outline/\+Skeleton-\/\+Outline\+Only}. This allows for separate outline child {\itshape Game\+Objects} that reference the existing Mesh of their parent, and re-\/draw the mesh using this outline shader.
\item Added example component {\ttfamily Render\+Existing\+Mesh} to render a mesh again with different materials, as required by the new {\ttfamily Skeleton-\/\+Outline\+Only} shaders. In URP the outline has to be rendered via a separate Game\+Object as URP does not allow multiple render passes. To add an outline to your Skeleten\+Renderer\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Add a child Game\+Object and move it a bit back (e.\+g. position Z = 0.\+01).
\item Add a {\ttfamily Render\+Existing\+Mesh} component, provided in the {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Scripts/\+Sample Components} directory.
\item Copy the original material, add \+\_\+\+\_\+\+Outline\+\_\+ to its name and set the shader to {\ttfamily Universal Render Pipeline/\+Spine/\+Outline/\+Skeleton-\/\+Outline\+Only}.
\item Assign this \+\_\+\+\_\+\+Outline\+\_\+ material at the {\ttfamily Render\+Existing\+Mesh} component under {\itshape Replacement Materials}.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Added {\ttfamily Outline Shaders URP} example scene to URP extension module to demonstrate the above additions.
\item Added support for Unity\textquotesingle{}s \href{https://docs.unity3d.com/Manual/class-SpriteAtlas.html}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Sprite\+Atlas}}} as atlas provider (as an alternative to {\ttfamily .atlas.\+txt} and {\ttfamily .png} files) alongside a skeleton data file. There is now an additional {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Sprite\+Atlas Import} tool window accessible via {\ttfamily Window -\/ \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} -\/ Sprite\+Atlas Import}. Additional information can be found in a new section on the \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#Advanced---Using-Unity-SpriteAtlas-as-Atlas-Provider}{\texttt{ spine-\/unity documentation page}}.
\item Added support for {\bfseries{multiple atlas textures at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic}}}. You can enable this feature by enabling the parameter {\ttfamily Multiple Canvas\+Renders} in the {\ttfamily Advanced} section of the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} Inspector. This automatically creates the required number of child {\ttfamily Canvas\+Renderer} Game\+Objects for each required draw call (submesh).
\item Added support for {\bfseries{Render Separator Slots}} at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic}. Render separation can be enabled directly in the {\ttfamily Advanced} section of the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} Inspector, it does not require any additional components (like {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Separator} or {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Parts\+Renderer} for {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} components). When enabled, additional separator Game\+Objects will be created automatically for each separation part, and {\ttfamily Canvas\+Renderer} Game\+Objects re-\/parented to them accordingly. The separator Game\+Objects can be moved around and re-\/parented in the hierarchy according to your requirements to achieve the desired draw order within your {\ttfamily Canvas}. \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} usage example can be found in the updated {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Other Examples/\+Skeleton\+Render\+Separator} scene.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic\+Custom\+Materials} component, providing functionality to override materials and textures of a {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic}, similar to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+Custom\+Materials}. Note\+: overriding materials or textures per slot is not provided due to structural limitations.
\item Added {\bfseries{Root Motion support}} for {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} via new components {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Root\+Motion} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim\+Root\+Motion}. The {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} component Inspector now provides a line {\ttfamily Root Motion} with {\ttfamily Add Component} and {\ttfamily Remove Component} buttons to add/remove the new {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Root\+Motion} component to your Game\+Object. The {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} Inspector detects whether root motion is enabled at the {\ttfamily Animator} component and adds a {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim\+Root\+Motion} component automatically.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} now provides an additional {\ttfamily Custom Mix\+Mode} parameter under {\ttfamily Mecanim Translator}. It is enabled by default in version 3.\+8 to maintain current behaviour, using the set {\ttfamily Mix \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode}} for each Mecanim layer. When disabled, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} will use the recommended {\ttfamily Mix\+Mode} according to the layer blend mode. Additional information can be found in the \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#Parameters-for-animation-blending-control}{\texttt{ Mecanim Translator section}} on the spine-\/unity documentation pages.
\item Added {\bfseries{Skeleton\+Graphic Timeline support}}. Added supprot for multi-\/track Timeline preview in the Editor outside of play mode (multi-\/track scrubbing). See the \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/spine-unity\#Timeline-Extension-UPM-Package}{\texttt{ Timeline-\/\+Extension-\/\+UPM-\/\+Package}} section of the spine-\/unity documentation for more information.
\item Added support for double-\/sided lighting at all {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Lit} shaders (including URP and LWRP packages).
\item Added frustum culling update mode parameters {\ttfamily Update When Invisible} (Inspector parameter) and {\ttfamily Update\+Mode} (available via code) to all Skeleton components. This provides a simple way to disable certain updates when the {\ttfamily Renderer} is no longer visible (outside all cameras, culled in frustum culling). The new {\ttfamily Update\+Mode} property allows disabling updates at a finer granularity level than disabling the whole component. Available modes are\+: {\ttfamily Nothing}, {\ttfamily Only\+Animation\+Status}, {\ttfamily Everything\+Except\+Mesh} and {\ttfamily Full\+Update}.
\item Added a new {\ttfamily Spine/\+Outline/\+Outline\+Only-\/\+ZWrite} shader to provide correct outline-\/only rendering. Note\+: the shader requires two render passes and is therefore not compatible with URP. The {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Other Examples/\+Outline Shaders} example scene has been updated to demonstrate the new shader.
\item Added {\ttfamily On\+Mesh\+And\+Materials\+Updated} callback event to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Render\+Separator} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Parts\+Renderer}. It is issued at the end of {\ttfamily Late\+Update}, before rendering.
\item Added {\ttfamily Root Motion Scale X/Y} parameters to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Root\+Motion\+Base} subclasses ({\ttfamily Skeleton\+Root\+Motion} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim\+Root\+Motion}). Also providing {\ttfamily Adjust\+Root\+Motion\+To\+Distance()} and other methods to allow for easy delta compensation. Delta compensation can be used to e.\+g. stretch a jump to a given distance. Root motion can be adjusted at the start of an animation or every frame via {\ttfamily skeleton\+Root\+Motion.\+Adjust\+Root\+Motion\+To\+Distance(target\+Position -\/ transform.\+position, track\+Index);}.
\item Now providing a {\ttfamily Canvas Group Tint Black} parameter at the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} Inspector in the {\ttfamily Advanced} section. When using the {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic Tint Black} shader you can enable this parameter to receive proper blending results when using {\ttfamily Additive} blend mode under a {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group}. Be sure to also have the parameter {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group Compatible} enabled at the shader. Note that the normal {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic} does not support {\ttfamily Additive} blend mode at a {\ttfamily Canvas\+Group}, as it requires additional shader channels to work.
\item Added {\ttfamily Mix and Match Skins} example scene to demonstrate how the 3.\+8 Skin API and combining skins can be used for a wardrobe and equipment use case.
\item \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Timeline Extensions\+: Added {\ttfamily Hold Previous} parameter at {\ttfamily Spine\+Animation\+State\+Clip}.
\item Added more warning messages at incompatible Skeleton\+Renderer/\+Skeleton\+Graphic Component vs Material settings. They appear both as an info box in the Inspector as well as upon initialization in the Console log window. The Inspector box warnings can be disabled via {\ttfamily Edit -\/ Preferences -\/ \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine}}.
\item Now providing {\ttfamily Before\+Apply} update callbacks at all skeleton animation components ({\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic}).
\item Added {\ttfamily Bounding\+Box\+Follower\+Graphic} component. This class is a counterpart of {\ttfamily Bounding\+Box\+Follower} that can be used with {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic}.
\item Added Inspector context menu functions {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer -\/ Add all Bounding\+Box\+Follower Game\+Objects} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic -\/ Add all Bounding\+Box\+Follower\+Graphic Game\+Objects} that automatically generate bounding box follower Game\+Objects for every {\ttfamily Bounding\+Box\+Attachment} for all skins of a skeleton.
\item {\ttfamily Get\+Remapped\+Clone()} now provides an additional parameter {\ttfamily pivot\+Shifts\+Mesh\+UVCoords} for {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment} to prevent uv shifts at a non-\/central Sprite pivot. This parameter defaults to {\ttfamily true} to maintain previous behaviour.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} components now provide an additional update mode {\ttfamily Only Event Timelines} at the {\ttfamily Update When Invisible} property. This mode saves additional timeline updates compared to update mode {\ttfamily Everything Except Mesh}.
\item Now all URP (Universal Render Pipeline) and LWRP (Lightweight Render Pipeline) shaders support SRP (Scriptable Render Pipeline) batching. See \href{https://docs.unity3d.com/Manual/SRPBatcher.html}{\texttt{ Unity SRPBatcher documentation pages}} for additional information.
\item Sprite shaders now provide four {\ttfamily Diffuse Ramp} modes as an Inspector Material parameter\+: {\ttfamily Hard}, {\ttfamily Soft}, {\ttfamily Old Hard} and {\ttfamily Old Soft}. In spine-\/unity 3.\+8 it defaults to {\ttfamily Old Hard} to keep the behaviour of existing projects unchanged. From 4.\+0 on it defaults to {\ttfamily Hard} for newly created materials while existing ones remain unchanged. Note that {\ttfamily Old Hard} and {\ttfamily Old Soft} ramp versions were using only the right half of the ramp texture, and additionally multiplying the light intensity by 2, both leading to brighter lighting than without a ramp texture active. The new ramp modes {\ttfamily Hard} and {\ttfamily Soft} use the full ramp texture and do not modify light intensity, being consistent with lighting without a ramp texture active.
\item Added {\bfseries{native support for slot blend modes}} {\ttfamily Additive}, {\ttfamily Multiply} and {\ttfamily Screen} with automatic assignment at newly imported skeleton assets. {\ttfamily Blend\+Mode\+Material\+Assets} are now obsolete and replaced by the native properties at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\+Asset}. The {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\+Asset} Inspector provides a new {\ttfamily Blend Modes -\/ Upgrade} button to upgrade an obsolete {\ttfamily Blend\+Mode\+Material\+Asset} to the native blend modes properties. This upgrade will be performed automatically on imported and re-\/imported assets in Unity 2020.\+1 and newer to prevent reported {\ttfamily Blend\+Mode\+Material\+Asset} issues in these Unity versions. spine-\/unity 4.\+0 and newer will automatically perform this upgrade regardless of the Unity version.
\item {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower} and {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower\+Graphic} components now provide better support for following bones when the skeleton\textquotesingle{}s Transform is not the parent of the follower\textquotesingle{}s Transform. Previously e.\+g. rotating a common parent Transform did not lead to the desired result, as well as negatively scaling a skeleton\textquotesingle{}s Transform when it is not a parent of the follower\textquotesingle{}s Transform.
\item URP and LWRP {\ttfamily Sprite} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Lit} shaders no longer require {\ttfamily Advanced -\/ Add Normals} enabled to properly cast and receive shadows. It is recommended to disable {\ttfamily Add Normals} if normals are otherwise not needed.
\item Added an example component {\ttfamily Root\+Motion\+Delta\+Compensation} located in {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Scripts/\+Sample Components} which can be used for applying simple delta compensation. You can enable and disable the component to toggle delta compensation of the currently playing animation on and off.
\item Root motion delta compensation now allows to only adjust X or Y components instead of both. Adds two parameters to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Root\+Motion\+Base.\+Adjust\+Root\+Motion\+To\+Distance()} which default to adjusting both X and Y as before. The {\ttfamily Root\+Motion\+Delta\+Compensation} example component exposes these parameters as public attributes.
\item Root motion delta compensation now allows to also add translation root motion to e.\+g. adjust a horizontal jump upwards or downwards over time. This is necessary because a Y root motion of zero cannot be scaled to become non-\/zero.
\item {\ttfamily Attachment.\+Get\+Remapped\+Clone(\+Sprite)} method now provides an additional optional parameter {\ttfamily use\+Original\+Region\+Scale}. When set to {\ttfamily true}, the replaced attachment\textquotesingle{}s scale is used instead of the Sprite\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Pixel per Unity} setting, allowing for more consistent scaling. {\itshape Note\+:} When remapping Sprites, be sure to set the Sprite\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Mesh \doxylink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{Type}} to {\ttfamily Full Rect} and not {\ttfamily Tight}, otherwise the scale will be wrong.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Changes of default values}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim}\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Layer Mix \doxylink{monitors_8c_a46c8a310cf4c094f8c80e1cb8dc1f911}{Mode}} now defaults to {\ttfamily Mix\+Mode.\+Mix\+Next} instead of {\ttfamily Mix\+Mode.\+Mix\+Always}.
\item {\ttfamily Blend\+Mode\+Material\+Asset} and it\textquotesingle{}s instance {\ttfamily Default Blend\+Mode\+Materials.\+asset} now have {\ttfamily Apply Additive Material} set to {\ttfamily true} by default in order to apply all blend modes by default.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Deprecated}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Deprecated {\ttfamily Modules/\+Slot\+Blend\+Modes/\+Slot\+Blend\+Modes} component. Changed namespace from {\ttfamily Spine.\+Unity.\+Modules} to {\ttfamily Spine.\+Unity.\+Deprecated}. Moved to {\ttfamily Deprecated/\+Slot\+Blend\+Modes}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Restructuring (Non-\/\+Breaking)}}

Note\+: The following changes will most likely not affect users of the Spine-\/\+Unity runtime as the API remains unchanged and no references are invalidated.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Removed duplicates of {\ttfamily .cginc} files in {\ttfamily Modules/\+Shaders/\+Sprite} that were also present in the {\ttfamily Modules/\+Shaders/\+Sprite/\+CGIncludes} directory.
\item Moved shaders from {\ttfamily Modules/\+Shaders} to {\ttfamily Shaders} directory.
\item Moved shaders from {\ttfamily Modules/\+Skeleton\+Graphic/\+Shaders} to {\ttfamily Shaders/\+Skeleton\+Graphic}.
\item Renamed shader {\ttfamily Shaders/\+Spine-\/\+Skeleton\+Lit.\+shader} to {\ttfamily Shaders/\+Spine-\/\+Skeleton-\/\+Lit.\+shader}.
\item Moved components from {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} to {\ttfamily Components} and {\ttfamily Components/\+Following} except for {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic\+Mirror} which was moved to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Scripts/\+Sample Components}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower}, {\ttfamily Bone\+Follower\+Graphic} and {\ttfamily Point\+Follower} from {\ttfamily Components} directory to {\ttfamily Components/\+Following}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily Bounding\+Box\+Follower} component from {\ttfamily Modules/\+Bounding\+Box\+Follower} to {\ttfamily Components/\+Following}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily Modules/\+Skeleton\+Render\+Separator} directory to {\ttfamily Components/\+Skeleton\+Render\+Separator}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily Modules/\+Custom\+Materials} directory to {\ttfamily Components/\+Skeleton\+Renderer\+Custom\+Materials}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily Asset Types/\+Blend\+Mode\+Materials\+Asset.\+cs} class, {\ttfamily Shaders/\+Blend\+Modes/\+Default Blend\+Mode\+Materials.\+asset} and materials from {\ttfamily Shaders/\+Blend\+Modes} to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data\+Modifier\+Assets/\+Blend\+Mode\+Materials} directory.
\item Moved {\ttfamily Modules/\+Ghost} directory to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Scripts/\+Sample Components/\+Ghost}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily Modules/\+Skeleton\+Utility Modules} directory to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Scripts/\+Sample Components/\+Skeleton\+Utility Modules}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily Modules/\+Animation\+Match\+Modifier} directory to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Scripts/\+Mecanim\+Animation\+Match\+Modifier}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Ragdoll} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Ragdoll2D} components from {\ttfamily Modules/\+Ragdoll} directory to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Examples/\+Scripts/\+Sample Components/\+Skeleton\+Utility Modules}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily Attachment\+Tools.\+cs} to {\ttfamily Utility} directory.
\item Split the file {\ttfamily Attachment\+Tools} into 5 separate files for each contained class. No namespace or other API changes performed.
\item Split the file {\ttfamily Mesh Generation/\+Spine\+Mesh} into 4 separate files for each contained class. No namespace or other API changes performed.
\item Moved {\ttfamily \doxylink{_skeleton_extensions_8cs}{Skeleton\+Extensions.\+cs}} to {\ttfamily Utility} directory.
\item Moved {\ttfamily Modules/\+Yield\+Instructions} directory to {\ttfamily Utility/\+Yield\+Instructions}.
\item Moved corresponding editor scripts of the above components to restructured directories as well.
\item Renamed inspector editor class {\ttfamily Point\+Follower\+Editor} to {\ttfamily Point\+Follower\+Inspector} for consistency reasons.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md867}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XNA/\+Mono\+Game}{XNA/\+Mono\+Game}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md867}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Updated to latest Mono\+Game version 3.\+7.\+1
\item Rewrote example project to be cleaner and better demonstrate basic \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} features.
\item Added mix-\/and-\/match example to demonstrate the new Skin API.
\item Added normalmap support via {\ttfamily Spine\+Effect\+Normalmap} and support for loading multiple texture layers following a suffix-\/pattern. Please see the example code on how to use them.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md868}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Java}{Java}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md868}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}\#get\+Attachment\+Vertices()} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}\#get\+Deform()}.
\item Changed the {\ttfamily .json} curve format and added more assumptions for omitted values, reducing the average size of JSON exports.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Skin\#add\+Attachment()} to {\ttfamily Skin\#set\+Attachment()}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\#apply\+Deform()} and replaced it with {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\#deform\+Attachment}. The attachment set on this field is used to decide if a {\ttfamily Deform\+Timeline} should be applied to the attachment active on the slot to which the timeline is applied.
\item Removed {\ttfamily inherit\+Deform} field, getter, and setter from {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment}.
\item Changed {\ttfamily .skel} binary format, added a string table. References to strings in the data resolve to this string table, reducing storage size of binary files considerably.
\item {\ttfamily Json\+Rollback} tool now converts from 3.\+8 JSON to 3.\+7.
\item Changed the {\ttfamily .json} and {\ttfamily .skel} file formats to accomodate the new feature and file size optimiations. Old projects must be exported with \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 3.\+8.\+20+ to be compatible with the 3.\+8 \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} runtimes.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily x} and {\ttfamily y} coordinates for setup pose AABB in {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data}.
\item Added support for rotated mesh region UVs.
\item Added skin-\/specific bones and constraints which are only updated if the skeleton\textquotesingle{}s current skin contains them.
\item Improved Skin API to make it easier to handle mix-\/and-\/match use cases.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#get\+Attachments()}. Returns all attachments in the skin.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#get\+Attachments(int slot\+Index)}. Returns all attachements in the skin for the given slot index.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#add\+Skin(\+Skin skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#copy\+Skin(\+Skin skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin. {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment} are shallowly copied and will retain any parent mesh relationship. All other attachment types are deep copied.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Attachment\#\doxylink{level1__impl_8h_a7ffc26122ca6f9bec01f9bc5e64f3006}{copy()}} to all attachment type implementations. This lets you deep copy an attachment to modify it independently from the original, i.\+e. when programmatically changing texture coordinates or mesh vertices.
\item Added {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment\#new\+Linked\+Mesh()}, creates a linked mesh linkted to either the original mesh, or the parent of the original mesh.
\item Added IK softness.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md869}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lib\+GDX}{lib\+GDX}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md869}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Viewer} can load a skeleton by specifying it as the first argument on the command line.
\item Added mix-\/and-\/match example to demonstrate the new Skin API.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md870}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Lua}{Lua}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md870}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item Added mix-\/and-\/match example to demonstrate the new Skin API.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md872}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Corona}{Corona}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md872}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
