\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md873}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Typescript/\+Javascript}{Typescript/\+Javascript}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md873}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Mix\+Direction.\+in/out} to {\ttfamily Mix\+Direction.\+mix\+In/mix\+Out} as it was crashing a JS compressor.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}\#get\+Attachment\+Vertices()} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}\#get\+Deform()}.
\item Changed the {\ttfamily .json} curve format and added more assumptions for omitted values, reducing the average size of JSON exports.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily Skin\#add\+Attachment()} to {\ttfamily Skin\#set\+Attachment()}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\#apply\+Deform()} and replaced it with {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\#deform\+Attachment}. The attachment set on this field is used to decide if a {\ttfamily Deform\+Timeline} should be applied to the attachment active on the slot to which the timeline is applied.
\item Removed {\ttfamily inherit\+Deform} field, getter, and setter from {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment}.
\item Changed {\ttfamily .skel} binary format, added a string table. References to strings in the data resolve to this string table, reducing storage size of binary files considerably.
\item Changed the {\ttfamily .json} and {\ttfamily .skel} file formats to accomodate the new feature and file size optimiations. Old projects must be exported with \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 3.\+8.\+20+ to be compatible with the 3.\+8 \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} runtimes.
\item Updated runtime to be compatible with Type\+Script 3.\+6.\+3.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for loading binary data via {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager\#load\+Binary()}. {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager\#\doxylink{stdlist__overload_8cpp_a120a90058439faee14791b33f94c0693}{get()}} will return a {\ttfamily Uint8\+Array} for such assets.
\item Added support for loading binaries via new {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Binary}. Parses a {\ttfamily Uint8\+Array}.
\item Added {\ttfamily x} and {\ttfamily y} coordinates for setup pose AABB in {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data}.
\item Added support for rotated mesh region UVs.
\item Added skin-\/specific bones and constraints which are only updated if the skeleton\textquotesingle{}s current skin contains them.
\item Improved Skin API to make it easier to handle mix-\/and-\/match use cases.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#get\+Attachments()}. Returns all attachments in the skin.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#get\+Attachments(slot\+Index\+: number)}. Returns all attachements in the skin for the given slot index.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#add\+Skin(skin\+: Skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skin\#copy\+Skin(skin\+: Skin)}. Adds all attachments, bones, and skins from the specified skin to this skin. {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment} are shallowly copied and will retain any parent mesh relationship. All other attachment types are deep copied.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Attachment\#\doxylink{level1__impl_8h_a7ffc26122ca6f9bec01f9bc5e64f3006}{copy()}} to all attachment type implementations. This lets you deep copy an attachment to modify it independently from the original, i.\+e. when programmatically changing texture coordinates or mesh vertices.
\item Added {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment\#new\+Linked\+Mesh()}, creates a linked mesh linkted to either the original mesh, or the parent of the original mesh.
\item Added IK softness.
\item Added {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager.\+set\+Raw\+Data\+URI(path, data)}. Allows to embed data URIs for skeletons, atlases and atlas page images directly in the HTML/\+JS without needing to load it from a separate file.
\item Added {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager.\+load\+All()} to allow Promise/async/await based waiting for completion of asset load. See the {\ttfamily spine-\/canvas} examples.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+get\+Bound\+Rect()} helper method to calculate the bouding rectangle of the current pose, returning the result as {\ttfamily \{ x, y, width, height \}}. Note that this method will create temporary objects which can add to garbage collection pressure.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md874}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Web\+GL backend}{Web\+GL backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md874}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_input}{Input}} can now take a partially defined implementation of {\ttfamily Input\+Listener}.
\item Added mix-\/and-\/match example to demonstrate the new Skin API.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md875}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Canvas backend}{Canvas backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md875}
\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md876}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Three.\+js backend}{Three.\+js backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md876}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mesh} now takes an optional {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mesh\+Material\+Parameters\+Customizer} function that allows you to modify the {\ttfamily Shader\+Material\+Parameters} before the material is finalized. Use it to modify things like THREEJS\textquotesingle{} {\ttfamily Material.\+depth\+Test} etc. See \#1590.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md877}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Player}{Player}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md877}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\#set\+Animation()} can now be called directly to set the animation being displayed.
\item The player supports loading {\ttfamily .skel} binary skeleton files by setting the {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\+Config\#skel\+Url} field instead of {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\+Config\#json\+Url}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Spine\+Player\+Config\#raw\+Data\+URIs}. Allows to embed data URIs for skeletons, atlases and atlas page images directly in the HTML/\+JS without needing to load it from a separate file. See the example for a demonstration.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md878}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{3.\+7}{3.\+7}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md878}
\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md879}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{AS3}{AS3}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md879}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The completion event will fire for looped 0 duration animations every frame.
\item {\ttfamily Mix\+Pose} is now called {\ttfamily Mix\+Blend}
\item Skeleton {\ttfamily flip\+X/flipY} has been replaced with {\ttfamily scale\+X/scaleY}. This cleans up applying transforms and is more powerful. Allows scaling a whole skeleton which has bones that disallow scale inheritance
\item Mix time is no longer affected by {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#time\+Scale}. See \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/issues/1194}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/issues/1194}}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added additive animation blending. When playing back multiple animations on different tracks, where each animation modifies the same skeleton property, the results of tracks with lower indices are discarded, and only the result from the track with the highest index is used. With animation blending, the results of all tracks are mixed together. This allows effects like mixing multiple facial expressions (angry, happy, sad) with percentage mixes. By default the old behaviour is retained (results from lower tracks are discarded). To enable additive blending across animation tracks, call {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#set\+Mix\+Blend(Mix\+Blend.\+add)} on each track. To specify the blend percentage, set {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#alpha}. See \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/forum/morph-target-track-animation-mix-mode-9459}{\texttt{ http\+://esotericsoftware.\+com/forum/morph-\/target-\/track-\/animation-\/mix-\/mode-\/9459}} for a discussion.
\item Support for stretchy IK
\item Support for audio events, see {\ttfamily audio\+Path}, {\ttfamily volume} and {\ttfamily balance} fields on event (data).
\item {\ttfamily Track\+Entry} has an additional field called {\ttfamily hold\+Previous}. It can be used to counter act a limitation of {\ttfamily Animation\+State} resulting in "{}dipping"{} of parts of the animation. For a full discussion of the problem and the solution we\textquotesingle{}ve implemented, see this \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/forum/Probably-Easy-Animation-mixing-with-multiple-tracks-10682?p=48130&hilit=holdprevious\#p48130}{\texttt{ forum thread}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md880}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Starling}{Starling}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md880}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for vertex effects. See {\ttfamily Raptor\+Example.\+as}
\item Added \textquotesingle{}get\+Texture()\textquotesingle{} method to \textquotesingle{}Starling\+Texture\+Atlas\+Attachment\+Loader\textquotesingle{}
\item Breaking change\+: if a skeleton requires two color tinting, you have to enable it via {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Sprite.\+two\+Color\+Tint = true}. In this case the skeleton will use the {\ttfamily Two\+Color\+Mesh\+Style}, which internally uses a different vertex layout and shader. This means that skeletons with two color tinting enabled will break batching and hence increase the number of draw calls in your app.
\item Added {\ttfamily Vertex\+Effect} and implementations {\ttfamily Jitter\+Effect} and {\ttfamily Swirl\+Effect}. Allows you to modify vertices before they are submitted for drawing. See Starling changes.
\item Fix issues with Starling\+Atlas\+Attachment\+Loader, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/issues/939}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/issues/939}}
\item Fix issues with region trimming support, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/262bc26c64d4111002d80e201cb1a3345e6727df}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/262bc26c64d4111002d80e201cb1a3345e6727df}}
\item Added support for overriding {\ttfamily Starling\+Atlas\+Attachment\+Loader\#get\+Texture()}, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/ea7dbecb98edc74e439aa9ef90dcf6eed865f718}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/ea7dbecb98edc74e439aa9ef90dcf6eed865f718}}
\item Texture atlas operations are no longer handled in {\ttfamily Starling\#new\+Region\+Attachment} and {\ttfamily Starling\#new\+Mesh\+Attachment} but delegated to the atlas.
\item Added sample for additive animation blending, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/blob/6a556de01429878df47bb276a97959a8bdbbe32f/spine-starling/spine-starling-example/src/spine/examples/OwlExample.as}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/blob/6a556de01429878df47bb276a97959a8bdbbe32f/spine-\/starling/spine-\/starling-\/example/src/spine/examples/\+Owl\+Example.\+as}}
\item Added sample on how to use bounding box attachment vertices \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/e20428b02699226164fa73ba4b12f7d029ae6f4d}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/e20428b02699226164fa73ba4b12f7d029ae6f4d}}
\item Fully transparent meshes are not submitted for rendering.
\item No hit-\/tests are performed when a skeleton is invisible.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md881}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{C}{C}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md881}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Listeners on {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_animation_state}{sp\+Animation\+State}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_track_entry}{sp\+Track\+Entry}} will now also be called if a track entry gets disposed as part of disposing an animation state.
\item The completion event will fire for looped 0 duration animations every frame.
\item The spine-\/cocos2dx and spine-\/ue4 runtimes are now based on spine-\/cpp. See below for changes.
\item Skeleton {\ttfamily flip\+X/flipY} has been replaced with {\ttfamily scale\+X/scaleY}. This cleans up applying transforms and is more powerful. Allows scaling a whole skeleton which has bones that disallow scale inheritance
\item Mix time is no longer affected by {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#time\+Scale}. See \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/issues/1194}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/issues/1194}}
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_mesh_attachment}{sp\+Mesh\+Attachment}} has two new fields {\ttfamily region\+Texture\+With} and {\ttfamily region\+Texture\+Height}. These must be set in custom attachment loader. See {\ttfamily Atlas\+Attachment\+Loader}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for local and relative transform constraint calculation, including additional fields in {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_transform_constraint_data}{sp\+Transform\+Constraint\+Data}}.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\#apply} and {\ttfamily Timeline\#apply}{\ttfamily now take enums}Mix\+Pose{\ttfamily and}Mix\+Direction{\ttfamily instead of booleans}
\item {\ttfamily Added}sp\+Vertex\+Effect{\ttfamily and corresponding implementations}sp\+Jitter\+Vertex\+Effect{\ttfamily and}sp\+Swirl\+Vertex\+Effect{\ttfamily . Create/dispose through the corresponding}sp\+XXXVertex\+Effect\+\_\+create()/dispose(){\ttfamily functions. Set on framework/engine specific renderer.}
\item {\ttfamily Functions in}extension.\+h{\ttfamily are not prefixed with}\+\_\+sp{\ttfamily instead of just}\+\_\+{\ttfamily to avoid interference with other libraries.}
\item {\ttfamily Introduced}SP\+\_\+\+API{\ttfamily macro. Every spine-\/c function is prefixed with this macro. By default, it is an empty string. Can be used to markup spine-\/c functions with e.\+g.}{\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+declspec} when compiling to a dll or linking to that dll.
\item Added {\ttfamily void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}user\+Data} to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_animation_state}{sp\+Animation\+State}}to be consumed in callbacks.
\item Added additive animation blending. When playing back multiple animations on different tracks, where each animation modifies the same skeleton property, the results of tracks with lower indices are discarded, and only the result from the track with the highest index is used. With animation blending, the results of all tracks are mixed together. This allows effects like mixing multiple facial expressions (angry, happy, sad) with percentage mixes. By default the old behaviour is retained (results from lower tracks are discarded). To enable additive blending across animation tracks, call {\ttfamily sp\+Track\+Entry-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}mix\+Blend = SP\+\_\+\+MIXBLEND\+\_\+\+ADD)} on each track. To specify the blend percentage, set {\ttfamily sp\+Track\+Entry-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}alpha}. See \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/forum/morph-target-track-animation-mix-mode-9459}{\texttt{ http\+://esotericsoftware.\+com/forum/morph-\/target-\/track-\/animation-\/mix-\/mode-\/9459}} for a discussion.
\item Optimized attachment lookup to give a 40x speed-\/up. See \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/cab81276263890b65d07fa2329ace16db1e365ff}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/cab81276263890b65d07fa2329ace16db1e365ff}}
\item Support for stretchy IK
\item Support for audio events, see {\ttfamily audio\+Path}, {\ttfamily volume} and {\ttfamily balance} fields on event (data).
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_track_entry}{sp\+Track\+Entry}} has an additional field called {\ttfamily hold\+Previous}. It can be used to counter act a limitation of {\ttfamily Animation\+State} resulting in "{}dipping"{} of parts of the animation. For a full discussion of the problem and the solution we\textquotesingle{}ve implemented, see this \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/forum/Probably-Easy-Animation-mixing-with-multiple-tracks-10682?p=48130&hilit=holdprevious\#p48130}{\texttt{ forum thread}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md882}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cocos2d-\/\+Objc}{Cocos2d-\/\+Objc}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md882}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added vertex effect support to modify vertices of skeletons on the CPU. See {\ttfamily Raptor\+Example.\+m}.
\item Explanation how to handle ARC, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/a4f122b08c5e2a51d6aad6fc5a947f7ec31f2eb8}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/a4f122b08c5e2a51d6aad6fc5a947f7ec31f2eb8}}
\item The super class {\ttfamily \+::update()} method of {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} is now called, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/f7bb98185236a6d8f35bfefc70afe4f31e9ec9d2}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/f7bb98185236a6d8f35bfefc70afe4f31e9ec9d2}}
\item Added improved tint-\/black shader.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md883}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SFML}{SFML}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md883}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily spine-\/sfml.\+h} no longer defines {\ttfamily SPINE\+\_\+\+SHORT\+\_\+\+NAMES} to avoid collisions with other APIs. See \#1058.
\item Added support for vertex effects. See raptor example.
\item Added premultiplied alpha support to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Drawable}. Use {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Drawable\+::set\+Use\+Premultiplied\+Alpha()}, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/34086c1f41415309b2ecce86055f6656fcba2950}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/34086c1f41415309b2ecce86055f6656fcba2950}}
\item Added additive animation blending sample, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/blob/b7e712d3ca1d6be3ebcfe3254dc2cea9c44dda71/spine-sfml/example/main.cpp\#L369}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/blob/b7e712d3ca1d6be3ebcfe3254dc2cea9c44dda71/spine-\/sfml/example/main.\+cpp\#\+L369}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md884}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{C++}{C++}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md884}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Additions \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added C++ \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} runtime. See the \href{https://esotericsoftware.com/spine-cpp}{\texttt{ spine-\/cpp Runtime Guide}} for more information on spine-\/cpp.
\item Added parsing of non-\/essential data (fps, images path, audio path) to for {\ttfamily .json}/{\ttfamily .skel} parsers.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md885}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cocos2d-\/x}{Cocos2d-\/x}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md885}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added ETC1 alpha support, thanks @halx99! Does not work when two color tint is enabled.
\item Added {\ttfamily sp\+Atlas\+Page\+\_\+set\+Custom\+Texture\+Loader()} which let\textquotesingle{}s you do texture loading manually. Thanks @jareguo.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+:set\+Slots\+Range()} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+::create\+With\+Skeleton()}. This allows you to split rendering of a skeleton up into multiple parts, and render other nodes in between. See {\ttfamily \doxylink{_skeleton_renderer_separator_example_8cpp}{Skeleton\+Renderer\+Separator\+Example.\+cpp}} for an example.
\item Fully transparent attachments will not be rendered, improving rendering performance.
\item Added improved tint-\/black shader.
\item Updated to cocos2d-\/x 3.\+16
\item The skeleton setup pose and world transform are now calculated on initialization to avoid flickering on start-\/up.
\item Updated to cocos2d-\/x 3.\+17.\+1
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change}}\+: Switched from \mbox{[}spine-\/c\mbox{]}(spine-\/c) to \mbox{[}spine-\/cpp\mbox{]}(spine-\/cpp) as the underlying \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} runtime. See the \href{https://esotericsoftware.com/spine-cpp}{\texttt{ spine-\/cpp Runtime Guide}} for more information on spine-\/cpp.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Cocos2d\+Attachment\+Loader} to be used when constructing an {\ttfamily Atlas}. Used by default by {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} when creating instances via the {\ttfamily create\+XXX} methods.
\item All C structs and enums {\ttfamily sp\+XXX} have been replaced with their C++ equivalents {\ttfamily spine\+::\+XXX} in all public interfaces.
\item All instantiations via {\ttfamily new} of C++ classes from spine-\/cpp should contain {\ttfamily (\+\_\+\+\_\+\+FILE\+\_\+\+\_\+, \+\_\+\+\_\+\+LINE\+\_\+\+\_\+)}. This allows the tracking of instantations and detection of memory leaks via the {\ttfamily \doxylink{classspine_1_1_debug_extension}{spine\+::\+Debug\+Extension}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md886}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SFML}{SFML}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md886}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Create a second SFML backend using \href{spine-cpp/}{\texttt{ spine-\/cpp}}. See the \href{https://esotericsoftware.com/spine-cpp}{\texttt{ spine-\/cpp Runtime Guide}} for more information on spine-\/cpp.
\item Added support for vertex effects. See raptor example.
\item Added premultiplied alpha support to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Drawable}. Use {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Drawable\+::set\+Use\+Premultiplied\+Alpha()}, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/34086c1f41415309b2ecce86055f6656fcba2950}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/34086c1f41415309b2ecce86055f6656fcba2950}}
\item Added additive animation blending sample, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/blob/b7e712d3ca1d6be3ebcfe3254dc2cea9c44dda71/spine-sfml/example/main.cpp\#L369}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/blob/b7e712d3ca1d6be3ebcfe3254dc2cea9c44dda71/spine-\/sfml/example/main.\+cpp\#\+L369}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md887}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UE4}{UE4}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md887}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item spine-\/c is now exposed from the plugin shared library on Windows via \+\_\+\+\_\+declspec.
\item Updated to Unreal Engine 4.\+18
\item Added C++ example, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/15011e81b7061495dba45e28b4d3f4efb10d7f40}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/15011e81b7061495dba45e28b4d3f4efb10d7f40}}
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+Component} generates collision meshes by default.
\item Disabled generation of collision meshes by {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+Component}. Both {\ttfamily Procedural\+Mesh\+Component} and {\ttfamily Runtime\+Mesh\+Component} have a bug that generates a new PhysiX file every frame per component. Users are advised to add a separate collision shape to the root scene component of an actor instead.
\item Using UE4 {\ttfamily FMemory} allocator by default. This should fix issues on some consoles.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change}} moved away from {\ttfamily Runtime\+Mesh\+Component}, as its maintainance has seized, back to {\ttfamily Procedural\+Mesh\+Component}. Existing projects should just work. However, if you run into issues, you may have to remove the old {\ttfamily Spine\+Skeleton\+Renderer\+Component} and add a new one to your existing actors.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change}} due to the removal of {\ttfamily Runtime\+Mesh\+Component} and reversal to {\ttfamily Procedural\+Mesh\+Component}, two color tinting is currently not supported. {\ttfamily Procedural\+Mesh\+Component} does not support enough vertex attributes for us to encode the second color in the vertex stream. You can remove the {\ttfamily Runtime\+Mesh\+Component/} directory from your plugins directory and remove the component from any {\ttfamily build.\+cs} files that may reference it.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change}}\+: Switched from \mbox{[}spine-\/c\mbox{]}(spine-\/c) to \mbox{[}spine-\/cpp\mbox{]}(spine-\/cpp) as the underlying \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} runtime. See the \href{https://esotericsoftware.com/spine-cpp}{\texttt{ spine-\/cpp Runtime Guide}} for more information on spine-\/cpp.
\item All C structs and enums {\ttfamily sp\+XXX} have been replaced with their C++ equivalents {\ttfamily spine\+::\+XXX} in all public interfaces.
\item All instantiations via {\ttfamily new} of C++ classes from spine-\/cpp should contain {\ttfamily (\+\_\+\+\_\+\+FILE\+\_\+\+\_\+, \+\_\+\+\_\+\+LINE\+\_\+\+\_\+)}. This allows the tracking of instantations and detection of memory leaks via the {\ttfamily \doxylink{classspine_1_1_debug_extension}{spine\+::\+Debug\+Extension}}.
\item Updated to Unreal Engine 4.\+20 (samples require 4.\+17+), see the {\ttfamily spine-\/ue4/\+Plugins/\+Spine\+Plugin/\+Source/\+Spine\+Plugin/\+Spine\+Plugin.\+build.\+cs} file on how to compile in 4.\+20 with the latest UBT API changes.
\item Updated to Unreal Engine 4.\+21 (samples require 4.\+21).
\item {\bfseries{Breaking change}}\+: {\ttfamily UBone\+Driver\+Component} and {\ttfamily UBone\+Follower\+Component} are now {\ttfamily UScene\+Component} instead of {\ttfamily UActor\+Component}. They either update only themselves, or also the owning {\ttfamily UActor}, depending on whether the new flag {\ttfamily Use\+Component\+Transform} is set. See \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/pull/1175}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/pull/1175}}
\item Added query methods for slots, bones, skins and animations to {\ttfamily Spine\+Skeleton\+Component} and {\ttfamily UTrack\+Entry}. These allow you to query these objects by name in both C++ and blueprints.
\item Added {\ttfamily Preview Animation} and {\ttfamily Preview Skin} properties to {\ttfamily Spine\+Skeleton\+Animation\+Component}. Enter an animation or skin name to live-\/preview it in the editor. Enter an empty string to reset the animation or skin.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md888}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{C}{C}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md888}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The completion event will fire for looped 0 duration animations every frame.
\item Skeleton {\ttfamily flip\+X/flipY} has been replaced with {\ttfamily scale\+X/scaleY}. This cleans up applying transforms and is more powerful. Allows scaling a whole skeleton which has bones that disallow scale inheritance
\item Mix time is no longer affected by {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#time\+Scale}. See \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/issues/1194}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/issues/1194}}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added additive animation blending. When playing back multiple animations on different tracks, where each animation modifies the same skeleton property, the results of tracks with lower indices are discarded, and only the result from the track with the highest index is used. With animation blending, the results of all tracks are mixed together. This allows effects like mixing multiple facial expressions (angry, happy, sad) with percentage mixes. By default the old behaviour is retained (results from lower tracks are discarded). To enable additive blending across animation tracks, call {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#Mix\+Blend = Mix\+Blend.\+add} on each track. To specify the blend percentage, set {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#Alpha}. See \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/forum/morph-target-track-animation-mix-mode-9459}{\texttt{ http\+://esotericsoftware.\+com/forum/morph-\/target-\/track-\/animation-\/mix-\/mode-\/9459}} for a discussion.
\item Support for stretchy IK
\item Support for audio events, see {\ttfamily audio\+Path}, {\ttfamily volume} and {\ttfamily balance} fields on event (data).
\item {\ttfamily Track\+Entry} has an additional field called {\ttfamily hold\+Previous}. It can be used to counter act a limitation of {\ttfamily Animation\+State} resulting in "{}dipping"{} of parts of the animation. For a full discussion of the problem and the solution we\textquotesingle{}ve implemented, see this \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/forum/Probably-Easy-Animation-mixing-with-multiple-tracks-10682?p=48130&hilit=holdprevious\#p48130}{\texttt{ forum thread}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md889}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Unity}{Unity}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md889}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Runtime and Editor, and Assembly Definition}} Files and folders have been reorganized into "{}\+Runtime"{} and "{}\+Editor"{}. Each of these have an {\ttfamily .asmdef} file that defines these separately as their own assembly in Unity {\itshape (Note\+: \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} {\ttfamily .asmdef} files are currently deactivated to {\ttfamily .txt} extension, see below)}. For projects not using assembly definition, you may delete the {\ttfamily .asmdef} files. These assembly definitions will be ignored by older versions of Unity that don\textquotesingle{}t support it.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In this scheme, the entirety of the base spine-\/csharp runtime is inside the "{}\+Runtime"{} folder, to be compiled in the same assembly as spine-\/unity so they can continue to share internal members.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{\doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} {\ttfamily .asmdef} files are now deactivated (using {\ttfamily .txt} extension) by default}} This prevents problems when updating \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} through unitypackages, overwriting the Timeline reference entry in {\ttfamily spine-\/unity.\+asmdef} (added automatically when enabling Unity 2019 Timeline support, see {\ttfamily Timeline Support for Unity 2019}), causing compile errors. In case you want to enable the {\ttfamily .asmdef} files, rename the files\+: {\ttfamily Spine/\+Runtime/spine-\/unity.\+txt} to {\ttfamily Spine/\+Runtime/spine-\/unity.\+asmdef} and {\ttfamily Spine/\+Editor/spine-\/unity-\/editor.\+txt} to {\ttfamily Spine/\+Editor/spine-\/unity-\/editor.\+asmdef}.
\item {\bfseries{Skeleton\+Animator is now Skeleton\+Mecanim}} The Spine-\/\+Unity Mecanim-\/driven component {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animator} has been renamed {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim} to make it more autocomplete-\/friendly and more obvious at human-\/glance. The .meta files and guids should remain intact so existing projects and prefabs should not break. However, user code needs to be updated to use {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mecanim}.
\item {\bfseries{Spine\+Atlas\+Asset}} The existing {\ttfamily Atlas\+Asset} type has been renamed to {\ttfamily Spine\+Atlas\+Asset} to signify that it specifically uses a Spine/lib\+GDX atlas as its source. Serialization should be intact but user code will need to be updated to refer to existing atlases as {\ttfamily Spine\+Atlas\+Asset}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Atlas\+Asset\+Base}} {\ttfamily Spine\+Atlas\+Asset} now has an abstract base class called {\ttfamily Spine\+Atlas\+Asset}. This is the base class to derive when using alternate atlas sources. Existing Skeleton\+Data\+Asset field "{}atlas\+Assets"{} now have the "{}\+Atlas\+Asset\+Base"{} type. Serialization should be intact, but user code will need to be updated to refer to the atlas assets accordingly.
\item This change is in preparation for alternate atlas options such as Unity\textquotesingle{}s Sprite\+Atlas.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Optional Straight Alpha for shaders}} Spine-\/\+Unity\textquotesingle{}s included Unity shaders now have a {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+STRAIGHT\+\_\+\+ALPHA\+\_\+\+INPUT} shader\+\_\+feature, toggled as a checkbox in the Material\textquotesingle{}s inspector. This allows the Material to use a non-\/premultiplied alpha/straight alpha input texture.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The following shaders now have the "{}\+Straight Alpha Texture"{} checkbox when used on a material\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton}
\item {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Tint Black}
\item {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Lit}
\item {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Tint}
\item {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Fill}
\item {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic (Premultiply Alpha)} was renamed to {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic}
\item {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic Tint Black (Premultiply Alpha)} was renamed to {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic Tint Black}
\item {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton PMA Multiply}
\item {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton PMA Screen}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Dedicated straight alpha shaders were removed from the runtime.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Spine/\+Straight Alpha/\+Skeleton Fill}
\item {\ttfamily Spine/\+Straight Alpha/\+Skeleton Tint}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Detection of Incorrect Texture Settings}} Especially when atlas textures are exported with setting {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha} enabled, it is important to configure Unity\textquotesingle{}s texture import settings correctly. By default, you will now receive warnings where texture settings are expected to cause incorrect rendering.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The following rules apply\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily s\+RGB (\doxylink{external_2magic__enum_2example_2example_8cpp_a692f5062ca261bdb3a62a63faddfd27f}{Color} Texture)} shall be disabled when {\ttfamily Generate Mip Maps} is enabled, otherwise you will receive white border outlines.
\item {\ttfamily Alpha Is Transparency} shall be disabled on {\ttfamily Premultiply alpha} textures, otherwise you will receive light ghosting artifacts in transparent areas.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item These warnings can be disabled in {\ttfamily Edit -\/ Preferences -\/ \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Sprite Mask Support for all Included Shaders}} The {\ttfamily Skeleton Animation} and {\ttfamily Skeleton Mecanim} components now provide an additional {\ttfamily Mask Interaction} field in the Inspector, covering identical functionality as Unity\textquotesingle{}s built in {\ttfamily Sprite Renderer} component\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Mask Interaction} modes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily None} -\/ The sprite will not interact with the masking system. Default behavior.
\item {\ttfamily Visible Inside Mask} -\/ The sprite will be visible only in areas where a mask is present.
\item {\ttfamily Visible Outside Mask} -\/ The sprite will be visible only in areas where no mask is present.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Automatically Generated Materials} When switching {\ttfamily Mask Interaction} modes in the Inspector outside of Play mode, the required additional material assets are generated for the respective {\ttfamily Stencil Compare} parameters -\/ with file suffixes `'\+\_\+\+Inside\+Mask\textquotesingle{}{\ttfamily and}\textquotesingle{}\+\_\+\+Outside\+Mask\textquotesingle{}{\ttfamily , placed in the same folder as the original materials. By default all generated materials are kept as references by the}Skeleton Animation{\ttfamily component for switching at runtime. These materials can be managed and optimized via the}Skeleton\+Animation{\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}s}Advanced{\ttfamily section\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Using the
\end{DoxyItemize}}Clear{\ttfamily button you can clear the reference to unneeded materials,
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Using the
\end{DoxyItemize}}Delete{\ttfamily button the respective assets are deleted as well as references cleared. Note that other}Skeleton Animation{\ttfamily Game\+Objects might still reference the materials, so use with caution!
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item With the
\end{DoxyItemize}}Set{\ttfamily button you can again assign a link to the respective materials to prepare them for runtime use. If the materials were not present or have been deleted, they are generated again based on the default materials.}
\item {\ttfamily When switching}Mask Interaction{\ttfamily mode at runtime, the previously prepared materials are switched active automatically. When the respective materials have not been prepared, material copies of the default materials are created on the fly. Note that these materials are not shared between similar}Skeleton Animation{\ttfamily Game\+Objects, so it is recommended to use the generated material assets where possible.}
\item {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+Every shader now exposes the}Stencil Compare{\ttfamily parameter\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} for further customization. This way you have maximum flexibility to use custom mechanisms to switch materials at runtime if you should ever need more than the three materials generated by}Skeleton Animation{\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}s}Mask Interaction{\ttfamily parameter. Reference}Stencil Compare{\ttfamily values are\+: -\/}Compare\+Function.\+Disabled{\ttfamily for}Mask Interaction -\/ None{\ttfamily  -\/}Compare\+Function.\+Less\+Equal{\ttfamily for}Mask Interaction -\/ Visible Inside Mask{\ttfamily  -\/}Compare\+Function.\+Greater{\ttfamily for}Mask Interaction -\/ Visible Outside Mask{\ttfamily }
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+Rect\+Mask2D Support for Skeleton\+Graphic\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Both}Skeleton\+Graphic` shaders '{\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic}\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}{\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic Tint Black}\textquotesingle{} now respect masking areas defined via Unity\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Rect\+Mask2D} component.
\item {\bfseries{Timeline Support for Unity 2019}} using the existing Timeline components. By default, all \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Timeline components are deactivated in Unity 2019 and {\bfseries{can be activated via the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Preferences menu}}. This step became necessary because in Unity 2019, Timeline has been moved to a separate Package and is no longer included in the Unity core. Please visit {\ttfamily Edit -\/ Preferences -\/ \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine}} and at {\ttfamily Timeline Package Support} hit {\ttfamily Enable} to automatically perform all necessary steps to activate the Timeline components. This will automatically\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item download the Unity Timeline package
\item activate the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Timeline components by setting the compile definition {\ttfamily SPINE\+\_\+\+TIMELINE\+\_\+\+PACKAGE\+\_\+\+DOWNLOADED} for all platforms
\item modify the {\ttfamily spine-\/unity.\+asmdef} file by adding the reference to the Unity Timeline library.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Added {\ttfamily Create 2D Hinge Chain} functionality at {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Utility\+Bone} inspector, previously only {\ttfamily Create 3D Hinge Chain} was available.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md890}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XNA/\+Mono\+Game}{XNA/\+Mono\+Game}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md890}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for any {\ttfamily Effect} to be used by {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}
\item Added support for {\ttfamily IVertex\+Effect} to modify vertices of skeletons on the CPU. {\ttfamily IVertex\+Effect} instances can be set on the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}. See example project.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Debug\+Renderer}
\item Made {\ttfamily Mesh\+Batcher} of Skeleton\+Renderer accessible via a getter. Allows user to batch their own geometry together with skeleton meshes for maximum batching instead of using XNA Sprite\+Batcher.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md891}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Java}{Java}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md891}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Skeleton attachments\+: Moved update of attached skeleton out of lib\+GDX {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}, added overloaded method {\ttfamily Skeleton\#update\+World\+Transform(\+Bone)}, used for {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Attachment}. You now MUST call this new method with the bone of the parent skeleton to which the child skeleton is attached. See {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Attachment\+Test} for and example.
\item The completion event will fire for looped 0 duration animations every frame.
\item {\ttfamily Mix\+Pose} is now called {\ttfamily Mix\+Blend}.
\item Skeleton {\ttfamily flip\+X/flipY} has been replaced with {\ttfamily scale\+X/scaleY}. This cleans up applying transforms and is more powerful. Allows scaling a whole skeleton which has bones that disallow scale inheritance
\item Mix time is no longer affected by {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#time\+Scale}. See \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/issues/1194}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/issues/1194}}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Event\+Data\#audio\+Path} field. This field contains the file name of the audio file used for the event.
\item Added convenience method to add all attachments from one skin to another, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/a0b7bb6c445efdfac12b0cdee2057afa3eff3ead}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/a0b7bb6c445efdfac12b0cdee2057afa3eff3ead}}
\item Added additive animation blending. When playing back multiple animations on different tracks, where each animation modifies the same skeleton property, the results of tracks with lower indices are discarded, and only the result from the track with the highest index is used. With animation blending, the results of all tracks are mixed together. This allows effects like mixing multiple facial expressions (angry, happy, sad) with percentage mixes. By default the old behaviour is retained (results from lower tracks are discarded). To enable additive blending across animation tracks, call {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#set\+Mix\+Blend(Mix\+Blend.\+add)} on each track. To specify the blend percentage, set {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#alpha}. See \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/forum/morph-target-track-animation-mix-mode-9459}{\texttt{ http\+://esotericsoftware.\+com/forum/morph-\/target-\/track-\/animation-\/mix-\/mode-\/9459}} for a discussion.
\item Support for stretchy IK
\item Support for audio events, see {\ttfamily audio\+Path}, {\ttfamily volume} and {\ttfamily balance} fields on event (data).
\item {\ttfamily Track\+Entry} has an additional field called {\ttfamily hold\+Previous}. It can be used to counter act a limitation of {\ttfamily Animation\+State} resulting in "{}dipping"{} of parts of the animation. For a full discussion of the problem and the solution we\textquotesingle{}ve implemented, see this \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/forum/Probably-Easy-Animation-mixing-with-multiple-tracks-10682?p=48130&hilit=holdprevious\#p48130}{\texttt{ forum thread}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md892}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lib\+GDX}{lib\+GDX}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md892}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Vertex\+Effect} interface, instances of which can be set on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}. Allows to modify vertices before submitting them to GPU. See {\ttfamily Swirl\+Effect}, {\ttfamily Jitter\+Effect} and {\ttfamily Vertex\+Effect\+Test}.
\item Added improved tint-\/black shader.
\item Improved performance by avoiding batch flush when not switching between normal and additive rendering with PMA
\item Improvements to skeleton viewer.
\item {\ttfamily Two\+Color\+Polygon\+Batch} implements the {\ttfamily Batch} interface, allowing to the be used with other lib\+GDX classes that require a batcher for drawing, potentially improving performance. See \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/a46b3d1d0c135d51f9bef9ca17a5f8e5dda69927}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/a46b3d1d0c135d51f9bef9ca17a5f8e5dda69927}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Drawable} to render skeletons in scene2d UI \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/b93686c185e2c9d5466969a8e07eee573ebe4b97}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/b93686c185e2c9d5466969a8e07eee573ebe4b97}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md893}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Lua}{Lua}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md893}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}

When playing back multiple animations on different tracks, where each animation modifies the same skeleton property, the results of tracks with lower indices are discarded, and only the result from the track with the highest index is used.
