\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The completion event will fire for looped 0 duration animations every frame.
\item Skeleton {\ttfamily flip\+X/flipY} has been replaced with {\ttfamily scale\+X/scaleY}. This cleans up applying transforms and is more powerful. Allows scaling a whole skeleton which has bones that disallow scale inheritance
\item Mix time is no longer affected by {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#time\+Scale}. See \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/issues/1194}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/issues/1194}}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager.\+load\+Texture\+Atlas}. Instead of loading the {\ttfamily .atlas} and corresponding image files manually, you can simply specify the location of the {\ttfamily .atlas} file and Asset\+Manager will load the atlas and all its images automatically. {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager.\+get("{}atlasname.\+atlas"{})} will then return an instance of {\ttfamily spine.\+Texture\+Atlas}.
\item Added additive animation blending. When playing back multiple animations on different tracks, where each animation modifies the same skeleton property, the results of tracks with lower indices are discarded, and only the result from the track with the highest index is used. With animation blending, the results of all tracks are mixed together. This allows effects like mixing multiple facial expressions (angry, happy, sad) with percentage mixes. By default the old behaviour is retained (results from lower tracks are discarded). To enable additive blending across animation tracks, call {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#set\+Mix\+Blend(Mix\+Blend.\+add)} on each track. To specify the blend percentage, set {\ttfamily Track\+Entry\#alpha}. See \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/forum/morph-target-track-animation-mix-mode-9459}{\texttt{ http\+://esotericsoftware.\+com/forum/morph-\/target-\/track-\/animation-\/mix-\/mode-\/9459}} for a discussion. See \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/blob/f045d221836fa56191ccda73dd42ae884d4731b8/spine-ts/webgl/tests/test-additive-animation-blending.html}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/blob/f045d221836fa56191ccda73dd42ae884d4731b8/spine-\/ts/webgl/tests/test-\/additive-\/animation-\/blending.\+html}} for an example.
\item Added work-\/around for i\+OS Web\+Kit JIT bug, see \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/c28bbebf804980f55cdd773fed9ff145e0e7e76c}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Esoteric\+Software/spine-\/runtimes/commit/c28bbebf804980f55cdd773fed9ff145e0e7e76c}}
\item Support for stretchy IK
\item Support for audio events, see {\ttfamily audio\+Path}, {\ttfamily volume} and {\ttfamily balance} fields on event (data).
\item {\ttfamily Track\+Entry} has an additional field called {\ttfamily hold\+Previous}. It can be used to counter act a limitation of {\ttfamily Animation\+State} resulting in "{}dipping"{} of parts of the animation. For a full discussion of the problem and the solution we\textquotesingle{}ve implemented, see this \href{http://esotericsoftware.com/forum/Probably-Easy-Animation-mixing-with-multiple-tracks-10682?p=48130&hilit=holdprevious\#p48130}{\texttt{ forum thread}}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Asset\+Manager\#set\+Raw\+Data\+URI(path, data)}. Allows to set raw data URIs for a specific path, which in turn enables embedding assets into Java\+Script/\+HTML.
\item {\ttfamily Polygon\+Batcher} will now disable {\ttfamily CULL\+\_\+\+FACE} and restore the state as it was before rendering.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md897}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Web\+GL backend}{Web\+GL backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md897}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Vertex\+Effect} interface, instances of which can be set on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}. Allows to modify vertices before submitting them to GPU. See {\ttfamily Swirl\+Effect}, {\ttfamily Jitter\+Effect}, and the example which allows to set effects.
\item Added {\ttfamily slot\+Range\+Start} and {\ttfamily slot\+Range\+End} parameters to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\#draw} and {\ttfamily Scene\+Renderer\#draw\+Skeleton}. This allows you to render only a range of slots in the draw order. See {\ttfamily spine-\/ts/webgl/tests/test-\/slot-\/range.\+html} for an example.
\item Added improved tint-\/black shader.
\item Added {\ttfamily Scene\+Renderer\#draw\+Texture\+UV()}, allowing to draw a texture with manually specified texture coordinates.
\item Exposed all renderers in {\ttfamily Scene\+Renderer}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md898}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Canvas backend}{Canvas backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md898}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for shearing and non-\/uniform scaling inherited from parent bones.
\item Added support for alpha tinting.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md899}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Three.\+js backend}{Three.\+js backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md899}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Vertex\+Effect} interface, instances of which can be set on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mesh}. Allows to modify vertices before submitting them to GPU. See {\ttfamily Swirl\+Effect}, {\ttfamily Jitter\+Effect}.
\item Added support for multi-\/page atlases
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md900}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Widget backend}{Widget backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md900}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added fields {\ttfamily atlas\+Content}, {\ttfamily atlas\+Pages\+Content}, and {\ttfamily json\+Content} to {\ttfamily Widget\+Configuration} allowing you to directly pass the contents of the {\ttfamily .atlas}, atlas page {\ttfamily .png} files, and the {\ttfamily .json} file without having to do a request. See {\ttfamily README.\+md} and the example for details.
\item {\ttfamily Spine\+Widget.\+set\+Animation()} now takes an additional optional parameter for callbacks when animations are completed/interrupted/etc.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md901}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{3.\+6}{3.\+6}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md901}
\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md902}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{AS3}{AS3}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md902}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Removed {\ttfamily Bone.\+world\+To\+Local\+RotationX} and {\ttfamily Bone.\+world\+To\+Local\+RotationY}. Replaced by {\ttfamily Bone.\+world\+To\+Local\+Rotation} (rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item Made {\ttfamily Bone} fields {\ttfamily \+\_\+a}, {\ttfamily \+\_\+b}, {\ttfamily \+\_\+c}, {\ttfamily \+\_\+d}, {\ttfamily \+\_\+worldX} and {\ttfamily \+\_\+worldY} public, removed underscore prefix.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices} overload, changed {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices2} to {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices}, added {\ttfamily stride} parameter.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+vertices} field. The vertices array is provided to {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices} by the API user now.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+update\+World\+Vertices}, added {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices}. The new method now computes the x/y positions of the 4 vertices of the corner and places them in the provided {\ttfamily world\+Vertices} array, starting at {\ttfamily offset}, then moving by {\ttfamily stride} array elements when advancing to the next vertex. This allows to directly compose the vertex buffer and avoids a copy. The computation of the full vertices, including vertex colors and texture coordinates, is now done by the backend\textquotesingle{}s respective renderer.
\item Replaced {\ttfamily r}, {\ttfamily g}, {\ttfamily b}, {\ttfamily a} fields with instances of new {\ttfamily \doxylink{external_2magic__enum_2example_2example_8cpp_a692f5062ca261bdb3a62a63faddfd27f}{Color}} class in {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment}, {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment}, {\ttfamily Skeleton}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Data}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}} and {\ttfamily Slot\+Data}.
\item The completion event will fire for looped 0 duration animations every frame.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+get\+Bounds} from reference implementation.
\item Added support for local and relative transform constraint calculation, including additional fields in {\ttfamily Transform\+Constraint\+Data}
\item Added {\ttfamily Bone.\+local\+To\+World\+Rotation}(rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item Added two color tinting support, including {\ttfamily Two\+Color\+Timeline} and additional fields on {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}} and {\ttfamily Slot\+Data}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Point\+Attachment}, additional method {\ttfamily new\+Point\+Attachment} in {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader} interface.
\item Added {\ttfamily Clipping\+Attachment}, additional method {\ttfamily new\+Clipping\+Attachment} in {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader} interface.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\+State\#apply} returns boolean indicating if any timeline was applied or not.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\#apply} and {\ttfamily Timeline\#apply}{\ttfamily now take enums}Mix\+Pose{\ttfamily and}Mix\+Direction{\ttfamily instead of booleans}
\item {\ttfamily Added}Vertex\+Effect{\ttfamily and implementations}Jitter\+Effect{\ttfamily and}Swirl\+Effect\`{}. Allows you to modify vertices before they are submitted for drawing. See Starling changes.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md903}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Starling}{Starling}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md903}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed renderer to work with 3.\+6 changes.
\item Added support for two color tinting.
\item Added support for clipping.
\item Added support for rotated regions in texture atlas loaded via Starling\+Atlas\+Attachment\+Loader.
\item Added support for vertex effects. See {\ttfamily Raptor\+Example.\+as}
\item Added \textquotesingle{}get\+Texture()\textquotesingle{} method to \textquotesingle{}Starling\+Texture\+Atlas\+Attachment\+Loader\textquotesingle{}
\item Breaking change\+: if a skeleton requires two color tinting, you have to enable it via {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Sprite.\+two\+Color\+Tint = true}. In this case the skeleton will use the {\ttfamily Two\+Color\+Mesh\+Style}, which internally uses a different vertex layout and shader. This means that skeletons with two color tinting enabled will break batching and hence increase the number of draw calls in your app.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md904}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{C}{C}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md904}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily sp\+Vertex\+Attachment\+\_\+compute\+World\+Vertices} and {\ttfamily sp\+Region\+Attachment\+\_\+compute\+World\+VerticeS} now take new parameters to make it possible to directly output the calculated vertex positions to a vertex buffer. Removes the need for additional copies in the backends\textquotesingle{} respective renderers.
\item Removed {\ttfamily sp\+Bounding\+Box\+Attachment\+\_\+compute\+World\+Vertices}, superseded by {\ttfamily sp\+Vertex\+Attachment\+\_\+compute\+World\+Vertices}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily sp\+Path\+Attachment\+\_\+compute\+World\+Vertices} and {\ttfamily sp\+Path\+Attachment\+\_\+compute\+World\+Vertices1}, superseded by {\ttfamily sp\+Vertex\+Attachment\+\_\+compute\+World\+Vertices}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily sp\+\_\+\+Mesh\+Attachment\+\_\+compute\+World\+Vertices}, superseded by {\ttfamily sp\+Vertex\+Attachment\+\_\+compute\+World\+Vertices}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily sp\+Bone\+\_\+world\+To\+Local\+RotationX} and {\ttfamily sp\+Bone\+\_\+world\+To\+Local\+RotationY}. Replaced by {\ttfamily sp\+Bone\+\_\+world\+To\+Local\+Rotation} (rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item Replaced {\ttfamily r}, {\ttfamily g}, {\ttfamily b}, {\ttfamily a} fields with instances of new {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_color}{sp\+Color}} struct in {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_region_attachment}{sp\+Region\+Attachment}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_mesh_attachment}{sp\+Mesh\+Attachment}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_skeleton}{sp\+Skeleton}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_skeleton_data}{sp\+Skeleton\+Data}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_slot}{sp\+Slot}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_slot_data}{sp\+Slot\+Data}}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily \doxylink{_region_attachment_8c_ae352e1dd593d11fcdad4f4917b117e87}{sp\+Vertex\+Index}}from public API.
\item Listeners on {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_animation_state}{sp\+Animation\+State}} or {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_track_entry}{sp\+Track\+Entry}} will now be also called in case a track entry is disposed as part of dispoing the {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_animation_state}{sp\+Animation\+State}}.
\item The completion event will fire for looped 0 duration animations every frame.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for local and relative transform constraint calculation, including additional fields in {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_transform_constraint_data}{sp\+Transform\+Constraint\+Data}}.
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_point_attachment}{sp\+Point\+Attachment}}, additional method {\ttfamily sp\+Atlas\+Attachment\+Loade\+R\+\_\+new\+Point\+Attachment}.
\item Added support for local and relative transform constraint calculation, including additional fields in {\ttfamily Transform\+Constraint\+Data}
\item Added {\ttfamily sp\+Bone\+\_\+local\+To\+World\+Rotation}(rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item Added two color tinting support, including {\ttfamily sp\+Two\+Color\+Timeline} and additional fields on {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_slot}{sp\+Slot}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_slot_data}{sp\+Slot\+Data}}.
\item Added {\ttfamily user\+Data} field to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_track_entry}{sp\+Track\+Entry}}, so users can expose data in {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_animation_state}{sp\+Animation\+State}} callbacks.
\item Modified kvec.\+h used by \doxylink{_skeleton_binary_8c}{Skeleton\+Binary.\+c} to use \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine}\textquotesingle{}s MALLOC/\+FREE macros. That way there\textquotesingle{}s only one place to inject custom allocators (\href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/blob/master/spine-c/spine-c/include/spine/extension.h}{\texttt{ extension.\+h}}) \href{https://github.com/EsotericSoftware/spine-runtimes/commit/c2cfbc6cb8709daa082726222d558188d75a004f}{\texttt{ commit}}
\item Added macros to define typed dynamic arrays, see {\ttfamily Array.\+h/.c}
\item Added {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_clipping_attachment}{sp\+Clipping\+Attachment}} and respective enum.
\item Added {\ttfamily sp\+Skeleton\+Clipper} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{structsp_triangulator}{sp\+Triangulator}}, used to implement software clipping of attachments.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\+State\#apply} returns boolean indicating if any timeline was applied or not.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\#apply} and {\ttfamily Timeline\#apply}{\ttfamily now take enums}Mix\+Pose{\ttfamily and}Mix\+Direction{\ttfamily instead of booleans}
\item {\ttfamily Added}sp\+Vertex\+Effect{\ttfamily and corresponding implementations}sp\+Jitter\+Vertex\+Effect{\ttfamily and}sp\+Swirl\+Vertex\+Effect{\ttfamily . Create/dispose through the corresponding}sp\+XXXVertex\+Effect\+\_\+create()/dispose(){\ttfamily functions. Set on framework/engine specific renderer. See changes for spine-\/c based frameworks/engines below.}
\item {\ttfamily Functions in}extension.\+h{\ttfamily are not prefixed with}\+\_\+sp{\ttfamily instead of just}\+\_\+{\ttfamily to avoid interference with other libraries.}
\item {\ttfamily Introduced}SP\+\_\+\+API{\ttfamily macro. Every spine-\/c function is prefixed with this macro. By default, it is an empty string. Can be used to markup spine-\/c functions with e.\+g.}{\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+declspec} when compiling to a dll or linking to that dll.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md905}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cocos2d-\/X}{Cocos2d-\/X}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md905}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed renderer to work with 3.\+6 changes
\item Optimized rendering by removing all per-\/frame allocation in {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}, resulting in 15\% performance increase for large numbers of skeletons being rendered per frame.
\item Added support for two color tinting. Tinting is enabled/disabled per {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}/{\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animation} instance. Use {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+::set\+Two\+Color\+Tint()}. Note that two color tinting requires the use of a non-\/standard shader and vertex format. This means that skeletons rendered with two color tinting will break batching. However, skeletons with two color tinting enabled and rendered after each other will be batched.
\item Updated example to use Cocos2d-\/x 3.\+14.\+1.
\item Added mesh debug rendering. Enable/\+Disable via {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+::set\+Debug\+Meshes\+Enabled()}.
\item Added support for clipping.
\item Skeleton\+Renderer now combines the displayed color of the \doxylink{class_node}{Node} (cascaded from all parents) with the skeleton color for tinting.
\item Added support for vertex effects. See {\ttfamily \doxylink{_raptor_example_8cpp}{Raptor\+Example.\+cpp}}.
\item Added ETC1 alpha support, thanks @halx99! Does not work when two color tint is enabled.
\item Added {\ttfamily sp\+Atlas\+Page\+\_\+set\+Custom\+Texture\+Loader()} which let\textquotesingle{}s you do texture loading manually. Thanks @jareguo.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+:set\+Slots\+Range()} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\+::create\+With\+Skeleton()}. This allows you to split rendering of a skeleton up into multiple parts, and render other nodes in between. See {\ttfamily \doxylink{_skeleton_renderer_separator_example_8cpp}{Skeleton\+Renderer\+Separator\+Example.\+cpp}} for an example.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md906}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cocos2d-\/\+Objc}{Cocos2d-\/\+Objc}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md906}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed renderer to work with 3.\+6 changes
\item Added support for two color tinting. Tinting is enabled/disabled per {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer/\+Skeleton\+Animation.\+two\+Color\+Tint = true}. Note that two color tinted skeletons do not batch with other nodes.
\item Added support for clipping.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md907}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SFML}{SFML}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md907}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed renderer to work with 3.\+6 changes. Sadly, two color tinting does not work, as the vertex format in SFML is fixed.
\item Added support for clipping.
\item Added support for vertex effects. See raptor example.
\item Added premultiplied alpha support to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Drawable}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md908}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Unreal Engine 4}{Unreal Engine 4}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md908}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed renderer to work with 3.\+6 changes
\item Added new UPROPERTY to Spine\+Skeleton\+Renderer\+Component called {\ttfamily \doxylink{external_2magic__enum_2example_2example_8cpp_a692f5062ca261bdb3a62a63faddfd27f}{Color}}. This allows to set the tint color of the skeleton in the editor, C++ and Blueprints. Under the hood, the {\ttfamily sp\+Skeleton-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}color} will be set on every tick of the renderer component.
\item Added support for clipping.
\item Switched from built-\/in Procedural\+Mesh\+Component to Runtime\+Mesh\+Component by Koderz (\href{https://github.com/Koderz/UE4RuntimeMeshComponent}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/\+Koderz/\+UE4\+Runtime\+Mesh\+Component}}, MIT). Needed for more flexibility regarding vertex format, should not have an impact on existing code/assets. You need to copy the Runtime\+Mesh\+Component\+Plugin from our repository in {\ttfamily spine-\/ue4\textbackslash{}Plugins\textbackslash{}} to your project as well!
\item Added support for two color tinting. All base materials, e.\+g. Spine\+Unlit\+Normal\+Material, now do proper two color tinting. No material parameters have changed.
\item Updated to Unreal Engine 4.\+16.\+1. Note that 4.\+16 has a regression which will make it impossible to compile plain .c files!
\item spine-\/c is now exposed from the plugin shared library on Windows via \+\_\+\+\_\+declspec.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md909}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{C}{C}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md909}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment.\+parent\+Mesh} is now a private field to enforce using the {\ttfamily .Parent\+Mesh} setter property in external code. The {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment.\+Parent\+Mesh} property is an appropriate replacement wherever {\ttfamily .parent\+Mesh} was used.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+Get\+Bounds} takes a scratch array as input so it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to allocate a new array on each invocation itself. Reduces GC activity.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Bone.\+World\+To\+Local\+RotationX} and {\ttfamily Bone.\+World\+To\+Local\+RotationY}. Replaced by {\ttfamily Bone.\+World\+To\+Local\+Rotation} (rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item Added {\ttfamily stride} parameter to {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+Compute\+World\+Vertices}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+Vertices} field. The vertices array is provided to {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+Compute\+World\+Vertices} by the API user now.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+Update\+World\+Vertices}, added {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+Compute\+World\+Vertices}. The new method now computes the x/y positions of the 4 vertices of the corner and places them in the provided {\ttfamily world\+Vertices} array, starting at {\ttfamily offset}, then moving by {\ttfamily stride} array elements when advancing to the next vertex. This allows to directly compose the vertex buffer and avoids a copy. The computation of the full vertices, including vertex colors and texture coordinates, is now done by the backend\textquotesingle{}s respective renderer.
\item The completion event will fire for looped 0 duration animations every frame.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\item Added support for local and relative transform constraint calculation, including additional fields in {\ttfamily Transform\+Constraint\+Data}
\item Added {\ttfamily Bone.\+local\+To\+World\+Rotation}(rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item Added two color tinting support, including {\ttfamily Two\+Color\+Timeline} and additional fields on {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}} and {\ttfamily Slot\+Data}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Point\+Attachment}, additional method {\ttfamily New\+Point\+Attachment} in {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader} interface.
\item Added {\ttfamily Clipping\+Attachment}, additional method {\ttfamily New\+Clipping\+Attachment} in {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader} interface.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Clipper} and {\ttfamily Triangulator}, used to implement software clipping of attachments.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\+State.\+Apply} returns a bool indicating if any timeline was applied or not.
\item {\ttfamily Animation.\+Apply} and {\ttfamily Timeline.\+Apply}{\ttfamily now take enums}Mix\+Pose{\ttfamily and}Mix\+Direction\`{} instead of bools.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md910}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Unity}{Unity}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md910}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Refactored renderer to work with new 3.\+6 features.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Two color tinting}} is currently supported via extra UV2 and UV3 mesh vertex streams. To use Two color tinting, you need to\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item switch on "{}\+Tint Black"{} under "{}\+Advanced..."{},
\item use the new {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Tint Black} shader, or your own shader that treats the UV2 and UV3 streams similarly.
\item Additionally, for Skeleton\+Graphic, you can use {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton\+Graphic Tint Black} (or the bundled Skeleton\+Graphic\+Tint\+Black material) or your own shader that uses UV2 and UV3 streams similarly. {\bfseries{Additional Shader Channels}} Tex\+Coord1 and Tex\+Coord2 will need to be enabled from the Canvas component\textquotesingle{}s inspector. These correspond to UV2 and UV3.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Clipping}} is now supported. Caution\+: The Skeleton\+Animation switches to slightly slower mesh generation code when clipping so limit your use of {\ttfamily Clipping\+Attachment}s when using on large numbers of skeletons.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Skeleton\+Renderer.\+initial\+Flip}} \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} components such as Skeleton\+Renderer, Skeleton\+Animation, Skeleton\+Animator now has {\ttfamily initial\+FlipX} and {\ttfamily initial\+FlipY} fields which are also visible in the inspector under "{}\+Advanced..."{}. It will allow you to set and preview a starting flip value for your skeleton component. This is applied immediately when the internal skeleton object is instantiated.
\item {\bfseries{\mbox{[}Spine\+Attribute\mbox{]} Improvements}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Icons have been added to Spine\+Attribute\+Drawers}}. This should make your default inspectors easier to understand at a glance.
\item {\bfseries{Added Constraint Attributes}} You can now use {\ttfamily \mbox{[}\doxylink{class_spine_ik_constraint}{Spine\+Ik\+Constraint}\mbox{]}} {\ttfamily \mbox{[}\doxylink{class_spine_transform_constraint}{Spine\+Transform\+Constraint}\mbox{]}} {\ttfamily \mbox{[}\doxylink{class_spine_path_constraint}{Spine\+Path\+Constraint}\mbox{]}}
\item {\bfseries{Spine\+Attribute data\+Field}} parameter can also now detect sibling fields within arrays and serializable structs/classes.
\item {\bfseries{\mbox{[}Spine\+Attribute(include\+None\+:false)\mbox{]}}} Spine\+Attributes now have an {\ttfamily include\+None} optional parameter to specify if you want to include or exclude a none ("{}"{}) value option in the dropdown menu. Default is {\ttfamily include\+None\+:true}.
\item {\bfseries{\mbox{[}\doxylink{class_spine_attachment}{Spine\+Attachment}(skin\+Field\+:"{}my\+Skin"{})\mbox{]}}} The \doxylink{class_spine_attachment}{Spine\+Attachment} attribute now has a skin\+Field optional parameter to limit the dropdown items to attachments in a specific skin instead of the just default skin or all the skins in Skeleton\+Data.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Skeleton\+Debug\+Window}}. Debugging tools have been moved from the Skeleton\+Animation and Skeleton\+Utility component inspectors into its own utility window. You can access "{}\+Skeleton Debug"{} under the {\ttfamily Advanced...} foldout in the Skeleton\+Animation inspector, or in Skeleton\+Animation\textquotesingle{}s right-\/click/context menu.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Skeleton Baking Window}} The old Skeleton Baking feature is also now accessible through the Skeleton\+Data\+Asset\textquotesingle{}s right-\/click/context menu.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Attachment\+Tools source material}}. {\ttfamily Attachment\+Tools} methods can now accept a {\ttfamily source\+Material} argument to copy material properties from.
\item {\bfseries{Attachment\+Tools Skin Extensions}}. Using Attachment\+Tools, you can now add entries by slot name by also providing a skeleton argument. Also {\ttfamily Append(\+Skin)}, {\ttfamily Remove\+Attachment} and {\ttfamily Clear} have been added.
\item {\bfseries{Bone\+Follower and Skeleton\+Utility\+Bone Add Rigid\+Body Button}}. The Bone\+Follower and Skeleton\+Utility\+Bone component inspectors will now offer to add a {\ttfamily Rigidbody} or {\ttfamily Rigidbody2D} if it detects a collider of the appropriate type. Having a rigidbody on a moving transform with a collider fits better with the Unity physics systems and prevents excess calculations. It will not detect colliders on child objects so you have to add Rigidbody components manually accordingly.
\item {\bfseries{Skeleton\+Renderer.\+On\+Post\+Process\+Vertices}} is a new callback that gives you a reference to the Mesh\+Generator after it has generated a mesh from the current skeleton pose. You can access {\ttfamily mesh\+Generator.\+Vertex\+Buffer} or {\ttfamily mesh\+Generator.\+Color\+Buffer} to modify these before they get pushed into the Unity\+Engine.\+Mesh for rendering. This can be useful for non-\/shader vertex effects.
\item {\bfseries{Examples}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Examples now use properties}}. The code in the example scripts have been switched over to using properties instead of fields to encourage their use for consistency. This is in anticipation of both users who want to move the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} folders to the Unity Plugins folder (compiled as a different assembly), and of Unity 2017\textquotesingle{}s ability to manually define different assemblies for shorter compilation times.
\item {\bfseries{Mix And Match}}. The mix-\/and-\/match example scene, code and data have been updated to reflect the current recommended setup for animation-\/compatible custom equip systems The underlying API has changed since 3.\+5 and the new API calls in Mix\+And\+Match.\+cs is recommended. Documentation is in progress.
\item {\bfseries{Sample Components}}. {\ttfamily Atas\+Region\+Attacher} and {\ttfamily Sprite\+Attacher} are now part of {\ttfamily Sample Components}, to reflect that they are meant to be used as sample code rather than production. \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} few other sample components have also been added. New imports of the unitypackage Examples folder will see a "{}\+Legacy"{} folder comprised of old sample components that no longer contain the most up-\/to-\/date and recommended workflows, but are kept in case old setups used them for production.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{\doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} folder}}. In the unitypackage, the "{}spine-\/csharp"{} and "{}spine-\/unity"{} folders are now inside a "{}\+Spine"{} folder. This change will only affect fresh imports. Importing the unitypackage to update Spine-\/\+Unity in your existing project will update the appropriate files however you chose to arrange them, as long as the meta files are intact.
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The Sprite shaders module was updated to the latest version from the \href{https://github.com/traggett/UnitySpriteShaders/commits/master}{\texttt{ source}}. Some changes were made to the underlying keyword structure. You may need to review the settings of your lit materials. Particularly, your Fixed Normals settings.
\item The {\ttfamily Spine/\+Skeleton Lit} shader was switched over to non-\/fixed-\/function code. It now no longer requires mesh normals and has fixed normals at the shader level.
\item The old Mesh\+Generator classes, interfaces and code in {\ttfamily Spine.\+Unity.\+Mesh\+Generation} are now deprecated. All mesh-\/generating components now share the class {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_mesh_generator}{Spine.\+Unity.\+Mesh\+Generator}} defined in {\ttfamily \doxylink{_spine_mesh_8cs}{Spine\+Mesh.\+cs}}. Mesh\+Generator is a serializable class.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer.\+render\+Meshes} optimization is currently non-\/functional.
\item Old triangle-\/winding code has been removed from {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}. Please use shaders that have backface culling off.
\item Render settings in {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic} can now be accessed under {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Graphic.\+Mesh\+Generator.\+settings}. This is visible in the Skeleton\+Graphic inspector as {\ttfamily Advanced...}
\item We will continue to bundle the unitypackage with the empty .cs files of deprecated classes until \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} 3.\+7 to ensure the upgrade process does not break.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item The \mbox{[}\doxylink{class_spine_attachment}{Spine\+Attachment(slot\+Field\+:)}\mbox{]} optional parameter found property value now acts as a \doxylink{struct_find}{Find(slot\+Name)} argument rather than Contains(slot\+Name).
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animator} now uses a {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animator.\+Mecanim\+Translator} class to translate an Animator\textquotesingle{}s Mecanim \doxylink{struct_state}{State} Machine into skeleton poses. This makes code reuse possible for a Mecanim version of Skeleton\+Graphic.
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Animator} {\ttfamily autoreset} and the {\ttfamily mix\+Modes} array are now a part of Skeleton\+Animator\textquotesingle{}s Mecanim\+Translator {\ttfamily .Translator}. {\ttfamily auto\+Reset} is set to {\ttfamily true} by default. Old prefabs and scene objects with Skeleton Animator may no longer have correct values set.
\item Warnings and conditionals checking for specific Unity 5.\+2-\/and-\/below incompatibility have been removed.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md911}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{XNA/\+Mono\+Game}{XNA/\+Mono\+Game}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md911}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for clipping
\item Removed {\ttfamily Region\+Batcher} and {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Region\+Renderer}, renamed {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mesh\+Renderer} to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}
\item Added support for two color tint. For it to work, you need to add the {\ttfamily Spine\+Effect.\+fx} file to your content project, then load it via {\ttfamily var effect = Content.\+Load\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Effect\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}("{}\+Spine\+Effect"{});}, and set it on the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}. See the example project for code.
\item Added support for any {\ttfamily Effect} to be used by {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}
\item Added support for {\ttfamily IVertex\+Effect} to modify vertices of skeletons on the CPU. {\ttfamily IVertex\+Effect} instances can be set on the {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}. See example project.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Debug\+Renderer}
\item Made {\ttfamily Mesh\+Batcher} of Skeleton\+Renderer accessible via a getter. Allows user to batch their own geometry together with skeleton meshes for maximum batching instead of using XNA Sprite\+Batcher.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md912}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Java}{Java}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md912}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+get\+Bounds} takes a scratch array as input so it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to allocate a new array on each invocation itself. Reduces GC activity.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Bone.\+world\+To\+Local\+RotationX} and {\ttfamily Bone.\+world\+To\+Local\+RotationY}. Replaced by {\ttfamily Bone.\+world\+To\+Local\+Rotation} (rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item Added {\ttfamily stride} parameter to {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+vertices} field. The vertices array is provided to {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices} by the API user now.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+update\+World\+Vertices}, added {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices}. The new method now computes the x/y positions of the 4 vertices of the corner and places them in the provided {\ttfamily world\+Vertices} array, starting at {\ttfamily offset}, then moving by {\ttfamily stride} array elements when advancing to the next vertex. This allows to directly compose the vertex buffer and avoids a copy. The computation of the full vertices, including vertex colors and texture coordinates, is now done by the backend\textquotesingle{}s respective renderer.
\item Skeleton attachments\+: Moved update of attached skeleton out of lib\+GDX {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}, added overloaded method {\ttfamily Skeleton\#update\+World\+Transform(\+Bone), used for}Skeleton\+Attachment{\ttfamily . You now MUST call this new method with the bone of the parent skeleton to which the child skeleton is attached. See}Skeleton\+Attachment\+Test\`{} for and example.
\item The completion event will fire for looped 0 duration animations every frame.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for local and relative transform constraint calculation, including additional fields in {\ttfamily Transform\+Constraint\+Data}
\item Added {\ttfamily Bone.\+local\+To\+World\+Rotation}(rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item Added two color tinting support, including {\ttfamily Two\+Color\+Timeline} and additional fields on {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}} and {\ttfamily Slot\+Data}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Point\+Attachment}, additional method {\ttfamily new\+Point\+Attachment} in {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader} interface.
\item Added {\ttfamily Clipping\+Attachment}, additional method {\ttfamily new\+Clipping\+Attachment} in {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader} interface.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Clipper} and {\ttfamily Triangulator}, used to implement software clipping of attachments.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\+State\#apply} returns boolean indicating if any timeline was applied or not.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\#apply} and {\ttfamily Timeline\#apply}{\ttfamily now take enums}Mix\+Pose{\ttfamily and}Mix\+Direction\`{} instead of booleans
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md913}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lib\+GDX}{lib\+GDX}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md913}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed renderer to work with 3.\+6 changes
\item Added support for two color tinting. Use the new {\ttfamily Two\+Color\+Polygon\+Batch} together with {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}
\item Added support for clipping. See {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Clipper}. Used automatically by {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}. Does not work when using a {\ttfamily Sprite\+Batch} with {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}. Use {\ttfamily Polygon\+Sprite\+Batch} or {\ttfamily Two\+Color\+Polygon\+Batch} instead.
\item Added {\ttfamily Vertex\+Effect} interface, instances of which can be set on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}. Allows to modify vertices before submitting them to GPU. See {\ttfamily Swirl\+Effect}, {\ttfamily Jitter\+Effect} and {\ttfamily Vertex\+Effect\+Test}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md914}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Lua}{Lua}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md914}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Removed {\ttfamily Bone\+:world\+To\+Local\+RotationX} and {\ttfamily Bone\+:world\+To\+Local\+RotationY}. Replaced by {\ttfamily Bone\+:world\+To\+Local\+Rotation} (rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment\+:compute\+World\+Vertices} now takes offsets and stride to allow compositing vertices directly in a vertex buffer to be send to the GPU. The compositing is now performed in the backends\textquotesingle{} respective renderers. This also affects the subclasses {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment}, {\ttfamily Bounding\+Box\+Attachment} and {\ttfamily Path\+Attachment}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment\+:update\+World\+Vertices}, added {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment\+:compute\+World\+Vertices}, which takes offsets and stride to allow compositing vertices directly in a vertex buffer to be send to the GPU. The compositing is now performed in the backends\textquotesingle{} respective renderers.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment.\+world\+Vertices} field. Computation is now performed in each backends\textquotesingle{} respective renderer. The {\ttfamily uv} coordinates are now stored in {\ttfamily Mesh\+Attachment.\+uvs}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+vertices} field. Computation is now performed in each backends respective renderer. The {\ttfamily uv} coordinates for each vertex are now stored in the {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+uvs} field.
\item The completion event will fire for looped 0 duration animations every frame.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Bone\+:local\+To\+World\+Rotation}(rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item Added two color tinting support, including {\ttfamily Two\+Color\+Timeline} and additional fields on {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}} and {\ttfamily Slot\+Data}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Point\+Attachment}, additional method {\ttfamily new\+Point\+Attachment} in {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader} interface.
\item Added support for local and relative transform constraint calculation, including additional fields in {\ttfamily Transform\+Constraint\+Data}
\item Added {\ttfamily Clipping\+Attachment}, additional method {\ttfamily new\+Clipping\+Attachment} in {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader} interface.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Clipper} and {\ttfamily Triangulator}, used to implement software clipping of attachments.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\+State\#apply} returns boolean indicating if any timeline was applied or not.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\#apply} and {\ttfamily Timeline\#apply}{\ttfamily now take enums}Mix\+Pose{\ttfamily and}Mix\+Direction{\ttfamily instead of booleans}
\item {\ttfamily Added}Jitter\+Effect{\ttfamily and}Swirl\+Effect\`{} and support for vertex effects in Corona and Love
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md915}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Love2D}{Love2D}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md915}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed renderer to work with 3.\+6 changes
\item Added support for two color tinting. Enable it via {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer.\+new(true)}.
\item Added clipping support.
\item Added support for vertex effects. Set an implementation like "{}\+Jitter\+Effect"{} on {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+vertex\+Effect}. See {\ttfamily main.\+lua} for an example.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md916}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Corona}{Corona}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md916}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed renderer to work with 3.\+6 changes. Sadly, two color tinting is not supported, as Corona doesn\textquotesingle{}t let us change the vertex format needed and its doesn\textquotesingle{}t allow to modify shaders in the way needed for two color tinting
\item Added clipping support.
\item Added support for vertex effects. Set an implementation like "{}\+Jitter\+Effect"{} on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer.\+vertex\+Effect}. See {\ttfamily main.\+lua} for an example
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md917}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Typescript/\+Javascript}{Typescript/\+Javascript}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md917}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Breaking changes}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Skeleton.\+get\+Bounds} takes a scratch array as input so it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to allocate a new array on each invocation itself. Reduces GC activity.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Bone.\+world\+To\+Local\+RotationX} and {\ttfamily Bone.\+world\+To\+Local\+RotationY}. Replaced by {\ttfamily Bone.\+world\+To\+Local\+Rotation} (rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item Removed {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices} overload, changed {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices\+With} to {\ttfamily Vertex\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices}, added {\ttfamily stride} parameter.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+vertices} field. The vertices array is provided to {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices} by the API user now.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+update\+World\+Vertices}, added {\ttfamily Region\+Attachment.\+compute\+World\+Vertices}. The new method now computes the x/y positions of the 4 vertices of the corner and places them in the provided {\ttfamily world\+Vertices} array, starting at {\ttfamily offset}, then moving by {\ttfamily stride} array elements when advancing to the next vertex. This allows to directly compose the vertex buffer and avoids a copy. The computation of the full vertices, including vertex colors and texture coordinates, is now done by the backend\textquotesingle{}s respective renderer.
\item The completion event will fire for looped 0 duration animations every frame.
\item Removed the \doxylink{namespace_spine}{Spine} Widget in favor of \href{https://esotericsoftware.com/spine-player}{\texttt{ Spine Web Player}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Additions}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added support for local and relative transform constraint calculation, including additional fields in {\ttfamily Transform\+Constraint\+Data}
\item Added {\ttfamily Bone.\+local\+To\+World\+Rotation}(rotation given relative to x-\/axis, counter-\/clockwise, in degrees).
\item Added two color tinting support, including {\ttfamily Two\+Color\+Timeline} and additional fields on {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_slot}{Slot}} and {\ttfamily Slot\+Data}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Point\+Attachment}, additional method {\ttfamily new\+Point\+Attachment} in {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader} interface.
\item Added {\ttfamily Clipping\+Attachment}, additional method {\ttfamily new\+Clipping\+Attachment} in {\ttfamily Attachment\+Loader} interface.
\item Added {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Clipper} and {\ttfamily Triangulator}, used to implement software clipping of attachments.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\+State\#apply} returns boolean indicating if any timeline was applied or not.
\item {\ttfamily Animation\#apply} and {\ttfamily Timeline\#apply}{\ttfamily now take enums}Mix\+Pose{\ttfamily and}Mix\+Direction{\ttfamily instead of booleans}
\item {\ttfamily Added}Asset\+Manager.\+load\+Texture\+Atlas{\ttfamily . Instead of loading the}.atlas{\ttfamily and corresponding image files manually, you can simply specify the location of the}.atlas{\ttfamily file and Asset\+Manager will load the atlas and all its images automatically.}Asset\+Manager.\+get("{}atlasname.\+atlas"{}){\ttfamily will then return an instance of}spine.\+Texture\+Atlas\`{}.
\item Added the \href{https://esotericsoftware.com/spine-player}{\texttt{ Spine Web Player}}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md918}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Web\+GL backend}{Web\+GL backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md918}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed Web\+GL context loss
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Restorable} interface, implemented by any Web\+GL resource that needs restoration after a context loss. All Web\+GL resource classes ({\ttfamily Shader}, {\ttfamily Mesh}, {\ttfamily GLTexture}) implement this interface.
\item Added {\ttfamily Managed\+Web\+GLRendering\+Context}. Handles setup of a {\ttfamily Web\+GLRendering\+Context} given a canvas element and restoration of Web\+GL resources ({\ttfamily Shader}, {\ttfamily Mesh}, {\ttfamily GLTexture}) on Web\+GL context loss. Web\+GL resources register themselves with the {\ttfamily Managed\+Web\+GLRendering\+Context}. If the context is informed of a context loss and restoration, the registered Web\+GL resources\textquotesingle{} {\ttfamily restore()} method is called. The {\ttfamily restore()} method implementation on each resource type will recreate the GPU side objects.
\item All classes that previously took a {\ttfamily Web\+GLRendering\+Context} in the constructor now also allow a {\ttfamily Managed\+Web\+GLRendering\+Context}. This ensures existing applications do not break.
\item To use automatic context restauration\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Create or fetch a canvas element from the DOM
\item Instantiate a {\ttfamily Managed\+Web\+GLRendering\+Context}, passing the canvas to the constructor. This will setup a {\ttfamily Web\+GLRendering\+Context} internally and manage context loss/restoration.
\item Pass the {\ttfamily Managed\+Web\+GLRendering\+Context} to the constructors of classes that you previously passed a {\ttfamily Web\+GLRendering\+Context} to ({\ttfamily Asset\+Manager}, {\ttfamily GLTexture}, {\ttfamily Mesh}, {\ttfamily Shader}, {\ttfamily Polygon\+Batcher}, {\ttfamily Scene\+Renderer}, {\ttfamily Shape\+Renderer}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Debug\+Renderer}).
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Fixed renderer to work with 3.\+6 changes.
\item Added support for two color tinting.
\item Improved performance by using {\ttfamily DYNAMIC\+\_\+\+DRAW} for vertex buffer objects and fixing bug that copied to much data to the GPU each frame in {\ttfamily Polygon\+Batcher}/{\ttfamily Mesh}.
\item Added two color tinting support, enabled by default. You can disable it via the constructors of {\ttfamily Scene\+Renderer}, {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}and {\ttfamily Polygon\+Batcher}. Note that you will need to use a shader created via {\ttfamily Shader.\+new\+Two\+Colored\+Textured\+Shader} shader with {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer} and {\ttfamily Polygon\+Batcher} if two color tinting is enabled.
\item Added clipping support
\item Added {\ttfamily Vertex\+Effect} interface, instances of which can be set on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer}. Allows to modify vertices before submitting them to GPU. See {\ttfamily Swirl\+Effect}, {\ttfamily Jitter\+Effect}, and the example which allows to set effects.
\item Added {\ttfamily slot\+Range\+Start} and {\ttfamily slot\+Range\+End} parameters to {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Renderer\#draw} and {\ttfamily Scene\+Renderer\#draw\+Skeleton}. This allows you to render only a range of slots in the draw order. See {\ttfamily spine-\/ts/webgl/tests/test-\/slot-\/range.\+html} for an example.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md919}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Canvas backend}{Canvas backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md919}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed renderer to work for 3.\+6 changes. Sadly, we can\textquotesingle{}t support two color tinting via the Canvas API.
\item Added support for shearing and non-\/uniform scaling inherited from parent bones.
\item Added support for alpha tinting.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md920}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Three.\+js backend}{Three.\+js backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md920}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed renderer to work with 3.\+6 changes. Two color tinting is not supported.
\item Added clipping support
\item Added {\ttfamily Vertex\+Effect} interface, instances of which can be set on {\ttfamily Skeleton\+Mesh}. Allows to modify vertices before submitting them to GPU. See {\ttfamily Swirl\+Effect}, {\ttfamily Jitter\+Effect}.
\item Added support for multi-\/page atlases
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md921}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Widget backend}{Widget backend}}\label{md_external_2spine-runtimes_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md921}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed Web\+GL context loss (see Web\+GL backend changes). Enabled automatically.
\item Fixed renderer to work for 3.\+6 changes. Supports two color tinting \& clipping (see Web\+GL backend changes for details).
\item Added fields {\ttfamily atlas\+Content}, {\ttfamily atlas\+Pages\+Content}, and {\ttfamily json\+Content} to {\ttfamily Widget\+Configuration} allowing you to directly pass the contents of the {\ttfamily .atlas}, atlas page {\ttfamily .png} files, and the {\ttfamily .json} file without having to do a request. See {\ttfamily README.\+md} and the example for details.
\item {\ttfamily Spine\+Widget.\+set\+Animation()} now takes an additional optional parameter for callbacks when animations are completed/interrupted/etc. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
